1 Data Pre-Processing and Unweighted Analyses

This code pulls in the master database (a STATA file) and does some initial cleaning - this will only need to be run once, and then the data
can be accessed in the usual way.

# setup-packages chunk is the authoritative loader.
stopifnot(
  requireNamespace("kableExtra", quietly = TRUE),
  requireNamespace("gtsummary", quietly = TRUE),
  requireNamespace("purrr", quietly = TRUE)
)

# globally tighten gtsummary/gt tables (smaller font + tighter padding)
gtsummary::theme_gtsummary_compact()

project_root <- here::here()
knitr::opts_knit$set(root.dir = project_root)

# keep figures anchored in PDF to reduce heading-only/blank pages
if (knitr::is_latex_output()) {
  knitr::opts_chunk$set(fig.pos = "H")
}

# helper: scale generic data.frames for PDF output



                                                                          3
kable_pdf <- function(df, caption = NULL, font_size = 7) {
  kbl <- knitr::kable(df, format = "latex", booktabs = TRUE, caption = caption)
  kbl <- kableExtra::kable_styling(
    kbl,
    latex_options = c("hold_position", "scale_down"),
    font_size     = font_size,
    full_width    = TRUE,
    position      = "center"
  )
  mark_float_emitted()
  kbl
}

# helper: resolve a notebook display path relative to the repo root so the
# canonical render path never depends on the notebook subdirectory.
display_path <- function(path, must_exist = TRUE) {
  vapply(path, function(one_path) {
    path_abs <- tryCatch(
      fs::path_abs(one_path, start = project_root),
      error = function(e) NA_character_
    )
    if (is.na(path_abs)) {
      stop("Could not resolve display path: ", one_path)
    }
    if (must_exist && !file.exists(path_abs)) {
      stop("Missing display artifact: ", path_abs)
    }
    if (!(fs::path_has_parent(path_abs, project_root) || identical(path_abs, project_root))) {
      stop("Display path escapes project root: ", path_abs)
    }
    fs::path_rel(path_abs, start = project_root)
  }, character(1), USE.NAMES = FALSE)
}

# helper: pretty, relative paths for PDF output
pretty_path <- function(p) {




                                                          4
    vapply(p, function(one_path) {
      out <- tryCatch(display_path(one_path, must_exist = FALSE)[[1]], error = function(e) NA_character_)
      if (is.na(out) || out == "." || grepl("^\\.\\.", out)) {
        return(basename(one_path))
      }
      out
    }, character(1), USE.NAMES = FALSE)
}

# helper: emit inline notebook graphics through one canonical path. For PDF
# renders we cap the height explicitly so headings plus image can fit on the
# page without triggering TeX pagination loops.
render_inline_graphic <- function(file,
                                  width = "0.94\\linewidth",
                                  height = "0.72\\textheight") {
  inline_path <- display_path(file)
  if (knitr::is_latex_output()) {
    out <- c(
      "\\begin{center}",
      sprintf(
        "\\includegraphics[width=%s,height=%s,keepaspectratio]{%s}",
        width, height, inline_path
      ),
      "\\end{center}"
    )
    return(knitr::asis_output(paste(out, collapse = "\n")))
  }
  knitr::include_graphics(inline_path)
}

# Canonical PDF path: export all figure/table artifacts, keep executed source
# visible, and reserve rendered output for manuscript-facing displays plus
# compact provenance/status summaries. QA/debug figures remain sidecar artifacts.
VALIDATION_INLINE_ANALYSIS_PREVIEWS <- FALSE

# helper: normalize manuscript-facing text to a plain-ASCII representation so




                                                            5
# PDF labels/captions do not depend on platform-specific glyph handling.
safe_manuscript_text <- function(x) {
  if (is.null(x) || !length(x)) return(x)
  x <- as.character(x)
  replacements <- c(
    "\u00a0" = " ",
    "\u2010" = "-",
    "\u2011" = "-",
    "\u2012" = "-",
    "\u2013" = "-",
    "\u2014" = "-",
    "\u2212" = "-",
    "\u2026" = "...",
    "\u03bc" = "u",
    "\u00b5" = "u",
    "\u2264" = "<=",
    "\u2265" = ">=",
    "\u0394" = "Delta",
    "\u03b4" = "delta",
    "\u03b2" = "beta",
    "\u2082" = "2",
    "\u00b2" = "^2",
    "\u00b3" = "^3",
    "\u2080" = "0",
    "\u2081" = "1",
    "\u2083" = "3",
    "\u2084" = "4",
    "\u2085" = "5",
    "\u2086" = "6",
    "\u2087" = "7",
    "\u2088" = "8",
    "\u2089" = "9"
  )
  for (i in seq_along(replacements)) {
    x <- gsub(names(replacements)[i], replacements[[i]], x, fixed = TRUE)
  }




                                                          6
    x <- iconv(x, from = "", to = "ASCII//TRANSLIT", sub = "?")
    x <- gsub("\\s+", " ", x)
    trimws(x)
}

# helper: flag non-ASCII manuscript labels early so validation renders fail
# before the final PDF silently substitutes or drops glyphs.
is_ascii_text <- function(x) {
  if (is.null(x) || !length(x)) return(logical(0))
  !grepl("[^ -~]", x)
}

# helper: derive one stable manuscript caption from the centralized registry.
manuscript_caption <- function(label, title) {
  label <- safe_manuscript_text(label)
  title <- safe_manuscript_text(title)
  stopifnot(length(label) == length(title))
  ifelse(!nzchar(title), label, paste0(label, ". ", title))
}

# helper: collapse component-level validation states into one build status.
collapse_validation_status <- function(status_values) {
  status_values <- unique(status_values[!is.na(status_values) & nzchar(status_values)])
  if ("FAIL" %in% status_values) return("FAIL")
  if ("PASS_WITH_WARNINGS" %in% status_values) return("PASS_WITH_WARNINGS")
  "PASS"
}

# helper: strip manual "Table X." prefixes in PDF to avoid double numbering
strip_manual_table_number <- function(caption) {
  if (is.null(caption)) return(caption)
  if (!knitr::is_latex_output()) return(caption)
  cap <- gsub("^\\s*(\\*\\*)?Table\\s+[0-9A-Za-z]+\\.?\\s*:?\\s*", "", caption)
  cap
}




                                                            7
# helper: escape LaTeX special chars in plain captions
escape_latex_text <- function(x) {
  if (is.null(x)) return(x)
  if (!knitr::is_latex_output()) return(x)
  gsub("([\\\\%$&#{}_\\^~])", "\\\\\\1", x, perl = TRUE)
}

# helper: strip markdown/LaTeX numbering and formatting so captions can be
# safely reused in both inline Quarto output and standalone PDF exports.
plain_caption_text <- function(caption) {
  if (is.null(caption) || !nzchar(caption)) return("")
  cap <- strip_manual_table_number(caption)
  cap <- gsub("\\*\\*", "", cap)
  cap <- gsub("\\s+", " ", cap)
  trimws(cap)
}

# helper: replace CO2 labels with LaTeX-safe subscripts in table text so PDF
# tables render predictably even when the visible code uses plain ASCII labels.
latex_safe_table_text <- function(x) {
  if (!knitr::is_latex_output() || is.null(x) || !length(x)) return(x)
  out <- x
  out <- gsub("PaCO�", "PaCO\\\\textsubscript{2}", out, fixed = TRUE)
  out <- gsub("PvCO�", "PvCO\\\\textsubscript{2}", out, fixed = TRUE)
  out <- gsub("PaCO2", "PaCO\\\\textsubscript{2}", out, fixed = TRUE)
  out <- gsub("PvCO2", "PvCO\\\\textsubscript{2}", out, fixed = TRUE)
  out
}

# helper: build one plain-text heading string for manually managed table
# displays, where the notebook wants explicit manuscript labels.
table_heading_block <- function(title = NULL, display_label = NULL) {
  title <- plain_caption_text(title)
  label <- if (is.null(display_label) || !nzchar(display_label)) "" else trimws(as.character(display_label))
  heading <- trimws(paste(if (nzchar(label)) paste0(label, ".") else "", title))
  if (!nzchar(heading)) return("")




                                                           8
    if (!knitr::is_latex_output()) return(paste0("**", heading, "**\n\n"))
    heading <- latex_safe_table_text(escape_latex_text(heading))
    paste0("\\begin{center}\\textbf{", heading, "}\\end{center}")
}

# helper: emit a table heading plus one or more LaTeX/Markdown table blocks,
# keeping page-break and landscape behavior explicit in one place.
render_table_blocks <- function(table_blocks, title = NULL, display_label = NULL,
                                 landscape = FALSE, page_break_before = FALSE) {
  heading <- table_heading_block(title = title, display_label = display_label)
  out <- c(if (nzchar(heading)) heading else character(0), table_blocks)
  if (knitr::is_latex_output() && isTRUE(landscape)) {
    out <- c("\\begin{landscape}", out, "\\end{landscape}")
  }
  if (knitr::is_latex_output() && isTRUE(page_break_before)) {
    out <- c("\\clearpage", out)
  }
  mark_float_emitted()
  knitr::asis_output(paste(out, collapse = "\n\n"))
}

# helper: mark points where a visible table/figure has been emitted; this is a
# semantic hook more than a data object, but it keeps display code readable.
mark_float_emitted <- function() {
  invisible(TRUE)
}
# helper: flush accumulated LaTeX floats at important manuscript boundaries so
# tables and figures stay near the code that generated them.
float_barrier <- function(mode = c("soft", "section", "hard", "flush")) {
  if (!knitr::is_latex_output()) return(invisible(NULL))
  mode <- match.arg(mode)
  cmd <- switch(
    mode,
    soft = "\\FloatBarrier\\nopagebreak",
    section = "\\FloatBarrier\\nopagebreak\\par\\noindent",
    hard = "\\FloatBarrier\\clearpage",




                                                            9
      flush = "\\FloatBarrier\\pagebreak"
    )
    knitr::asis_output(cmd)
}

# helper: render full tables for PDF (no previews)
render_table_pdf <- function(df, caption, file_stub,
                             wide = FALSE,
                             digits = 2,
                             max_cols = 6,
                             landscape = NULL,
                             display_label = NULL,
                             caption_mode = c("plain", "numbered", "none"),
                             page_break_before = FALSE) {
  stopifnot(is.data.frame(df))
  caption_mode <- match.arg(caption_mode)
  out_csv <- results_path(paste0(file_stub, ".csv"))
  write_csv_safely(df, out_csv, row_names = FALSE)

    if (is.null(landscape)) landscape <- (wide || ncol(df) > max_cols)
    use_longtable <- nrow(df) > 40
    n_cols <- ncol(df)
    parts <- if (n_cols <= max_cols) list(df) else {
      idx <- split(seq_len(n_cols), ceiling(seq_len(n_cols) / max_cols))
      lapply(idx, function(ii) df[, ii, drop = FALSE])
    }

    build_kbl <- function(df_part, cap) {
      cap <- plain_caption_text(cap)
      cap_numbered <- if (identical(caption_mode, "numbered")) {
        escape_latex_text(latex_safe_table_text(cap))
      } else {
        NULL
      }
      kbl <- knitr::kable(
        df_part,




                                                            10
          format    = "latex",
          booktabs = TRUE,
          longtable = use_longtable,
          caption   = cap_numbered,
          digits    = digits
        )
        kbl <- kableExtra::kable_styling(
          kbl,
          latex_options = if (use_longtable) c("repeat_header") else c("hold_position", "scale_down"),
          font_size     = if (ncol(df_part) > max_cols || wide) 6 else 7,
          full_width    = FALSE,
          position      = "center"
        )
        latex_safe_table_text(as.character(kbl))
    }

    letters_part <- LETTERS[seq_along(parts)]
    out <- unlist(lapply(seq_along(parts), function(i) {
      cap_i <- if (length(parts) == 1L) caption else paste0(caption, " (Part ", letters_part[i], ")")
      build_kbl(parts[[i]], cap_i)
    }))
    if (identical(caption_mode, "numbered")) {
      mark_float_emitted()
      return(knitr::asis_output(paste(out, collapse = "\n\n")))
    }
    title_i <- if (identical(caption_mode, "none")) NULL else caption
    render_table_blocks(
      out,
      title = title_i,
      display_label = display_label,
      landscape = landscape,
      page_break_before = page_break_before
    )
}

# helper: conditionally show a rendered table in the notebook while still




                                                              11
# always exporting the CSV/PDF artifact needed downstream.
render_table_pdf_maybe <- function(df, caption, file_stub,
                                   wide = FALSE,
                                   digits = 2,
                                   max_cols = 6,
                                   landscape = NULL,
                                   show = TRUE,
                                   display_label = NULL,
                                   caption_mode = c("plain", "numbered", "none")) {
  caption_mode <- match.arg(caption_mode)
  if (!isTRUE(show)) {
    write_csv_safely(df, results_path(paste0(file_stub, ".csv")), row_names = FALSE)
    return(invisible(NULL))
  }
  tbl <- render_table_pdf(
    df,
    caption = caption,
    file_stub = file_stub,
    wide = wide,
    digits = digits,
    max_cols = max_cols,
    landscape = landscape,
    display_label = display_label,
    caption_mode = caption_mode
  )
  if (isTRUE(show)) {
    return(tbl)
  }
  invisible(NULL)
}

    df_part,

    longtable = FALSE,

    kbl,
    latex_options = c("hold_position", "scale_down"),

          paste0("\\medskip\\noindent\\textbf{", escape_latex_text(latex_safe_table_text(panel_title)), "}\\par"),

# helper: render a standalone table PDF that can be cited outside the notebook.
# This path is used for manuscript/supplement table artifacts with stable names.
resolve_latex_command <- function(cmd = "pdflatex") {
  cmd_path <- Sys.which(cmd)
  if (nzchar(cmd_path)) return(cmd_path)

    fallback <- fs::path(path.expand("~"), "Library", "TinyTeX", "bin", "universal-darwin", cmd)
    if (file.exists(fallback)) {
      tex_dir <- fs::path_dir(fallback)
      current_path <- Sys.getenv("PATH", unset = "")
      path_parts <- strsplit(current_path, .Platform$path.sep, fixed = TRUE)[[1]]
      if (!tex_dir %in% path_parts) {
        Sys.setenv(PATH = paste(c(tex_dir, current_path), collapse = .Platform$path.sep))




                                                            14
        }
        return(fallback)
    }

    stop(
      "Required LaTeX command not found on PATH: ", cmd,
      ". Install TinyTeX or expose the TeX bin directory before rendering."
    )
}

write_standalone_table_pdf <- function(df, caption, file_stub,
                                       wide = FALSE,
                                       digits = 2,
                                       max_cols = 6,
                                       landscape = NULL,
                                       display_label = NULL) {
  stopifnot(is.data.frame(df))
  out_csv <- results_path(paste0(file_stub, ".csv"))
  write_csv_safely(df, out_csv, row_names = FALSE)

    if (is.null(landscape)) landscape <- (wide || ncol(df) > max_cols)
    use_longtable <- nrow(df) > 40
    n_cols <- ncol(df)
    parts <- if (n_cols <= max_cols) list(df) else {
      idx <- split(seq_len(n_cols), ceiling(seq_len(n_cols) / max_cols))
      lapply(idx, function(ii) df[, ii, drop = FALSE])
    }

    build_kbl <- function(df_part) {
      kbl <- knitr::kable(
        df_part,
        format = "latex",
        booktabs = TRUE,
        longtable = use_longtable,
        caption = NULL,
        digits = digits




                                                            15
    )
    kbl <- kableExtra::kable_styling(
      kbl,
      latex_options = if (use_longtable) c("repeat_header") else c("hold_position", "scale_down"),
      font_size = if (ncol(df_part) > max_cols || wide) 6 else 7,
      full_width = FALSE,
      position = "center"
    )
    latex_safe_table_text(as.character(kbl))
}

letters_part <- LETTERS[seq_along(parts)]
table_blocks <- unlist(lapply(seq_along(parts), function(i) {
  cap_i <- if (length(parts) == 1L) caption else paste0(caption, " (Part ", letters_part[i], ")")
  c(
    table_heading_block(cap_i, display_label = display_label),
    build_kbl(parts[[i]])
  )
}))
if (isTRUE(landscape)) {
  table_blocks <- c("\\begin{landscape}", table_blocks, "\\end{landscape}")
}

tex_doc <- c(
  "\\documentclass{article}",
  "\\usepackage[margin=0.75in]{geometry}",
  "\\usepackage{booktabs}",
  "\\usepackage{longtable}",
  "\\usepackage{pdflscape}",
  "\\usepackage{float}",
  "\\usepackage{graphicx}",
  "\\begin{document}",
  table_blocks,
  "\\end{document}"
)




                                                          16
    build_dir <- fs::path(tempdir(), paste0("table_pdf_", file_stub))
    fs::dir_create(build_dir, recurse = TRUE)
    tex_file <- fs::path(build_dir, paste0(file_stub, ".tex"))
    writeLines(tex_doc, tex_file, useBytes = TRUE)

    latex_cmd <- resolve_latex_command("pdflatex")
    latex_log <- tryCatch(
      system2(
         latex_cmd,
         args = c(
           "-interaction=nonstopmode",
           "-halt-on-error",
           "-output-directory", build_dir,
           tex_file
         ),
         stdout = TRUE,
         stderr = TRUE
      ),
      error = function(e) stop("Standalone table PDF render failed for ", file_stub, ": ", conditionMessage(e))
    )
    latex_status <- attr(latex_log, "status")
    if (!is.null(latex_status) && latex_status != 0) {
      stop(
         "Standalone table PDF render failed for ", file_stub, " via pdflatex. Last log lines: ",
         paste(utils::tail(latex_log, 20), collapse = " | ")
      )
    }
    pdf_file <- sub("\\.tex$", ".pdf", tex_file)
    if (!file.exists(pdf_file)) {
      stop("Standalone table PDF render failed for ", file_stub, ": expected PDF not found at ", pdf_file)
    }
    out_pdf <- results_path(paste0(file_stub, ".pdf"))
    fs::file_copy(pdf_file, out_pdf, overwrite = TRUE)
    invisible(out_pdf)
}

# helper: turn any gtsummary table into a PDF-safe LaTeX table while keeping
# numbering under explicit notebook control.
to_pdf_table <- function(tbl, font_size = 8, landscape = FALSE,
                         label_col_width = NULL, longtable = FALSE,
                         caption_mode = c("plain", "numbered", "none"),
                         display_label = NULL,
                         page_break_before = FALSE) {




                                                            20
caption_mode <- match.arg(caption_mode)
tbl_ncol <- tryCatch(ncol(gtsummary::as_tibble(tbl)), error = function(e) NA_integer_)
if (is.finite(tbl_ncol) && tbl_ncol > 6 && font_size > 6) font_size <- 6

caption_text <- tryCatch(tbl$table_styling$caption, error = function(e) NULL)
tbl_local <- tbl
if (!identical(caption_mode, "numbered")) {
  tbl_local$table_styling$caption <- NULL
}

kbl <- gtsummary::as_kable(
  tbl_local,
  format     = "latex",
  booktabs = TRUE,
  longtable = longtable
)

if (!is.null(label_col_width)) {
  kbl <- kableExtra::column_spec(kbl, 1, width = label_col_width)
}

latex_opts <- if (longtable) {
  c("repeat_header")
} else {
  c("hold_position", "scale_down")
}
kbl <- kableExtra::kable_styling(
  kbl,
  latex_options = latex_opts,
  font_size     = font_size,
  full_width    = !longtable,
  position      = "center"
)

kbl_txt <- latex_safe_table_text(as.character(kbl))
if (identical(caption_mode, "numbered")) {




                                                        21
     mark_float_emitted()
     return(knitr::asis_output(kbl_txt))
    }
    title_i <- if (identical(caption_mode, "none")) NULL else caption_text
    render_table_blocks(
      kbl_txt,
      title = title_i,
      display_label = display_label,
      landscape = landscape,
      page_break_before = page_break_before
    )
}

# helper: scan the notebook source for package usage so the render fails fast
# if a collaborator has not restored the required `renv` environment.
extract_notebook_pkgs <- function(path) {
  if (!file.exists(path)) return(character())
  lines <- readLines(path, warn = FALSE)
  # Local extractor used for both `library(pkg)` and `pkg::fn()` patterns.
  capture_group <- function(pattern, x) {
    hits <- regexec(pattern, x, perl = TRUE)



                                                                  22
     matches <- regmatches(x, hits)
     vals <- vapply(matches, function(m) if (length(m) >= 2) m[2] else NA_character_, character(1))
     vals[is.finite(nchar(vals))]
    }
    lib_pkgs <- capture_group("library\\s*\\(\\s*['\"]?([A-Za-z][A-Za-z0-9.]*)['\"]?", lines)
    ns_pkgs <- capture_group("([A-Za-z][A-Za-z0-9.]*)::[A-Za-z][A-Za-z0-9._]*", lines)
    unique(c(lib_pkgs, ns_pkgs))
}

qmd_source <- here::here("Code Drafts", "ABG-VBG analysis 2026-4-21.qmd")
notebook_pkgs <- extract_notebook_pkgs(qmd_source)

renv_dep_pkgs <- character()
if ("renv" %in% rownames(installed.packages())) {
  renv_dep_pkgs <- tryCatch(
    {
       dep_tbl <- renv::dependencies(qmd_source, progress = FALSE)
       if (!is.null(dep_tbl$Package)) unique(dep_tbl$Package) else character()
    },
    error = function(e) character()
  )
}

base_drop <- c("base", "datasets", "graphics", "grDevices", "methods", "stats", "tools", "utils")
ignore_pkgs <- c("pkg")
required_pkgs <- sort(unique(setdiff(c(seed_pkgs, notebook_pkgs), c(base_drop, ignore_pkgs))))
if (length(renv_dep_pkgs)) {
  renv_only <- setdiff(renv_dep_pkgs, c(required_pkgs, base_drop, ignore_pkgs))
  if (length(renv_only)) {
    message("Dependency audit note (renv::dependencies only): ", paste(sort(renv_only), collapse = ", "))
  }
}

# Fail fast if packages are missing (use renv to install)
missing_pkgs <- setdiff(required_pkgs, rownames(installed.packages()))
if (length(missing_pkgs)) {




                                                            23
    stop(
      "Missing packages: ", paste(missing_pkgs, collapse = ", "),
      ". Install with renv::install(c(...)); if renv is absent, install 'renv' first; then run renv::snapshot()."
    )
}

# Attach packages from one authoritative location.
ensure_packages_loaded <- function(pkgs) {
  invisible(lapply(pkgs, function(pkg) {
    if (!requireNamespace(pkg, quietly = TRUE)) {
      stop("Required package is not available: ", pkg)
    }
    if (!paste0("package:", pkg) %in% search()) {
      suppressPackageStartupMessages(library(pkg, character.only = TRUE))
    }
  }))
}
ensure_packages_loaded(required_pkgs)

# Purpose: cohort flow helpers.
format_count <- function(x) {
  format(as.integer(x), big.mark = ",", trim = TRUE, scientific = FALSE)
}

cohort_flow_input_path <- fs::path(data_dir_name, "full_db.dta")

# helper: read only the columns needed for Figure 1 so the cohort-flow section
# stays fast and does not depend on unrelated variables.
read_cohort_flow_input <- function(path, cols = cohort_flow_cols) {
  stopifnot(file.exists(path))
  haven::read_dta(path, col_select = dplyr::all_of(cols))
}

# helper: compute the count objects that feed the cohort-flow diagram. Keeping
# this logic in one function makes later figure edits less error-prone.
compute_cohort_flow_counts <- function(df) {
  encounter_type_num <- suppressWarnings(as.integer(df$encounter_type))
  if (anyNA(encounter_type_num)) {
    stop(
      "Cohort flow count input has missing encounter_type values (n = ",
      sum(is.na(encounter_type_num)), ")."
    )
  }

  has_abg_num <- suppressWarnings(as.integer(df$has_abg))
  has_vbg_num <- suppressWarnings(as.integer(df$has_vbg))
  has_abg_num[is.na(has_abg_num)] <- 0L
  has_vbg_num[is.na(has_vbg_num)] <- 0L



                                                            25
    analytic_flag <- encounter_type_num != 1L
    has_abg_flag <- analytic_flag & has_abg_num == 1L
    has_vbg_flag <- analytic_flag & has_vbg_num == 1L
    both_flag <- has_abg_flag & has_vbg_flag
    abg_only_flag <- has_abg_flag & !has_vbg_flag
    vbg_only_flag <- has_vbg_flag & !has_abg_flag
    neither_flag <- analytic_flag & !has_abg_flag & !has_vbg_flag
    abg_paco2_flag <- has_abg_flag & !is.na(df$paco2)
    vbg_co2_flag <- has_vbg_flag & !is.na(df$vbg_co2)

    analytic_n <- sum(analytic_flag, na.rm = TRUE)
    stopifnot(sum(abg_only_flag, na.rm = TRUE) + sum(vbg_only_flag, na.rm = TRUE) +
                sum(both_flag, na.rm = TRUE) + sum(neither_flag, na.rm = TRUE) == analytic_n)
    stopifnot(sum(abg_only_flag, na.rm = TRUE) + sum(both_flag, na.rm = TRUE) ==
                sum(has_abg_flag, na.rm = TRUE))
    stopifnot(sum(vbg_only_flag, na.rm = TRUE) + sum(both_flag, na.rm = TRUE) ==
                sum(has_vbg_flag, na.rm = TRUE))

    list(
      total_extracted = nrow(df),
      excluded_ambulatory = sum(encounter_type_num == 1L, na.rm = TRUE),
      analytic_ed_inpatient = analytic_n,
      abg_tested = sum(has_abg_flag, na.rm = TRUE),
      vbg_tested = sum(has_vbg_flag, na.rm = TRUE),
      both_abg_vbg = sum(both_flag, na.rm = TRUE),
      abg_only = sum(abg_only_flag, na.rm = TRUE),
      vbg_only = sum(vbg_only_flag, na.rm = TRUE),
      neither_abg_nor_vbg = sum(neither_flag, na.rm = TRUE),
      abg_with_paco2 = sum(abg_paco2_flag, na.rm = TRUE),
      vbg_with_vbg_co2 = sum(vbg_co2_flag, na.rm = TRUE)
    )
}

# helper: add the shared comparability annotation beneath the two weighted
# endpoints without changing the underlying consort graph geometry.




                                                            26
decorate_weighted_comparability <- function(built_graph, weighted_nodes,
                                            label_text,
                                            text_gp = grid::gpar(col = "grey25", cex = 0.78),
                                            label_x = grid::unit(0.5, "npc"),
                                            label_y = grid::unit(0.035, "npc")) {
  stopifnot(inherits(built_graph, "gTree"))
  stopifnot(length(weighted_nodes) == 2L)

    band_label <- grid::textGrob(
      label = label_text,
      x = label_x,
      y = label_y,
      just = "center",
      gp = text_gp,
      name = "weighted_comparability_label"
    )

    list(
      built_graph = built_graph,
      pre_draw = NULL,
      post_draw = function() {
        grid::grid.draw(band_label)
      }
    )
}

# helper: export the cohort-flow graph to manuscript artifacts plus an optional
# low-DPI inline preview while drawing the same built grob on each device to
# avoid device-specific layout drift.
save_cohort_flow_outputs <- function(graph, png_file, pdf_file,
                                     width_mm = 180, height_mm = 150,
                                     dpi = 600, bg = "white",
                                     decorate_fn = NULL,
                                     preview_file = NULL,
                                     preview_dpi = 96) {
  width_in <- width_mm / 25.4




                                                          27
height_in <- height_mm / 25.4
draw_graph <- function(new_page = TRUE) {
  built_graph <- consort::build_grid(graph)
  decoration <- NULL
  if (!is.null(decorate_fn)) {
    decoration <- decorate_fn(built_graph)
    if (inherits(decoration, "gTree")) {
      built_graph <- decoration
      decoration <- NULL
    } else if (is.list(decoration) && inherits(decoration$built_graph, "gTree")) {
      built_graph <- decoration$built_graph
    }
  }
  # Raster devices and inline replay paths often need an explicit new page,
  # but a freshly opened PDF device already has page 1 active. Calling
  # grid.newpage() there creates a blank first page and pushes the diagram to
  # page 2, which LaTeX then includes incorrectly.
  if (isTRUE(new_page)) {
    grid::grid.newpage()
  }
  if (is.list(decoration) && is.function(decoration$pre_draw)) {
    decoration$pre_draw()
  }
  grid::grid.draw(built_graph)
  if (is.list(decoration) && is.function(decoration$post_draw)) {
    decoration$post_draw()
  }
}

fs::dir_create(fs::path_dir(png_file), recurse = TRUE)
fs::dir_create(fs::path_dir(pdf_file), recurse = TRUE)

ragg::agg_png(
  filename = png_file,
  width = width_mm,
  height = height_mm,




                                                         28
 units = "mm",
 res = dpi,
 background = bg
)
draw_graph(new_page = TRUE)
grDevices::dev.off()

if (capabilities("cairo")) {
  grDevices::cairo_pdf(
    filename = pdf_file,
    width = width_in,
    height = height_in,
    bg = bg
  )
} else {
  grDevices::pdf(
    file = pdf_file,
    width = width_in,
    height = height_in,
    bg = bg
  )
}
draw_graph(new_page = FALSE)
grDevices::dev.off()

if (!is.null(preview_file)) {
  fs::dir_create(fs::path_dir(preview_file), recurse = TRUE)
  ragg::agg_png(
    filename = preview_file,

1.1 Helper functions for model diagnostics

# Diagnostics helper functions for MI/IPW pipeline

# helper: fail early if an analysis stage expects complete covariates but the
# current data still contains missing values in those columns.
assert_no_na_covars <- function(df, covars, context = "") {
  missing <- setdiff(covars, names(df))
  stopifnot(length(missing) == 0)
  na_counts <- vapply(df[, covars, drop = FALSE], function(x) sum(is.na(x)), numeric(1))
  if (any(na_counts > 0)) {



                                                          38
     msg <- paste0(
       "NA values found in covariates (", context, "): ",
       paste(names(na_counts)[na_counts > 0], na_counts[na_counts > 0], collapse = ", ")
     )
     stop(msg)
    }
    invisible(TRUE)
}

# helper: collapse the raw `mice` logged-events table into counts that are
# easier to review in diagnostics CSVs and notebook output.
summarize_logged_events <- function(mids_obj) {
  ev <- mids_obj$loggedEvents
  if (is.null(ev) || nrow(ev) == 0L) {
    return(data.frame(
       variable = character(),
       method = character(),
       event = character(),
       n = integer(),
       pct = numeric(),
       stringsAsFactors = FALSE
    ))
  }
  stopifnot(all(c("dep", "meth", "out") %in% names(ev)))
  tbl <- as.data.frame(table(ev$dep, ev$meth, ev$out), stringsAsFactors = FALSE)
  names(tbl) <- c("variable", "method", "event", "n")
  tbl <- tbl[tbl$n > 0, , drop = FALSE]
  tbl <- tbl[order(-tbl$n), , drop = FALSE]
  tbl$pct <- tbl$n / sum(tbl$n)
  tbl
}

# helper: consistently pull propensity scores out of WeightIt objects.
extract_weightit_ps <- function(w) {
  stopifnot(!is.null(w$ps))
  as.numeric(w$ps)




                                                           39
}

# helper: effective sample size for a vector of weights.
ess <- function(w) {
  w <- w[is.finite(w)]
  stopifnot(length(w) > 0)
  sum(w)^2 / sum(w^2)
}

# helper: quantify how much total weight is concentrated in the largest weights.
weight_concentration <- function(w, top_p = 0.01) {
  w <- w[is.finite(w)]
  stopifnot(length(w) > 0)
  ord <- sort(w, decreasing = TRUE)
  n_top <- max(1L, floor(length(ord) * top_p))
  sum(ord[seq_len(n_top)]) / sum(ord)
}

# helper: summarize one set of inverse-probability weights and their matching
# propensity scores for later diagnostics tables.
weight_summary <- function(w, ps, ps_floor, truncated) {
  w_ok <- w[is.finite(w)]
  stopifnot(length(w_ok) > 0)
  ps_ok <- ps[is.finite(ps)]
  stopifnot(length(ps_ok) > 0)
  out <- data.frame(
    n = length(w_ok),
    mean = mean(w_ok, na.rm = TRUE),
    sd = stats::sd(w_ok, na.rm = TRUE),
    min = min(w_ok, na.rm = TRUE),
    p01 = stats::quantile(w_ok, 0.01, na.rm = TRUE),
    p05 = stats::quantile(w_ok, 0.05, na.rm = TRUE),
    p95 = stats::quantile(w_ok, 0.95, na.rm = TRUE),
    p99 = stats::quantile(w_ok, 0.99, na.rm = TRUE),
    max = max(w_ok, na.rm = TRUE),
    sum_w = sum(w_ok, na.rm = TRUE),




                                                           40
     ess = ess(w_ok),
     top01_weight_share = weight_concentration(w_ok, top_p = 0.01),
     ps_floor = ps_floor,
     trunc_rate = mean(truncated, na.rm = TRUE),
     ps_min = min(ps_ok, na.rm = TRUE),
     ps_p01 = stats::quantile(ps_ok, 0.01, na.rm = TRUE),
     ps_p05 = stats::quantile(ps_ok, 0.05, na.rm = TRUE),
     ps_p95 = stats::quantile(ps_ok, 0.95, na.rm = TRUE),
     ps_max = max(ps_ok, na.rm = TRUE),
     stringsAsFactors = FALSE
    )
    out
}

# helper: convert fitted propensities into the project-specific one-sided IPSW
# weights used to standardize the tested cohorts back to the analytic cohort.
compute_ipow_weights <- function(w, treat, ps_floor_quantile = 0.01,
                                 stabilize = TRUE) {
  # One-sided IPSW for this project:
  # outcome models are fit only within the tested cohort, so only tested rows
  # receive inverse-propensity weights. The target is the full analytic cohort,
  # not the untested subgroup. We truncate extremely small propensities to avoid
  # unstable huge weights, then optionally stabilize so treated weights average ~1.
  ps <- extract_weightit_ps(w)
  if (length(ps) != length(treat)) stop("Propensity length mismatch.")
  treat <- as.integer(treat)
  if (!all(treat %in% c(0L, 1L))) stop("Treatment indicator must be 0/1.")

    ps_obs <- ps[treat == 1L & is.finite(ps)]
    if (!length(ps_obs)) stop("No treated observations with finite propensity.")
    ps_floor <- as.numeric(stats::quantile(ps_obs, probs = ps_floor_quantile, na.rm = TRUE))
    if (!is.finite(ps_floor) || ps_floor <= 0) stop("Invalid propensity floor.")

    w_raw <- rep(NA_real_, length(ps))
    w_raw[treat == 1L] <- 1 / ps[treat == 1L]




                                                            41
    cap <- 1 / ps_floor
    truncated <- treat == 1L & is.finite(ps) & ps < ps_floor
    w_trunc <- w_raw
    w_trunc[truncated] <- cap

    if (stabilize) {
      w_trunc <- w_trunc / mean(w_trunc[treat == 1L], na.rm = TRUE)
    }

    list(
      weights   = w_trunc,
      ps        = ps,
      ps_floor = ps_floor,
      cap       = cap,
      truncated = truncated
    )
}

# helper: stop immediately if a weighting step produces NaN/Inf values.
assert_finite_weights <- function(w, name = "weights") {
  if (any(!is.finite(w))) {
    stop("Non-finite values detected in ", name, ".")
  }
  invisible(TRUE)
}

# helper: time an expression and append one standardized row to the runtime log.
runtime_logger <- function(step_name, expr, notes = NA_character_) {
  start_time <- Sys.time()
  result <- eval(expr)
  end_time <- Sys.time()
  sec <- as.numeric(difftime(end_time, start_time, units = "secs"))
  row <- data.frame(
    step_name = step_name,
    seconds = sec,
    start_time = as.character(start_time),




                                                               42
     end_time = as.character(end_time),
     notes = notes,
     run_id = runtime_run_id,
     run_mode = RUN_MODE,
     n_subset = subset_n,
     stringsAsFactors = FALSE
    )
    runtime_log <<- dplyr::bind_rows(runtime_log, row)
    result
}

# helper: create a consistently labeled context object so warnings and model
# diagnostics can be traced back to the exact analysis stage that produced them.
make_context <- function(stage, component,
                         analysis_variant = NA_character_,
                         model_type = NA_character_,
                         group = NA_character_,
                         outcome = NA_character_,
                         imputation = NA_integer_,
                         batch = NA_integer_) {
  list(
    stage = stage,
    component = component,
    analysis_variant = analysis_variant,
    model_type = model_type,
    group = group,
    outcome = outcome,
    imputation = imputation,
    batch = batch
  )
}

# helper: evaluate an expression while intercepting warnings into a structured
# data frame instead of letting them vanish into console output.
capture_warnings <- function(expr, context) {
  warn_rows <- list()




                                                          43
stopifnot(all(c("stage", "component", "analysis_variant", "model_type",
                "group", "outcome", "imputation", "batch") %in% names(context)))
ctx <- list(
  stage = as.character(context$stage),
  component = as.character(context$component),
  analysis_variant = as.character(context$analysis_variant),
  model_type = as.character(context$model_type),
  group = as.character(context$group),
  outcome = as.character(context$outcome),
  imputation = as.integer(context$imputation),
  batch = as.integer(context$batch)
)
val <- withCallingHandlers(
  expr,
  warning = function(w) {
    warn_rows <<- append(warn_rows, list(data.frame(
      time = as.character(Sys.time()),
      stage = ctx$stage,
      component = ctx$component,
      analysis_variant = ctx$analysis_variant,
      model_type = ctx$model_type,
      group = ctx$group,
      outcome = ctx$outcome,
      imputation = ctx$imputation,
      batch = ctx$batch,
      message = conditionMessage(w),
      stringsAsFactors = FALSE
    )))
    invokeRestart("muffleWarning")
  }
)
warnings_df <- if (length(warn_rows)) {
  dplyr::bind_rows(warn_rows)
} else {
  data.frame(
    time = character(), stage = character(), component = character(),




                                                        44
       analysis_variant = character(), model_type = character(),
       group = character(), outcome = character(), imputation = integer(),
       batch = integer(), message = character(), stringsAsFactors = FALSE
      )
    }
    list(value = val, warnings = warnings_df)
}

# helper: append captured warnings to the global MI warning logs, while
# separating informational `mice` messages from actionable warnings.
append_warnings <- function(wlist) {
  stopifnot(is.data.frame(wlist) || is.list(wlist))
  df <- if (is.data.frame(wlist)) wlist else dplyr::bind_rows(wlist)
  stopifnot(is.data.frame(df))
  stopifnot("message" %in% names(df))
  info_rows <- df[grepl("^Number of logged events", df$message), , drop = FALSE]
  if (nrow(info_rows)) {
    mi_info_log <<- dplyr::bind_rows(mi_info_log, info_rows)
  }
  df <- df[!grepl("^Number of logged events", df$message), , drop = FALSE]
  if (nrow(df) == 0L) return(invisible(FALSE))
  mi_warn_log <<- dplyr::bind_rows(mi_warn_log, df)
  invisible(TRUE)
}

# helper: resolve the active notebook path across Quarto/knitr working-directory
# changes so later audits can always locate the source file.
resolve_current_qmd <- function() {
  # Resolve qmd path robustly across render/knit working directories.
  candidates <- c(
    tryCatch(knitr::current_input(), error = function(e) NA_character_),
    tryCatch(knitr::current_input(dir = TRUE), error = function(e) NA_character_),
    here::here("Code Drafts", "ABG-VBG analysis 2026-4-21.qmd"),
    "Code Drafts/ABG-VBG analysis 2026-4-21.qmd",
    "ABG-VBG analysis 2026-4-21.qmd",
    here::here("Code Drafts", "ABG-VBG analysis 2025-12-11.qmd"),




                                                           45
     "Code Drafts/ABG-VBG analysis 2025-12-11.qmd",
     "ABG-VBG analysis 2025-12-11.qmd"
    )
    candidates <- candidates[!is.na(candidates) & nzchar(candidates)]
    existing <- candidates[file.exists(candidates)]
    if (!length(existing)) {
      stop("Could not resolve qmd source path for audit checks.")
    }
    normalizePath(existing[[1]], winslash = "/", mustWork = TRUE)
}

# helper: pull warning tables out of lists of fit results and append them to
# the notebook-wide warning logs in one call.
collect_warnings_from_list <- function(xlist) {
  warn_list <- lapply(xlist, function(x) {
    if (is.list(x) && !is.null(x$warnings)) x$warnings else NULL
  })
  warn_list <- warn_list[!vapply(warn_list, is.null, logical(1))]
  append_warnings(warn_list)
  invisible(TRUE)
}

  if (nrow(df) == 0L) return(invisible(FALSE))
  mi_outcome_diag <<- dplyr::bind_rows(mi_outcome_diag, df)
  invisible(TRUE)
}

summarize_warnings_log <- function(path = results_path("warnings_log.csv")) {
  warn_df <- read.csv(path, stringsAsFactors = FALSE)
  if (nrow(warn_df) == 0L) return(data.frame())
  warn_df |>
    dplyr::count(stage, component, analysis_variant, model_type, message, sort = TRUE)




                                                            46
}

# helper: write CSV outputs with run identifiers attached so later audits can
# tell which render produced a given artifact.
write_csv_safely <- function(df, path, row_names = FALSE, required_cols = NULL) {
  run_id <- diag_run_id
  run_ts <- diag_run_ts
  stopifnot(!is.null(df))
  df <- as.data.frame(df)
  # Normalize pillar/vctrs numeric classes to base numeric for CSV export
  df <- dplyr::mutate(
    df,
    dplyr::across(
      where(~ inherits(.x, "pillar_num")),
      ~ suppressWarnings(as.numeric(.x))
    )
  )
  if (!is.null(required_cols)) {
    missing <- setdiff(required_cols, names(df))
    stopifnot(length(missing) == 0)
  }
  if (nrow(df) == 0L) {
    if (!("empty" %in% names(df))) df$empty <- logical(0)
  }
  df$run_id <- rep(run_id, nrow(df))
  df$run_ts <- rep(run_ts, nrow(df))
  utils::write.csv(df, path, row.names = row_names)
  invisible(TRUE)
}

# helper: write line-based diagnostics with the same run metadata header used
# for CSV artifacts.
write_diag_lines <- function(lines, path) {
  run_id <- diag_run_id
  run_ts <- diag_run_ts
  header <- paste0("run_id: ", run_id, " run_ts: ", run_ts)




                                                          47
    writeLines(c(header, lines), con = path)
    invisible(TRUE)
}

# helper: drop unused factor levels after filtering so model frames and tables
# do not silently carry dead categories.
droplevels_all <- function(df, vars = NULL) {
  if (is.null(vars)) {
    vars <- names(df)[vapply(df, is.factor, logical(1))]
  } else {
    vars <- intersect(vars, names(df))
    vars <- vars[vapply(df[vars], is.factor, logical(1))]
  }
  for (nm in vars) df[[nm]] <- droplevels(df[[nm]])
  df
}

# helper: append one GC-based memory snapshot for a named stage. This makes it
# easier to identify where long renders begin to consume disproportionate RAM.
append_mem_snapshot <- function(stage_id, context_id = NA_character_, when = "pre") {
  g <- gc()
  cn <- colnames(g)
  used_col <- if ("used" %in% cn) "used" else cn[grepl("used", cn)][1]
  trig_col <- if ("gc trigger" %in% cn) "gc trigger" else cn[grepl("trigger", cn)][1]
  max_col   <- if ("max used" %in% cn) "max used" else cn[grepl("max", cn)][1]
  n_used <- as.numeric(g["Ncells", used_col])
  v_used <- as.numeric(g["Vcells", used_col])
  v_trig <- as.numeric(g["Vcells", trig_col])
  v_max <- as.numeric(g["Vcells", max_col])
  mem_max <- tryCatch(mem.maxVSize(), error = function(e) NA_real_)
  row <- data.frame(
    run_id = diag_run_id,
    run_ts = diag_run_ts,
    stage_id = stage_id,
    context_id = context_id,
    when = when,




                                                          48
     time = as.character(Sys.time()),
     Ncells_used = n_used,
     Vcells_used = v_used,
     Vcells_gc_trigger = v_trig,
     Vcells_max_used = v_max,
     mem_max_vsize = mem_max,
     stringsAsFactors = FALSE
    )
    memory_snapshots <<- dplyr::bind_rows(memory_snapshots, row)
    invisible(TRUE)
}

# helper: write a compact CSV describing factor cardinality before expensive
# GBM fits, since high-cardinality factors are a common failure mode.
write_factor_levels_diag <- function(df, vars, context_id, file_prefix = "gbm_preflight_factor_levels") {
  key <- paste0(file_prefix, "::", context_id)
  if (key %in% factor_diag_written) {
    return(invisible(FALSE))
  }
  vars <- intersect(vars, names(df))
  if (!length(vars)) {
    return(invisible(FALSE))
  }
  diag <- lapply(vars, function(v) {
    x <- df[[v]]
    if (!is.factor(x)) return(NULL)
    tab <- table(x, useNA = "ifany")
    n_unused <- sum(tab == 0)
    top <- utils::head(sort(tab, decreasing = TRUE), 5)
    data.frame(
      variable = v,
      class = class(x)[1],
      nlevels = nlevels(x),
      n_unused_levels = n_unused,
      top_levels = paste(names(top), as.integer(top), sep = "=", collapse = "; "),
      n_missing = sum(is.na(x)),




                                                            49
       context_id = context_id,
       stringsAsFactors = FALSE
      )
    })
    diag <- dplyr::bind_rows(diag)
    if (nrow(diag) == 0L) return(invisible(FALSE))
    out_path <- results_path(paste0(file_prefix, "_", context_id, ".csv"))
    write_csv_safely(diag, out_path, row_names = FALSE)
    factor_diag_written <<- c(factor_diag_written, key)
    invisible(TRUE)
}

# helper: estimate sampled design-matrix width so large GBM model matrices can
# be anticipated before the full fit is attempted.
log_design_dims <- function(df, covars, context_id, sample_n = 5000L) {
  covars <- intersect(covars, names(df))
  if (!length(covars)) return(invisible(FALSE))
  n_full <- nrow(df)
  n_samp <- min(sample_n, n_full)
  set.seed(20251206)
  idx <- sample.int(n_full, n_samp)
  df_s <- df[idx, covars, drop = FALSE]
  fml <- stats::as.formula(paste("~", paste(covars, collapse = " + ")))
  mm <- stats::model.matrix(fml, data = df_s)
  n_factor <- sum(vapply(df_s, is.factor, logical(1)))
  max_nlevels <- if (n_factor > 0) max(vapply(df_s[vapply(df_s, is.factor, logical(1))], nlevels, integer(1))) else 0L
  row <- data.frame(
    run_id = diag_run_id,
    run_ts = diag_run_ts,
    context_id = context_id,
    nrow_full = n_full,
    nrow_sample = n_samp,
    ncol_model_matrix = ncol(mm),
    n_factor_vars = n_factor,
    max_nlevels_factor = max_nlevels,
    stringsAsFactors = FALSE




                                                            50
    )
    gbm_preflight_design_dims <<- dplyr::bind_rows(gbm_preflight_design_dims, row)
    invisible(TRUE)
}

# helper: run the full GBM preflight suite: drop empty levels, estimate design
# size, log warnings, and stop when the model matrix looks infeasible.
gbm_preflight <- function(df, covars, context_id, sample_n = 50000L) {
  df <- droplevels_all(df)
  write_factor_levels_diag(df, covars, context_id, file_prefix = "gbm_preflight_factor_levels")
  covars <- intersect(covars, names(df))
  if (!length(covars)) return(invisible(FALSE))
  n_full <- nrow(df)
  n_samp <- min(sample_n, n_full)
  set.seed(20251206)
  idx <- sample.int(n_full, n_samp)
  df_s <- df[idx, covars, drop = FALSE]
  fml <- stats::as.formula(paste("~", paste(covars, collapse = " + ")))
  mm <- stats::model.matrix(fml, data = df_s)
  n_factor <- sum(vapply(df_s, is.factor, logical(1)))
  max_nlevels <- if (n_factor > 0) {
    max(vapply(df_s[vapply(df_s, is.factor, logical(1))], nlevels, integer(1)))
  } else 0L
  est_bytes <- n_full * ncol(mm) * 8
  row <- data.frame(
    run_id = diag_run_id,
    run_ts = diag_run_ts,
    context_id = context_id,
    nrow_full = n_full,
    nrow_sample = n_samp,
    ncol_model_matrix = ncol(mm),
    n_factor_vars = n_factor,
    max_nlevels_factor = max_nlevels,
    est_bytes = est_bytes,
    est_gb = est_bytes / 1024^3,
    stringsAsFactors = FALSE




                                                            51
)
gbm_preflight_design_dims <<- dplyr::bind_rows(gbm_preflight_design_dims, row)
warn_msgs <- character()
if (is.finite(est_bytes) && est_bytes > GBM_MM_EST_BYTES_WARN) {
  warn_msgs <- c(warn_msgs, paste0("est_dense_mm_gb>", round(GBM_MM_EST_BYTES_WARN / 1024^3, 2)))
}
if (ncol(mm) > MAX_GBM_MM_COLS_WARN) {
  warn_msgs <- c(warn_msgs, paste0("mm_cols_warn>", MAX_GBM_MM_COLS_WARN))
}
if (max_nlevels > MAX_GBM_FACTOR_LEVELS_WARN) {
  warn_msgs <- c(warn_msgs, paste0("factor_levels_warn>", MAX_GBM_FACTOR_LEVELS_WARN))
}
if (length(warn_msgs)) {
  gbm_preflight_warnings <<- dplyr::bind_rows(
    gbm_preflight_warnings,
    data.frame(
      run_id = diag_run_id,
      run_ts = diag_run_ts,
      context_id = context_id,
      nrow_full = n_full,
      ncol_model_matrix = ncol(mm),
      max_nlevels_factor = max_nlevels,
      est_gb = est_bytes / 1024^3,
      warning = paste(warn_msgs, collapse = ";"),
      stringsAsFactors = FALSE
    )
  )
}
if (ncol(mm) > MAX_GBM_MM_COLS_STOP || max_nlevels > MAX_GBM_FACTOR_LEVELS_STOP) {
  stop(
    "GBM preflight stop: context=", context_id,
    "; ncol_model_matrix=", ncol(mm),
    "; max_nlevels_factor=", max_nlevels,
    ". Consider collapsing factor levels or removing high-cardinality predictors."
  )
}




                                                        52
    invisible(TRUE)
}

# helper: print a small preview with an optional title during debugging.
print_head <- function(df, n = 10, title = NULL) {
  if (!is.null(title)) message(title)
  if (is.null(df) || nrow(df) == 0L) {
    message("No rows to display.")
    return(invisible(FALSE))
  }
  print(utils::head(df, n))
  invisible(TRUE)
}

# helper: assert that an object is data-frame-like before downstream code tries
# to treat it as tabular data.
assert_is_df <- function(x, context = "") {
  if (is.null(x)) {
    stop(context, ": object is NULL")
  }
  if (!inherits(x, "data.frame")) {
    stop(context, ": expected data.frame/tibble; got class=",
         paste(class(x), collapse = ", "), " typeof=", typeof(x))
  }
  invisible(TRUE)
}

# helper: stop with a readable message when required columns are missing.
assert_has_cols <- function(df, cols, context = "") {
  missing <- setdiff(cols, names(df))
  if (length(missing)) {
    stop(context, ": missing required columns: ", paste(missing, collapse = ", "))
  }
  invisible(TRUE)
}




                                                          53
# helper: obtain `nrow()` only after validating that the input is truly tabular.
safe_nrow <- function(df, context = "") {
  assert_is_df(df, context)
  nr <- nrow(df)
  if (!is.numeric(nr) || length(nr) != 1L || is.na(nr)) {
    stop(context, ": nrow(df) returned invalid value: ",
         paste0(capture.output(str(nr)), collapse = " "))
  }
  as.integer(nr)
}

# helper: expose the cumulative plot-drop log for debugging and export.
plot_drop_log <- function() {
  plot_drop_log_df
}

# helper: record rows dropped during figure preparation so suspicious plotting
# losses are always audit-able after a render.
log_plot_drop <- function(plot_name, reason, n_dropped,
                          n_before = NA_integer_, n_after = NA_integer_,
                          stage = NA_character_, extra = NA_character_) {
  plot_drop_log_df <<- dplyr::bind_rows(
    plot_drop_log(),
    data.frame(plot = plot_name, reason = reason, n_dropped = n_dropped,
               n_before = n_before, n_after = n_after,
               stage = stage, extra = extra,
               stringsAsFactors = FALSE)
  )
  if (identical(PLOT_DROP_POLICY, "stop")) {
    stop("Plot data dropped in ", plot_name, ": ", reason)
  } else {
    warning("Plot data dropped in ", plot_name, ": ", reason, call. = FALSE)
  }
}

# helper: wrap model fitting so warnings, convergence flags, and simple




                                                          54
# separation diagnostics are captured in one standardized object.
fit_with_diagnostics <- function(fit_fun, context, prob_eps = PROB_EPS) {
  stopifnot(all(c("stage", "component", "analysis_variant", "model_type",
                  "group", "outcome", "imputation", "batch") %in% names(context)))
  cap <- capture_warnings(
    tryCatch(fit_fun(), error = function(e) e),
    context = context
  )
  append_warnings(cap$warnings)
  fit <- cap$value
  warn_msgs <- if (is.data.frame(cap$warnings)) cap$warnings$message else character()
  warning_n <- if (is.data.frame(cap$warnings)) nrow(cap$warnings) else 0L
  top_warning <- if (warning_n) warn_msgs[1] else NA_character_

  if (inherits(fit, "error")) {
    diag <- data.frame(
      stage = as.character(context$stage),
      component = as.character(context$component),
      analysis_variant = as.character(context$analysis_variant),
      model_type = as.character(context$model_type),
      group = as.character(context$group),
      outcome = as.character(context$outcome),
      imputation = as.integer(context$imputation),
      n_used = NA_integer_, events = NA_integer_,
      converged = NA, iter = NA_integer_,
      sep_flag = NA, nonconv_flag = NA,
      min_phat = NA_real_, max_phat = NA_real_,
      warning_n = warning_n, top_warning = top_warning,
      error_message = conditionMessage(fit),
      stringsAsFactors = FALSE
    )
    return(list(fit = NULL, diag = diag, warnings = cap$warnings))
  }

  phat <- tryCatch(fitted(fit), error = function(e) NA_real_)
  min_phat <- if (all(is.na(phat))) NA_real_ else min(phat, na.rm = TRUE)




                                                          55
    max_phat <- if (all(is.na(phat))) NA_real_ else max(phat, na.rm = TRUE)
    sep_flag <- FALSE
    if (is.finite(min_phat) && min_phat < prob_eps) sep_flag <- TRUE
    if (is.finite(max_phat) && max_phat > 1 - prob_eps) sep_flag <- TRUE
    if (any(grepl("fitted probabilities numerically 0 or 1", warn_msgs, fixed = TRUE))) sep_flag <- TRUE

    conv_val <- if (!is.null(fit$converged)) isTRUE(fit$converged) else NA
    iter_val <- if (!is.null(fit$iter)) fit$iter else NA_integer_
    nonconv_flag <- isFALSE(conv_val) || any(grepl("did not converge", warn_msgs, fixed = TRUE))

    mf <- tryCatch(model.frame(fit), error = function(e) NULL)
    y <- if (!is.null(mf)) tryCatch(model.response(mf), error = function(e) NULL) else NULL
    n_used <- if (!is.null(y)) length(y) else NA_integer_
    events <- if (!is.null(y) && is.numeric(y)) sum(y == 1, na.rm = TRUE) else NA_integer_

    diag <- data.frame(
      stage = as.character(context$stage),
      component = as.character(context$component),
      analysis_variant = as.character(context$analysis_variant),
      model_type = as.character(context$model_type),
      group = as.character(context$group),
      outcome = as.character(context$outcome),
      imputation = as.integer(context$imputation),
      n_used = n_used, events = events,
      converged = conv_val, iter = iter_val,
      sep_flag = sep_flag, nonconv_flag = nonconv_flag,
      min_phat = min_phat, max_phat = max_phat,
      warning_n = warning_n, top_warning = top_warning,
      error_message = NA_character_,
      stringsAsFactors = FALSE
    )
    list(fit = fit, diag = diag, warnings = cap$warnings)
}

# helper: confirm that a pooled MI variance object is finite before it is used
# to generate manuscript-facing confidence intervals.




                                                            56
pooled_mi_vcov_check <- function(pooled) {
  if (is.null(pooled$variance)) stop("MIcombine object missing variance matrix.")
  V <- pooled$variance
  if (any(!is.finite(V))) stop("Non-finite pooled variance detected.")
  within <- attr(pooled, "within")
  between <- attr(pooled, "between")
  if (!is.null(within) && any(!is.finite(within))) stop("Non-finite within variance.")
  if (!is.null(between) && any(!is.finite(between))) stop("Non-finite between variance.")
  invisible(TRUE)
}

# helper: one project-wide publication theme so manuscript and supplement
# figures inherit the same typography and guide styling.
theme_pub <- function(base_size = 10, base_family = "", legend_position = "top") {
  ggplot2::theme_minimal(base_size = base_size, base_family = base_family) +
    ggplot2::theme(
      plot.title = ggplot2::element_text(face = "bold", hjust = 0, size = ggplot2::rel(1.05)),
      plot.subtitle = ggplot2::element_text(color = "grey20"),
      plot.caption = ggplot2::element_text(size = ggplot2::rel(0.85), color = "grey25", hjust = 0),
      axis.title = ggplot2::element_text(color = "grey10"),
      axis.text = ggplot2::element_text(color = "grey10"),
      panel.grid.minor = ggplot2::element_blank(),
      panel.grid.major.x = ggplot2::element_blank(),
      panel.grid.major.y = ggplot2::element_line(color = "grey85", linewidth = 0.25),
      axis.line = ggplot2::element_line(color = "grey25", linewidth = 0.25),
      axis.ticks = ggplot2::element_line(color = "grey25", linewidth = 0.25),
      legend.position = legend_position,
      legend.title = ggplot2::element_text(face = "bold"),
      legend.background = ggplot2::element_blank(),
      legend.key = ggplot2::element_blank(),
      strip.background = ggplot2::element_rect(fill = "grey95", color = "grey80", linewidth = 0.25),
      strip.text = ggplot2::element_text(face = "bold")
    )
}

# helper: save a diagnostic plot with explicit dimensions and a vector PDF path




                                                          57
# when appropriate, avoiding IDE-dependent defaults.
save_diag_plot <- function(p, file, width = 8, height = 6, units = "in", dpi = 300, bg = "white") {
  if (grepl("\\.pdf$", file, ignore.case = TRUE)) {
    ggplot2::ggsave(
      filename = file,
      plot = p,
      width = width,
      height = height,
      units = units,
      device = grDevices::cairo_pdf,
      bg = bg
    )
    return(invisible(file))
  }
  ggplot2::ggsave(
    filename = file,
    plot = p,
    width = width,
    height = height,
    units = units,
    dpi = dpi,
    bg = bg
  )
  invisible(file)
}

plot_registry_path <- results_path("plot_registry.csv")

# helper: load the registry of previously written plots for this render family.
read_plot_registry <- function() {
  if (file.exists(plot_registry_path)) {
    utils::read.csv(plot_registry_path, stringsAsFactors = FALSE)
  } else {
    data.frame(
      run_id = character(), run_ts = character(),
      plot_name = character(), fig_path = character(), md5 = character(),




                                                          58
            stringsAsFactors = FALSE
        )
    }
}

# helper: persist the plot registry after each update.
write_plot_registry <- function(df) {
  write_csv_safely(df, plot_registry_path, row_names = FALSE)
}

# helper: add one saved plot file to the registry, or log a duplicate if a
# chunk tries to emit the same named figure twice.
register_plot_file <- function(plot_name, file, run_id = diag_run_id, run_ts = diag_run_ts) {
  md5 <- as.character(tools::md5sum(file))
  reg <- read_plot_registry()
  dup_name <- nrow(reg) > 0 &&
    any(reg$run_id == run_id & reg$plot_name == plot_name, na.rm = TRUE)
  if (dup_name) {
    log_plot_drop(
      plot_name,
      "duplicate_figure",
      n_dropped = 1,
      n_before = NA_integer_,
      n_after = NA_integer_,
      stage = "plot_registry",
      extra = file
    )
    return(FALSE)
  }
  reg <- dplyr::bind_rows(
    reg,
    data.frame(run_id = run_id, run_ts = run_ts,
               plot_name = plot_name, fig_path = file, md5 = md5,
               stringsAsFactors = FALSE)
  )
  write_plot_registry(reg)




                                                          59
    TRUE
}

# helper: save a figure to disk and include it in the notebook only if that
# named figure has not already been emitted in the current render.
print_plot_once <- function(p, plot_name, width = 8, height = 6, dpi = 300) {
  file_png <- results_path("figs", paste0(plot_name, ".png"))
  file_pdf <- results_path("figs", paste0(plot_name, ".pdf"))
  file_preview <- results_path("figs", paste0(plot_name, "-report-preview.png"))
  save_diag_plot(p, file_png, width = width, height = height, dpi = dpi)
  save_diag_plot(p, file_pdf, width = width, height = height, dpi = dpi)
  # Use a lighter inline preview while keeping manuscript artifacts high resolution.
  save_diag_plot(p, file_preview, width = width, height = height, dpi = min(dpi, 96))
  if (register_plot_file(plot_name, file_png)) {
    if (isTRUE(VALIDATION_INLINE_ANALYSIS_PREVIEWS)) {
      mark_float_emitted()
      render_inline_graphic(file_preview)
    } else {
      invisible(file_preview)
    }
  } else {
    invisible(NULL)
  }
}

# helper: build the canonical on-disk path for any artifact stub/ext pair.
artifact_file_path <- function(stub, ext, subdir = NULL) {
  if (is.null(stub) || is.na(stub) || !nzchar(stub)) return(NA_character_)
  if (is.null(subdir) || is.na(subdir) || !nzchar(subdir)) {
    return(results_path(paste0(stub, ".", ext)))
  }
  results_path(subdir, paste0(stub, ".", ext))
}

# helper: copy one canonical artifact to one or more manuscript-facing alias
# names without changing the original analysis-oriented filename.




                                                          60
write_artifact_alias <- function(source_stub, alias_stub, exts,
                                 source_subdir = NULL,
                                 alias_subdir = source_subdir) {
  copied <- character(0)
  missing <- character(0)

    for (ext in exts) {
      src <- artifact_file_path(source_stub, ext, source_subdir)
      dst <- artifact_file_path(alias_stub, ext, alias_subdir)
      if (!file.exists(src)) {
        missing <- c(missing, src)
        next
      }
      if (fs::path_norm(src) != fs::path_norm(dst)) {
        fs::file_copy(src, dst, overwrite = TRUE)
      }
      copied <- c(copied, dst)
    }

    if (length(missing)) {
      stop(
        "Missing source artifact(s) for alias [",
        alias_stub,
        "]: ",
        paste(vapply(missing, pretty_path, character(1L)), collapse = ", ")
      )
    }
    invisible(copied)
}

# helper: mirror one saved figure into its manuscript alias path.
write_plot_alias <- function(plot_name, alias_name,
                             source_subdir = "figs",
                             alias_subdir = source_subdir) {
  write_artifact_alias(
    source_stub = plot_name,




                                                            61
        alias_stub = alias_name,
        exts = c("png", "pdf"),
        source_subdir = source_subdir,
        alias_subdir = alias_subdir
    )
}

# helper: mirror one saved table export into its manuscript alias path.
write_table_alias <- function(file_stub, alias_stub,
                              source_subdir = NULL,
                              alias_subdir = source_subdir) {
  write_artifact_alias(
    source_stub = file_stub,
    alias_stub = alias_stub,
    exts = c("csv", "pdf"),
    source_subdir = source_subdir,
    alias_subdir = alias_subdir
  )
}

# helper: force a figure to appear in the notebook even if a previous chunk
# already emitted the same named artifact.
print_plot_force <- function(p, plot_name, width = 8, height = 6, dpi = 300) {
  # Use this for key publication figures that must always appear in the PDF.
  file_png <- results_path("figs", paste0(plot_name, ".png"))
  file_pdf <- results_path("figs", paste0(plot_name, ".pdf"))
  file_preview <- results_path("figs", paste0(plot_name, "-report-preview.png"))
  save_diag_plot(p, file_png, width = width, height = height, dpi = dpi)
  save_diag_plot(p, file_pdf, width = width, height = height, dpi = dpi)
  save_diag_plot(p, file_preview, width = width, height = height, dpi = min(dpi, 96))
  register_plot_file(plot_name, file_png)
  if (isTRUE(VALIDATION_INLINE_ANALYSIS_PREVIEWS)) {
    mark_float_emitted()
    render_inline_graphic(file_preview)
  } else {
    invisible(file_preview)




                                                          62
    }
}

# helper: map a model-matrix term back to its parent feature so SHAP fallbacks
# and coefficient-based summaries stay interpretable.
term_to_parent_feature <- function(term, feature_names) {
  if (is.na(term) || identical(term, "(Intercept)")) return(NA_character_)
  clean_term <- gsub("`", "", term, fixed = TRUE)
  feature_names <- sort(unique(feature_names), decreasing = TRUE)
  hit <- feature_names[vapply(feature_names, function(v) grepl(v, clean_term, fixed = TRUE), logical(1))]
  if (length(hit)) return(hit[[1]])
  NA_character_
}

binary_covariate_labels <- c("copd", "asthma", "osa", "chf", "acute_nmd", "phtn", "ckd", "dm")

categorical_level_labels <- list(
  sex = c("0" = "Female", "1" = "Male", "2" = "Unknown/other", Male = "Male", Female = "Female"),
  race_ethnicity = c(
    "0" = "White", "1" = "Black", "2" = "Hispanic", "3" = "Asian",
    "4" = "AI/AN", "5" = "NH/PI", "6" = "Unknown"
  ),

    "2" = "Emergency", "3" = "Inpatient",
    Emergency = "Emergency", Inpatient = "Inpatient"
  )
)

pretty_covariate_value <- function(feature, value) {
  value <- trimws(as.character(value))
  if (identical(value, "<NA>")) return("missing indicator")
  if (feature %in% binary_covariate_labels && value %in% c("0", "1")) {
    return(ifelse(value == "1", "yes", "no"))
  }
  level_map <- categorical_level_labels[[feature]]
  if (!is.null(level_map) && value %in% names(level_map)) return(unname(level_map[[value]]))
  gsub("_", " ", value, fixed = TRUE)
}

display_covariate_label_one <- function(term) {




                                                          64
    term <- as.character(term)
    if (!nzchar(term) || is.na(term)) return(term)
    if (identical(term, "Overall (mean |SMD|)")) return(term)

    base_names <- sort(names(covariate_display_labels), decreasing = TRUE)
    for (feature in base_names) {
      feature_label <- unname(covariate_display_labels[[feature]])
      if (identical(term, feature)) return(feature_label)

        prefix_colon <- paste0(feature, ":")
        if (startsWith(term, prefix_colon)) {
          value <- substring(term, nchar(prefix_colon) + 1L)
          return(paste0(feature_label, ": ", pretty_covariate_value(feature, value)))
        }

        prefix_us <- paste0(feature, "_")
        if (startsWith(term, prefix_us)) {
          value <- substring(term, nchar(prefix_us) + 1L)
          return(paste0(feature_label, ": ", pretty_covariate_value(feature, value)))
        }

        if (startsWith(term, feature) && nchar(term) > nchar(feature)) {
          value <- substring(term, nchar(feature) + 1L)
          if (feature %in% names(categorical_level_labels) && nzchar(value)) {
            return(paste0(feature_label, ": ", pretty_covariate_value(feature, value)))
          }
        }
    }

    tools::toTitleCase(gsub("_", " ", term, fixed = TRUE))
}

display_covariate_label <- function(term) {
  vapply(term, display_covariate_label_one, character(1L), USE.NAMES = FALSE)
}




                                                              65
# helper: subsample rows reproducibly before SHAP-style calculations so
# diagnostics remain stable while keeping runtime bounded.
sample_rows_for_shap <- function(df, n_max = SHAP_SAMPLE_N, seed = 20251206L) {
  stopifnot(is.data.frame(df) || is.matrix(df))
  if (nrow(df) <= n_max) return(df)
  set.seed(seed)
  df[sample.int(nrow(df), size = n_max, replace = FALSE), , drop = FALSE]
}

# helper: refit the GBM weighting model with the exact options needed for the
# downstream feature-contribution diagnostics.
fit_weightit_gbm_for_shap <- function(formula_obj, data_obj) {
  args <- c(
    list(
       formula = formula_obj,
       data = data_obj,
       method = "gbm",
       estimand = "ATE",
       missing = "ind",
       include.obj = TRUE
    ),
    gbm_params
  )
  do.call(WeightIt::weightit, args)
}

# helper: compute the top GBM contribution features for one non-MI weighting
# model, with a deterministic fallback to relative influence if `fastshap` fails.
extract_nonmi_gbm_shap_top <- function(weight_obj, x_df, feature_names, group_label,
                                       nsim = SHAP_NSIM, top_n = SHAP_TOP_N) {
  if (!HAS_FASTSHAP) {
    return(
      data.frame(
        group = character(),
        feature = character(),
        mean_abs_shap = numeric(),




                                                          66
         stringsAsFactors = FALSE
     )
 )
}
stopifnot(inherits(weight_obj, "weightit"))
stopifnot(!is.null(weight_obj$obj))
gbm_obj <- weight_obj$obj
best_tree <- weight_obj$info$best.tree
if (is.null(best_tree) || !is.finite(best_tree) || best_tree <= 0) {
  best_tree <- gbm_obj$n.trees
}
x_use <- x_df[, feature_names, drop = FALSE]
char_cols <- names(x_use)[vapply(x_use, is.character, logical(1))]
if (length(char_cols)) {
  for (nm in char_cols) x_use[[nm]] <- factor(x_use[[nm]])
}
x_use <- droplevels_all(x_use)
x_background <- as.data.frame(
  sample_rows_for_shap(x_use, n_max = max(SHAP_SAMPLE_N, 5000L), seed = 20251206L)
)
x_shap <- as.data.frame(
  sample_rows_for_shap(x_use, n_max = SHAP_SAMPLE_N, seed = 20251206L)
)

pred_fun <- function(object, newdata) {
  new_use <- newdata[, object$var.names, drop = FALSE]
  as.numeric(stats::predict(object, newdata = new_use, n.trees = best_tree, type = "link"))
}

shap_mat <- tryCatch(
  fastshap::explain(
    object = gbm_obj,
    feature_names = feature_names,
    X = x_background,
    newdata = x_shap,
    pred_wrapper = pred_fun,




                                                        67
      nsim = nsim,
      adjust = FALSE
    ),
    error = function(e) {
       warning(
         "fastshap failed for ", group_label,
         "; falling back to GBM relative influence. ",
         conditionMessage(e),
         call. = FALSE
       )
       NULL
    }
)

if (is.null(shap_mat)) {
  gbm_imp <- tryCatch(
    gbm::summary.gbm(gbm_obj, plotit = FALSE),
    error = function(e) data.frame(var = character(), rel.inf = numeric(), stringsAsFactors = FALSE)
  )
  if (!nrow(gbm_imp)) {
    return(data.frame(group = character(), feature = character(), mean_abs_shap = numeric(), stringsAsFactors =
     ↪  FALSE))
  }
  return(
    gbm_imp |>
      dplyr::transmute(
        group = group_label,
        feature = as.character(var),
        mean_abs_shap = as.numeric(rel.inf) / 100
      ) |>
      dplyr::arrange(dplyr::desc(mean_abs_shap)) |>
      dplyr::slice_head(n = top_n)
  )
}

out <- data.frame(




                                                         68
      group = group_label,
      feature = colnames(shap_mat),
      mean_abs_shap = colMeans(abs(shap_mat), na.rm = TRUE),
      stringsAsFactors = FALSE
    ) |>
      dplyr::arrange(dplyr::desc(mean_abs_shap)) |>
      dplyr::slice_head(n = top_n)
    out
}

# helper: plot the top contribution features side by side for ABG and VBG so
# readers can compare the ordering models directly.
plot_shap_top10_two_panel <- function(df_top, title_text, x_label) {
  # Keep only top-N per cohort and force descending order inside each panel.
  df_top_plot <- df_top |>
    dplyr::group_by(group) |>
    dplyr::arrange(dplyr::desc(mean_abs_shap), .by_group = TRUE) |>
    dplyr::slice_head(n = SHAP_TOP_N) |>
    dplyr::mutate(
      feature_rank = dplyr::row_number(),
      feature_plot = paste0(sprintf("%02d", feature_rank), ". ", display_covariate_label(feature)),
      group = factor(group, levels = c("ABG", "VBG"))
    ) |>
    dplyr::ungroup()

    # Prefixing with rank makes ordering deterministic in each facet.
    ggplot2::ggplot(
      df_top_plot,
      ggplot2::aes(
        x = mean_abs_shap,
        y = stats::reorder(feature_plot, mean_abs_shap),
        fill = group
      )
    ) +
      ggplot2::geom_col(show.legend = FALSE) +
      ggplot2::facet_wrap(~group, scales = "free_y", ncol = 2) +




                                                               69
    ggplot2::labs(
      title = title_text,
      x = x_label,
      y = NULL
    ) +
    ggplot2::scale_y_discrete(labels = function(x) sub("^[0-9]+\\.\\s*", "", x)) +
    theme_pub(base_size = 10)
}

# helper: prepend a whole-cohort balance summary row so the love plot reports
# both term-level and overall balance shifts.
add_overall_love_rows <- function(df_in, overall_label = "Overall (mean |SMD|)") {
  # Summarize whole-plot balance for each cohort/sample pair and display it
  # as the top row so readers can quickly judge global balance shift.
  overall <- df_in |>
    dplyr::group_by(group, sample) |>
    dplyr::summarise(
      abs_smd = mean(abs_smd, na.rm = TRUE),
      abs_smd_raw = mean(abs_smd_raw, na.rm = TRUE),
      .groups = "drop"
    ) |>
    dplyr::mutate(term = overall_label)
  dplyr::bind_rows(overall, df_in)
}

# helper: apply one consistent love-plot layout across weighting diagnostics.
loveplot_style <- function(df_in, title_text) {
  # Build a classic love-plot view with:
  # 1) a segment from Raw -> IPW for each term, and
  # 2) explicit Raw/IPW points so both samples are always visible.
  # This avoids overplotting where one sample can hide the other.
  df_plot <- df_in |>
    dplyr::mutate(
      sample = factor(sample, levels = c("Raw", "IPW")),
      term_label = display_covariate_label(term),
      order_val = dplyr::if_else(




                                                          70
         term == "Overall (mean |SMD|)",
         max(abs_smd_raw, na.rm = TRUE) + 1,
         abs_smd_raw
     )
 )

df_wide <- df_plot |>
  dplyr::select(group, term, term_label, order_val, sample, abs_smd) |>
  tidyr::pivot_wider(names_from = sample, values_from = abs_smd)

ggplot2::ggplot(df_plot, ggplot2::aes(y = stats::reorder(term_label, order_val))) +
  ggplot2::geom_segment(
    data = df_wide,
    ggplot2::aes(
      x = Raw,
      xend = IPW,
      y = stats::reorder(term_label, order_val),
      yend = stats::reorder(term_label, order_val)
    ),
    inherit.aes = FALSE,
    color = "grey65",
    linewidth = 0.3,
    alpha = 0.8
  ) +
  ggplot2::geom_point(
    data = df_plot |> dplyr::filter(sample == "Raw"),
    ggplot2::aes(x = abs_smd, color = sample, shape = sample, size = term == "Overall (mean |SMD|)"),
    alpha = 0.95
  ) +
  ggplot2::geom_point(
    data = df_plot |> dplyr::filter(sample == "IPW"),
    ggplot2::aes(x = abs_smd, color = sample, shape = sample, size = term == "Overall (mean |SMD|)"),
    alpha = 0.95
  ) +
  ggplot2::geom_vline(xintercept = 0.10, linetype = "dashed", color = "grey30") +
  ggplot2::facet_wrap(~group, ncol = 2) +




                                                        71

CO2_RATE_OUTCOMES <- c("imv_proc", "niv_proc", "death_60d", "hypercap_resp_failure")
CO2_RATE_OUTCOME_LABELS <- c(
  imv_proc = "IMV",
  niv_proc = "NIV",
  death_60d = "Death (60d)",
  hypercap_resp_failure = "Hypercapnic RF"
)

# helper: bin CO2 values and compute observed outcome rates for exploratory
# shape checks before the fully modeled spline figures are built.
compute_co2_bin_rates <- function(df, co2_var, outcomes, outcome_labels,
                                  weight_var = NULL, q = c(0.02, 0.98),
                                  bin_width = 1, cohort_label = NA_character_) {
  assert_is_df(df, context = paste0("compute_co2_bin_rates(", co2_var, ")"))
  stopifnot(co2_var %in% names(df))
  stopifnot(all(outcomes %in% names(df)))
  stopifnot(length(q) == 2L, q[1] < q[2], is.finite(bin_width), bin_width > 0)
  if (!is.null(weight_var)) stopifnot(weight_var %in% names(df))

    co2_vals <- suppressWarnings(as.numeric(df[[co2_var]]))
    keep <- is.finite(co2_vals)
    if (!any(keep)) {
      return(tibble::tibble(




                                                              72
         cohort = character(), outcome = character(), outcome_label = character(),
         bin_lo = numeric(), bin_mid = numeric(), n_bin = integer(), rate = numeric()
    ))
}

q_lohi <- stats::quantile(co2_vals[keep], probs = q, na.rm = TRUE, names = FALSE)
keep <- keep & co2_vals >= q_lohi[1] & co2_vals <= q_lohi[2]
if (!is.null(weight_var)) {
  w <- suppressWarnings(as.numeric(df[[weight_var]]))
  keep <- keep & is.finite(w) & !is.na(w) & (w > 0)
}
if (!any(keep)) {
  return(tibble::tibble(
     cohort = character(), outcome = character(), outcome_label = character(),
     bin_lo = numeric(), bin_mid = numeric(), n_bin = integer(), rate = numeric()
  ))
}

d <- df[keep, , drop = FALSE]
d$co2_work <- co2_vals[keep]
d$bin_lo <- floor(d$co2_work / bin_width) * bin_width
d$bin_mid <- d$bin_lo + (bin_width / 2)
if (!is.null(weight_var)) {
  d$w_work <- suppressWarnings(as.numeric(d[[weight_var]]))
}

rate_rows <- lapply(outcomes, function(outcome_nm) {
  y <- suppressWarnings(as.numeric(d[[outcome_nm]] == 1))
  y[is.na(d[[outcome_nm]])] <- NA_real_
  tmp <- d[, c("bin_lo", "bin_mid"), drop = FALSE]
  tmp$y <- y
  if (!is.null(weight_var)) tmp$w <- d$w_work
  if (!is.null(weight_var)) {
    tmp <- tmp[is.finite(tmp$w) & !is.na(tmp$w) & !is.na(tmp$y), , drop = FALSE]
  } else {
    tmp <- tmp[!is.na(tmp$y), , drop = FALSE]




                                                             73
     }
     if (!nrow(tmp)) return(NULL)

     if (!is.null(weight_var)) {
       out <- tmp |>
         dplyr::group_by(bin_lo, bin_mid) |>
         dplyr::summarise(
           n_bin = dplyr::n(),
           rate = ifelse(sum(w, na.rm = TRUE) > 0, sum(y * w, na.rm = TRUE) / sum(w, na.rm = TRUE), NA_real_),
           .groups = "drop"
         )
     } else {
       out <- tmp |>
         dplyr::group_by(bin_lo, bin_mid) |>
         dplyr::summarise(
           n_bin = dplyr::n(),
           rate = mean(y, na.rm = TRUE),
           .groups = "drop"
         )
     }

      out |>
        dplyr::mutate(
          cohort = cohort_label,
          outcome = outcome_nm,
          outcome_label = dplyr::if_else(
             outcome_nm %in% names(outcome_labels),
             as.character(outcome_labels[[outcome_nm]]),
             outcome_nm
          )
        ) |>
        dplyr::select(cohort, outcome, outcome_label, bin_lo, bin_mid, n_bin, rate)
    })

    dplyr::bind_rows(rate_rows)
}

# helper: average binned outcome-rate diagnostics across imputations for a
# quick MI-aware visual check of the empirical shape.
pool_mi_bin_rates <- function(rate_df_all_imps) {
  assert_is_df(rate_df_all_imps, context = "pool_mi_bin_rates")
  stopifnot("imp" %in% names(rate_df_all_imps))
  rate_df_all_imps |>
    dplyr::group_by(cohort, outcome, outcome_label, bin_lo, bin_mid) |>
    dplyr::summarise(
      n_bin = mean(n_bin, na.rm = TRUE),
      rate = mean(rate, na.rm = TRUE),
      n_imp_contrib = sum(is.finite(rate)),
      .groups = "drop"
    )
}

                                                          75
