}

# helper: derive log-scale odds-ratio axis limits from the observed confidence
# intervals so related figures stay comparable without manual tuning.
compute_or_axis_spec <- function(df_list, lo_col = "conf.low", hi_col = "conf.high",
                                 min_pow = -6, max_pow = 6,
                                 default_limits = c(0.25, 16)) {
  if (inherits(df_list, "data.frame")) df_list <- list(df_list)
  if (!is.list(df_list)) df_list <- list(df_list)
  vals <- unlist(lapply(df_list, function(df) {
    assert_is_df(df, context = "compute_or_axis_spec")
    stopifnot(all(c(lo_col, hi_col) %in% names(df)))
    lo <- df[[lo_col]]
    hi <- df[[hi_col]]
    c(lo, hi)
  }), use.names = FALSE)
  vals <- vals[is.finite(vals) & vals > 0]
  if (!length(vals)) {
    lo_pow <- floor(log2(default_limits[1]))
    hi_pow <- ceiling(log2(default_limits[2]))
  } else {
    lo_pow <- floor(log2(min(vals)))
    hi_pow <- ceiling(log2(max(vals)))
  }
  lo_pow <- max(lo_pow, min_pow)
  hi_pow <- min(hi_pow, max_pow)
  if (lo_pow > hi_pow) hi_pow <- lo_pow
  limits <- 2^c(lo_pow, hi_pow)
  breaks <- 2^(lo_pow:hi_pow)
  list(limits = limits, breaks = breaks)
}




                                                          76
# helper: apply a consistent odds-ratio y-axis specification to spline plots.
or_axis_scale <- function(spec) {
  list(
    ggplot2::scale_y_log10(
       breaks = spec$breaks,
       labels = scales::number_format(accuracy = 0.01)
    ),
    ggplot2::coord_cartesian(ylim = spec$limits)
  )
}

# helper: derive probability-axis limits from the observed confidence bands so
# all probability panels share a stable visual range.
compute_prob_axis_spec <- function(df_list, lo_col = "p_LCL", hi_col = "p_UCL",
                                   floor = 0, ceiling = 1, pad = 0.02) {
  if (inherits(df_list, "data.frame")) df_list <- list(df_list)
  if (!is.list(df_list)) df_list <- list(df_list)
  vals <- unlist(lapply(df_list, function(df) {
    assert_is_df(df, context = "compute_prob_axis_spec")
    stopifnot(all(c(lo_col, hi_col) %in% names(df)))
    c(df[[lo_col]], df[[hi_col]])
  }), use.names = FALSE)
  vals <- vals[is.finite(vals)]
  if (!length(vals)) return(list(limits = c(floor, ceiling)))
  lo <- max(floor, min(vals) - pad)
  hi <- min(ceiling, max(vals) + pad)
  if (lo >= hi) {
    lo <- floor
    hi <- ceiling
  }
  list(limits = c(lo, hi))
}

# helper: apply a consistent probability y-axis specification to spline plots.
prob_axis_scale <- function(spec, accuracy = 1) {




                                                          77
    list(
      ggplot2::scale_y_continuous(labels = scales::percent_format(accuracy = accuracy)),
      ggplot2::coord_cartesian(ylim = spec$limits)
    )
}

KEY_RESULTS_OUTCOME_LEVELS <- c("IMV", "NIV", "Death (60d)", "Hypercapnic RF")
KEY_RESULTS_OUTCOME_MAP <- c(
  imv_proc = "IMV",
  niv_proc = "NIV",
  death_60d = "Death (60d)",
  hypercap_resp_failure = "Hypercapnic RF",
  IMV = "IMV",
  NIV = "NIV",
  Death60d = "Death (60d)",
  HCRF = "Hypercapnic RF",
  "Death (60d)" = "Death (60d)",
  "Hypercapnic RF" = "Hypercapnic RF"
)
KEY_RESULTS_GROUP_LEVELS <- c("ABG", "VBG")
KEY_RESULTS_GROUP_COLORS <- c("ABG" = "#F8766D", "VBG" = "#00BFC4")
KEY_RESULTS_GROUP_LINETYPES <- c("ABG" = "solid", "VBG" = "longdash")
KEY_RESULTS_FIG_WIDTH <- 10.5
KEY_RESULTS_FIG_HEIGHT <- 11

# helper: map raw outcome names from multiple upstream pipelines onto one
# ordered set of manuscript-facing labels for the spline key-results figures.
normalize_key_results_outcome <- function(x, context = "key-results") {
  out_chr <- as.character(x)
  mapped <- dplyr::recode(out_chr, !!!KEY_RESULTS_OUTCOME_MAP, .default = NA_character_)
  bad <- is.na(mapped)
  if (any(bad)) {
    stop(
      context, ": unmapped outcome labels: ",
      paste(sort(unique(out_chr[bad])), collapse = ", ")
    )




                                                            78
    }
    factor(mapped, levels = KEY_RESULTS_OUTCOME_LEVELS)
}

# helper: coerce cohort labels onto one stable ABG/VBG factor order.
normalize_key_results_group <- function(x, context = "key-results") {
  grp <- factor(as.character(x), levels = KEY_RESULTS_GROUP_LEVELS)
  if (any(is.na(grp))) {
    stop(
      context, ": unmapped group labels: ",
      paste(sort(unique(as.character(x)[is.na(grp)])), collapse = ", ")
    )
  }
  grp
}

# helper: standardize spline odds-ratio curve objects onto one common schema
# before they are combined into manuscript-facing figures.
normalize_key_results_or_df <- function(df, group = NULL, co2_col = "co2",
                                        outcome_col = "outcome",
                                        or_col = "OR", lcl_col = "LCL", ucl_col = "UCL",
                                        context = "key-results OR") {
  assert_is_df(df, context = context)
  stopifnot(outcome_col %in% names(df), or_col %in% names(df),
            lcl_col %in% names(df), ucl_col %in% names(df))
  if (!co2_col %in% names(df)) stop(context, ": missing CO2 column ", co2_col)
  group_vec <- if ("group" %in% names(df)) df$group else rep(group, nrow(df))
  if (is.null(group_vec)) stop(context, ": group must be supplied or present in data.")

    out <- tibble::tibble(
      group = normalize_key_results_group(group_vec, context = context),
      outcome = normalize_key_results_outcome(df[[outcome_col]], context = context),
      co2 = suppressWarnings(as.numeric(df[[co2_col]])),
      OR = suppressWarnings(as.numeric(df[[or_col]])),
      LCL = suppressWarnings(as.numeric(df[[lcl_col]])),
      UCL = suppressWarnings(as.numeric(df[[ucl_col]]))




                                                            79
    ) |>
      dplyr::filter(is.finite(co2), is.finite(OR), is.finite(LCL), is.finite(UCL),
                    OR > 0, LCL > 0, UCL > 0)

    if (!nrow(out)) stop(context, ": no finite OR rows after filtering.")
    out
}

# helper: standardize spline probability curves onto one common schema before
# the ABG/VBG overlays are assembled.
normalize_key_results_prob_df <- function(df, group = NULL, co2_col = "co2",
                                          outcome_col = "outcome",
                                          p_col = "p", lcl_col = "p_LCL", ucl_col = "p_UCL",
                                          context = "key-results probability") {
  assert_is_df(df, context = context)
  stopifnot(outcome_col %in% names(df), p_col %in% names(df),
            lcl_col %in% names(df), ucl_col %in% names(df))
  if (!co2_col %in% names(df)) stop(context, ": missing CO2 column ", co2_col)
  group_vec <- if ("group" %in% names(df)) df$group else rep(group, nrow(df))
  if (is.null(group_vec)) stop(context, ": group must be supplied or present in data.")

    out <- tibble::tibble(
      group = normalize_key_results_group(group_vec, context = context),
      outcome = normalize_key_results_outcome(df[[outcome_col]], context = context),
      co2 = suppressWarnings(as.numeric(df[[co2_col]])),
      p = suppressWarnings(as.numeric(df[[p_col]])),
      p_LCL = suppressWarnings(as.numeric(df[[lcl_col]])),
      p_UCL = suppressWarnings(as.numeric(df[[ucl_col]]))
    ) |>
      dplyr::filter(
         is.finite(co2), is.finite(p), is.finite(p_LCL), is.finite(p_UCL),
         dplyr::between(p, 0, 1), dplyr::between(p_LCL, 0, 1), dplyr::between(p_UCL, 0, 1)
      )

    if (!nrow(out)) stop(context, ": no finite probability rows after filtering.")
    out




                                                            80
}

# helper: stack one named list of odds-ratio curves into a single tidy frame
# keyed by outcome for the combined spline figure.
bind_key_results_or_curves <- function(curve_list, group, co2_col, context = "key-results OR") {
  stopifnot(is.list(curve_list), length(curve_list) > 0L, !is.null(names(curve_list)))
  dplyr::bind_rows(lapply(names(curve_list), function(outcome_nm) {
    curve_df <- curve_list[[outcome_nm]]
    curve_df$outcome <- outcome_nm
    normalize_key_results_or_df(
      curve_df,
      group = group,
      co2_col = co2_col,
      context = context
    )
  }))
}

# helper: stack one named list of predicted-probability curves into a single
# tidy frame keyed by outcome for the combined spline figure.
bind_key_results_prob_curves <- function(curve_list, group, co2_col,
                                         context = "key-results probability") {
  stopifnot(is.list(curve_list), length(curve_list) > 0L, !is.null(names(curve_list)))
  dplyr::bind_rows(lapply(names(curve_list), function(outcome_nm) {
    curve_df <- curve_list[[outcome_nm]]
    curve_df$outcome <- outcome_nm
    normalize_key_results_prob_df(
      curve_df,
      group = group,
      co2_col = co2_col,
      context = context
    )
  }))
}

# helper: assemble the full spline key-results figure with shared legend and
# caption once both columns have been built.
build_key_results_figure <- function(or_df, prob_df, figure_title, figure_caption) {
  or_plot <- build_key_results_or_column(or_df, show_row_labels = TRUE)
  prob_plot <- build_key_results_prob_column(prob_df, show_row_labels = FALSE)
  annotation_args <- list(title = figure_title)
  if (!is.null(figure_caption) && nzchar(figure_caption)) {
    annotation_args$caption <- figure_caption
  }
  (or_plot | prob_plot) +
    patchwork::plot_layout(guides = "collect", widths = c(1, 1)) +
    do.call(
      patchwork::plot_annotation,
      c(
        annotation_args,
        list(theme = ggplot2::theme(
           plot.title = ggplot2::element_text(face = "bold", hjust = 0.5),
           plot.caption = ggplot2::element_text(hjust = 0)
        ))
      )
    ) &




                                                          84
    ggplot2::theme(legend.position = "top")
}

# helper: apply the shared odds-ratio axis specification to horizontal forest
# plots rather than vertical spline plots.
or_axis_scale_x <- function(spec) {
  list(
    ggplot2::scale_x_log10(
       breaks = spec$breaks,
       labels = scales::number_format(accuracy = 0.01)
    ),
    ggplot2::coord_cartesian(xlim = spec$limits)
  )
}

# helper: apply the shared probability axis specification to horizontal forest
# plots rather than vertical spline plots.
prob_axis_scale_x <- function(spec, accuracy = 1) {
  list(
    ggplot2::scale_x_continuous(labels = scales::percent_format(accuracy = accuracy)),
    ggplot2::coord_cartesian(xlim = spec$limits)
  )
}

  "Crude",
  "Adjusted",
  "Imputed",
  "Weighted and adjusted",
  "GBM-weighted"
)

                                                          85

# helper: coerce analysis-track labels onto one stable order for the
# categorical key-results tables and figures.
normalize_cat3_key_results_method <- function(x, context = "categorical key-results") {
  method <- factor(as.character(x), levels = CAT3_KEY_RESULTS_METHOD_LEVELS)
  if (any(is.na(method))) {
    stop(
      context, ": unmapped methods: ",
      paste(sort(unique(as.character(x)[is.na(method)])), collapse = ", ")
    )
  }
  method
}

# helper: coerce low/high contrasts onto one stable manuscript order.
normalize_cat3_key_results_contrast <- function(x, context = "categorical key-results") {
  contrast <- factor(as.character(x), levels = CAT3_KEY_RESULTS_CONTRAST_LEVELS)
  if (any(is.na(contrast))) {
    stop(
      context, ": unmapped contrasts: ",
      paste(sort(unique(as.character(x)[is.na(contrast)])), collapse = ", ")
    )
  }
  contrast
}

# helper: coerce low/normal/high category labels onto one stable order.
normalize_cat3_key_results_category <- function(x, context = "categorical key-results") {
  category <- factor(as.character(x), levels = CAT3_KEY_RESULTS_CATEGORY_LEVELS)
  if (any(is.na(category))) {
    stop(
      context, ": unmapped categories: ",
      paste(sort(unique(as.character(x)[is.na(category)])), collapse = ", ")
    )
  }




                                                          86
    category
}

# helper: translate raw model-term names into the displayed categorical
# contrasts used in tables and forest plots.
map_cat3_term_contrast <- function(term) {
  term_chr <- gsub("`", "", as.character(term))
  exposure <- dplyr::case_when(
    grepl("^pco2_cat_abg", term_chr) ~ sub("^pco2_cat_abg", "", term_chr),
    grepl("^pco2_cat_vbg", term_chr) ~ sub("^pco2_cat_vbg", "", term_chr),
    grepl("^co2_cat", term_chr) ~ sub("^co2_cat", "", term_chr),
    TRUE ~ term_chr
  )
  dplyr::case_when(
    grepl("Low$", exposure) ~ "Low vs normal",
    grepl("High$", exposure) ~ "High vs normal",
    TRUE ~ NA_character_
  )
}

# helper: reduce a fitted categorical model to the coefficient/vcov pieces
# needed for reusable predicted-probability calculations.
compact_cat3_fit <- function(fit_obj, context = "categorical probability prediction") {
  if (inherits(fit_obj, "glm") || inherits(fit_obj, "svyglm")) {
    return(list(coef = stats::coef(fit_obj), vcov = stats::vcov(fit_obj)))
  }
  if (is.list(fit_obj) && !is.null(fit_obj$coef) && !is.null(fit_obj$vcov)) {
    return(fit_obj)
  }
  stop(context, ": unsupported fit object class: ", paste(class(fit_obj), collapse = ", "))
}

# helper: standardize categorical odds-ratio outputs from the different model
# tracks into one shared export/plot schema.
normalize_cat3_key_results_or_df <- function(df, method,
                                             outcome_col = "outcome",




                                                          87
                                              group_col = "group",
                                              term_col = "term",
                                              or_col = "OR",
                                              lcl_col = "LCL",
                                              ucl_col = "UCL",
                                              context = "categorical key-results OR") {
    assert_is_df(df, context = context)
    assert_has_cols(df, c(outcome_col, group_col, term_col, or_col, lcl_col, ucl_col), context = context)

    out <- tibble::tibble(
      method = normalize_cat3_key_results_method(method, context = context),
      group = normalize_key_results_group(df[[group_col]], context = context),
      outcome = normalize_key_results_outcome(df[[outcome_col]], context = context),
      contrast = normalize_cat3_key_results_contrast(
         map_cat3_term_contrast(df[[term_col]]),
         context = context
      ),
      OR = suppressWarnings(as.numeric(df[[or_col]])),
      LCL = suppressWarnings(as.numeric(df[[lcl_col]])),
      UCL = suppressWarnings(as.numeric(df[[ucl_col]]))
    ) |>
      dplyr::filter(is.finite(OR), is.finite(LCL), is.finite(UCL), OR > 0, LCL > 0, UCL > 0)

    if (!nrow(out)) stop(context, ": no finite OR rows after filtering.")
    out
}

# helper: format one odds ratio and confidence interval for compact table
# display without repeating string-construction logic downstream.
format_or_ci_export <- function(estimate, lcl, ucl, digits = 2) {
  sprintf(
    paste0("%.", digits, "f (%.", digits, "f, %.", digits, "f)"),
    estimate, lcl, ucl
  )
}

# helper: turn raw three-level categorical model output into a manuscript-ready
# supplement table with harmonized labels and CI formatting.
build_supplement_threelevel_table <- function(df, method,




                                                            89
                                                outcome_col = "outcome",
                                                group_col = "group",
                                                term_col = "term",
                                                or_col = "estimate",
                                                lcl_col = "conf.low",
                                                ucl_col = "conf.high",
                                                context = "supplement three-level table") {
    normalize_cat3_key_results_or_df(
      df,
      method = method,
      outcome_col = outcome_col,
      group_col = group_col,
      term_col = term_col,
      or_col = or_col,
      lcl_col = lcl_col,
      ucl_col = ucl_col,
      context = context
    ) |>
      dplyr::transmute(
         group = as.character(group),
         outcome = as.character(outcome),
         contrast = as.character(contrast),
         `OR (95% CI)` = format_or_ci_export(OR, LCL, UCL)
      ) |>
      dplyr::arrange(
         factor(group, levels = KEY_RESULTS_GROUP_LEVELS),
         factor(outcome, levels = KEY_RESULTS_OUTCOME_LEVELS),
         factor(contrast, levels = CAT3_KEY_RESULTS_CONTRAST_LEVELS)
      )
}

# helper: decode categorical exposure terms into plotted low/high CO2
# categories for the legacy OR plots.
map_or_exposure <- function(df, plot_name) {
  assert_is_df(df, context = paste0("map_or_exposure(", plot_name, ")"))
  stopifnot(nrow(df) > 0L)
  stopifnot("term" %in% names(df))
  df$term <- gsub("`", "", df$term)
  df$exposure <- dplyr::case_when(
    grepl("^pco2_cat_abg", df$term) ~ gsub("^pco2_cat_abg", "", df$term),
    grepl("^pco2_cat_vbg", df$term) ~ gsub("^pco2_cat_vbg", "", df$term),
    grepl("^co2_cat", df$term)      ~ gsub("^co2_cat", "", df$term),
    TRUE                            ~ NA_character_
  )
  bad <- is.na(df$exposure) | !df$exposure %in% CO2_CAT_CONTRAST_LEVELS
  if (any(bad)) {
    out_path <- results_path("or_term_mapping_failures.csv")
    bad_terms <- data.frame(term = df$term[bad], group = df$group[bad],
                            plot_name = plot_name, stringsAsFactors = FALSE)
    write_csv_safely(bad_terms, out_path, row_names = FALSE)
    stop(paste0("Unmapped OR terms in ", plot_name, ". See ", out_path))
  }




                                                            94
    df$exposure <- factor(df$exposure, levels = CO2_CAT_CONTRAST_LEVELS)
    df
}

# helper: prepare one tidy data frame for the legacy categorical OR figures,
# including row-drop logging when required.
build_or_plot_df <- function(df, plot_name, expected_exposure_levels) {
  df <- tibble::as_tibble(df)
  req_cols <- c("outcome", "group", "estimate", "conf.low", "conf.high")
  req_cols <- c(req_cols, "exposure")
  assert_has_cols(df, unique(req_cols), context = paste0("build_or_plot_df(", plot_name, ")"))
  df <- dplyr::mutate(
    df,
    estimate = as.numeric(estimate),
    conf.low = as.numeric(conf.low),
    conf.high = as.numeric(conf.high)
  )
  if (safe_nrow(df, paste0("build_or_plot_df(", plot_name, ")")) == 0L) {
    stop("Empty OR plot data in ", plot_name)
  }
  drop <- !is.finite(df$estimate) | !is.finite(df$conf.low) | !is.finite(df$conf.high)
  if (any(drop)) {
    log_plot_drop(plot_name, "non-finite estimate/conf", sum(drop),
                  n_before = nrow(df), n_after = nrow(df) - sum(drop),
                  stage = "build_or_plot_df")
    df <- df[!drop, , drop = FALSE]
  }
  drop_pos <- (df$estimate <= 0) | (df$conf.low <= 0) | (df$conf.high <= 0)
  if (any(drop_pos, na.rm = TRUE)) {
    log_plot_drop(plot_name, "non-positive estimate/conf", sum(drop_pos, na.rm = TRUE),
                  n_before = nrow(df), n_after = nrow(df) - sum(drop_pos, na.rm = TRUE),
                  stage = "build_or_plot_df")
    df <- df[!drop_pos, , drop = FALSE]
  }
  exp_drop <- is.na(df$exposure) | trimws(as.character(df$exposure)) == ""
  if (any(exp_drop)) {




                                                            95
     log_plot_drop(plot_name, "missing exposure level", sum(exp_drop),
                   n_before = nrow(df), n_after = nrow(df) - sum(exp_drop),
                   stage = "build_or_plot_df")
     df <- df[!exp_drop, , drop = FALSE]
    }
    df$exposure <- factor(df$exposure, levels = expected_exposure_levels)
    bad_exp <- is.na(df$exposure)
    if (any(bad_exp)) {
      bad_df <- df[bad_exp, , drop = FALSE]
      bad_path <- results_path(paste0("or_unmapped_terms_", plot_name, ".csv"))
      write_csv_safely(bad_df, bad_path, row_names = FALSE)
      stop(paste0("Unmapped exposure terms in ", plot_name, ". See ", bad_path))
    }
    missing_levels <- setdiff(expected_exposure_levels, unique(as.character(df$exposure)))
    if (length(missing_levels)) {
      stop(paste0("Missing exposure levels in ", plot_name, ": ", paste(missing_levels, collapse = ", ")))
    }
    if (nrow(df) == 0L) {
      msg <- paste0("OR plot data empty after filtering in ", plot_name)
      stop(msg)
    }
    df
}

# helper: turn free-text model names into filesystem-safe stubs for diagram
# export without changing the displayed label.
.make_safe_name <- function(x) {



                                                          99
    x <- gsub("[^A-Za-z0-9]+", "-", x)
    x <- gsub("(^-|-$)", "", x)
    tolower(x)
}

# helper: recover the response and predictor names from a model formula before
# drawing a simple DAG representation.
.extract_model_vars <- function(fml) {
  tt <- stats::terms(fml)
  response <- all.vars(stats::update(fml, . ~ 1))
  response <- if (length(response)) response[1] else NA_character_
  term_labels <- attr(tt, "term.labels")
  preds <- unique(unlist(lapply(term_labels, function(t) {
    all.vars(stats::as.formula(paste("~", t)))
  })))
  preds <- setdiff(preds, response)
  list(response = response, preds = preds)
}

# helper: build a minimal DAG from a model formula so the notebook can export
# lightweight model-structure diagrams alongside the analysis.
.build_model_dag <- function(fml) {
  vars <- .extract_model_vars(fml)
  if (is.na(vars$response) || length(vars$preds) == 0L) {
    stop("Model diagram: formula has no response or predictors: ", deparse(fml))
  }
  edges <- paste(sprintf("%s -> %s", vars$preds, vars$response), collapse = "\n ")
  dagitty::dagitty(sprintf("dag { %s }", edges))
}

# helper: render and save one model diagram with a size that adapts to the
# number of variables in the formula.
save_model_diagram <- function(name, fml, width = NULL, height = NULL) {
  dag <- .build_model_dag(fml)

    vars <- .extract_model_vars(fml)




                                                         100
n_pred <- length(vars$preds)
n_nodes <- n_pred + 1L

label_size <- if (n_pred >= 35) 1.4 else if (n_pred >= 25) 1.8 else if (n_pred >= 15) 2.2 else 2.8
point_size <- if (n_pred >= 25) 2.0 else if (n_pred >= 15) 2.5 else 3.0

base_width <- if (is.null(width)) 8 else width
base_height <- if (is.null(height)) 6 else height
width <- max(base_width, min(24, 0.4 * n_nodes + 4))
height <- max(base_height, min(16, 0.25 * n_nodes + 4))

layout <- if (n_pred >= 8) "sugiyama" else "nicely"
dag_data <- ggdag::tidy_dagitty(dag, layout = layout)$data

p <- ggplot2::ggplot(
  dag_data,
  ggplot2::aes(x = x, y = y, xend = xend, yend = yend)
) +
  ggdag::geom_dag_edges() +
  ggdag::geom_dag_point(size = point_size) +
  ggdag::geom_dag_text_repel(
    ggplot2::aes(label = name),
    size = label_size,
    max.overlaps = Inf
  ) +
  ggplot2::scale_x_continuous(expand = ggplot2::expansion(mult = 0.15)) +
  ggplot2::scale_y_continuous(expand = ggplot2::expansion(mult = 0.15)) +
  ggplot2::theme_void() +
  ggplot2::labs(title = name) +
  ggplot2::theme(
    plot.title = ggplot2::element_text(size = 10, hjust = 0.5),
    plot.margin = ggplot2::margin(10, 10, 10, 10)
  )

file <- fs::path(model_diagram_dir, paste0(.make_safe_name(name), ".png"))
save_diag_plot(file = file, p = p, width = width, height = height, dpi = 300)




                                                          101
    if (isTRUE(show_model_diagrams)) print(p)
    file
}

model_diagrams <- list()
# helper: save one model diagram and register its path for later reuse.
register_model_diagram <- function(name, fml, width = 8, height = 6) {
  file <- save_model_diagram(name, fml, width = width, height = height)
  model_diagrams[[name]] <<- file
  invisible(file)
}

# helper: batch-register a named list of model formulas as diagram exports.
register_model_diagrams <- function(forms, width = 8, height = 6) {
  purrr::iwalk(forms, function(fml, nm) {
    register_model_diagram(nm, fml, width = width, height = height)
  })
}

# Make gt tables robust in PDF: full width, caption, small font
gt_pdf <- function(x, title = NULL, subtitle = NULL) {
  out <- x |>
    gt::tab_options(
      table.width              = gt::pct(100),
      table.align              = "left",
      table.font.size          = gt::px(9),
      data_row.padding         = gt::px(1),
      column_labels.font.size = gt::px(9),
      heading.title.font.size = gt::px(10),
      heading.subtitle.font.size = gt::px(9)
    ) |>
    gt::opt_align_table_header(align = "left")
  if (!is.null(title))    out <- out |> gt::tab_caption(title)
  if (!is.null(subtitle)) out <- out |> gt::tab_source_note(subtitle)
  out
}

# Sanitize variable labels for PDF/TOC safety (avoid Unicode subscripts)
sanitize_label_text <- function(x) {
  if (is.null(x)) return(x)



                                                                           104
  x <- gsub("\u2080", "0", x, fixed = TRUE)
  x <- gsub("\u2081", "1", x, fixed = TRUE)
  x <- gsub("\u2082", "2", x, fixed = TRUE)
  x <- gsub("\u2083", "3", x, fixed = TRUE)
  x <- gsub("\u2084", "4", x, fixed = TRUE)
  x <- gsub("\u2085", "5", x, fixed = TRUE)
  x <- gsub("\u2086", "6", x, fixed = TRUE)
  x <- gsub("\u2087", "7", x, fixed = TRUE)
  x <- gsub("\u2088", "8", x, fixed = TRUE)
  x <- gsub("\u2089", "9", x, fixed = TRUE)
  x
}
# helper: replace Unicode subscripts in variable labels before PDF rendering so
# gt/kable output stays stable across LaTeX engines.
sanitize_var_labels <- function(df) {
  labs <- labelled::var_label(df)
  labs <- lapply(labs, sanitize_label_text)
  labelled::var_label(df) <- labs
  df
}
stata_data <- sanitize_var_labels(stata_data)

  list(var_labels = var_labels, value_labels = value_labels),
  results_path("stata_labels.rds")
)

# helper: coerce mixed binary encodings onto an explicit {0,1,NA} integer scale
# before factors and models are built.
to01 <- function(x) {
  # Convert mixed encodings (logical/factor/character/numeric labels)
  # to a strict integer indicator in {0, 1, NA}.
  if (inherits(x, "haven_labelled")) x <- unclass(x)
  if (is.logical(x)) return(as.integer(x))
  if (is.factor(x)) x <- as.character(x)
  out <- rep(NA_integer_, length(x))
  xs <- suppressWarnings(as.numeric(x))
  is_num <- !is.na(xs)
  out[is_num & xs %in% c(0, 1)] <- as.integer(xs[is_num & xs %in% c(0, 1)])
  if (any(!is_num)) {
    idx <- which(!is_num)
    s <- trimws(tolower(as.character(x[idx])))
    # Explicit text mappings used in this project.



                                                         108
     # We support both binary labels and testing-status labels.
     out[idx[s %in% c("0","no","false","female","f")]] <- 0L
     out[idx[s %in% c("1","yes","true","male","m")]]   <- 1L
     out[idx[s %in% c("no test", "not tested", "untested", "control", "absent")]] <- 0L
     out[idx[s %in% c("test", "tested", "treated", "present")]] <- 1L
    }
    out
}

# helper: harmonize encounter-type source values onto the canonical
# Emergency/Inpatient factor used throughout the notebook.
normalize_encounter_type <- function(x) {
  # Harmonize encounter type across numeric codes and free-text variants.
  # Output is the canonical factor used in all models/tables:
  # Emergency / Inpatient.
  s_chr <- trimws(tolower(as.character(x)))
  num_from_text <- suppressWarnings(as.numeric(gsub("[^0-9]+", "", s_chr)))
  lab <- rep(NA_character_, length(s_chr))
  lab[!is.na(num_from_text) & num_from_text == 2] <- "Emergency"
  lab[!is.na(num_from_text) & num_from_text == 3] <- "Inpatient"
  is_na <- is.na(lab)
  is_em <- grepl("\\bemerg(?:ency)?\\b", s_chr) |
           grepl("(^|[^a-z])ed([^a-z]|$)", s_chr) |
           grepl("\\ba&e\\b", s_chr) |
           grepl("\\bemergency\\s+dept\\b", s_chr)
  is_ip <- grepl("\\binpatient\\b", s_chr) |
           grepl("\\binpt\\b",     s_chr) |
           grepl("\\binpat\\b",    s_chr) |
           grepl("(^|[^a-z])ip([^a-z]|$)", s_chr)
  lab[is_na & is_em] <- "Emergency"
  lab[is_na & is_ip] <- "Inpatient"
  factor(lab, levels = c("Emergency", "Inpatient"))
}

# helper: robustly coerce labelled/factor/character inputs to numeric while
# stripping non-numeric symbols that appear in imported EHR fields.




                                                          109
coerce_num <- function(x) {
  # Robust numeric coercion for labelled/factor/character inputs.
  # Non-numeric symbols are stripped to avoid parse failures.
  if (inherits(x, "haven_labelled")) x <- unclass(x)
  if (is.factor(x)) x <- as.character(x)
  if (is.character(x)) x <- gsub("[^0-9.+-]", "", x)
  suppressWarnings(as.numeric(x))
}

# Reference factor levels are captured once from source data.
# We then reuse them to keep category ordering stable across stages.
levels_ref <- list(
  sex = c("Female", "Male"),
  race_ethnicity = levels(factor(stata_data$race_ethnicity)),
  location = levels(factor(stata_data$location)),
  encounter_type = levels(normalize_encounter_type(stata_data$encounter_type))
)

# helper: perform the one-time global type normalization that the rest of the
# notebook assumes, while preserving row count.
normalize_types <- function(df, levels_ref = NULL) {
  # 1) Drop variables intentionally excluded due to extreme missingness.
  df <- df[, setdiff(names(df), drop_vars_ultra_missing), drop = FALSE]

  # 2) Coerce core numeric/lab/gas variables to numeric once.
  num_vars <- intersect(c(numeric_vars, co2_vars), names(df))
  for (nm in num_vars) df[[nm]] <- coerce_num(df[[nm]])

  # 3) Force sex to the canonical binary factor.
  stopifnot("sex" %in% names(df))
  df$sex <- factor(to01(df$sex), levels = c(0L, 1L), labels = c("Female", "Male"))

  # 4) Normalize encounter type into Emergency/Inpatient.
  stopifnot("encounter_type" %in% names(df))
  df$encounter_type <- normalize_encounter_type(df$encounter_type)




                                                         110
    # 5) Convert remaining categorical predictors to factors.
    # If reference levels are supplied, enforce them for consistency.
    for (nm in setdiff(cat_vars, c("sex", "encounter_type"))) {
      stopifnot(nm %in% names(df))
      if (!is.null(levels_ref) && !is.null(levels_ref[[nm]])) {
        df[[nm]] <- factor(df[[nm]], levels = levels_ref[[nm]])
      } else {
        df[[nm]] <- factor(df[[nm]])
      }
    }

    # 6) Ensure treatment indicators are explicit 0/1 integers.
    stopifnot(all(c("has_abg", "has_vbg") %in% names(df)))
    df$has_abg <- to01(df$has_abg)
    df$has_vbg <- to01(df$has_vbg)

    # Keep row count unchanged: this function is for type normalization only.
    df
}

# Reference profile for conditional curves
stopifnot(all(adj_core %in% names(subset_data)))

# helper: choose the modal observed level/value for each adjustment variable so
# predicted curves are conditioned on a plausible reference profile.
mode_level <- function(x) {




                                                         112
    if (is.factor(x)) {
      tab <- table(x, useNA = "no")
      if (!length(tab)) return(factor(NA, levels = levels(x)))
      lev <- names(tab)[which.max(tab)]
      return(factor(lev, levels = levels(x)))
    }
    if (is.character(x)) {
      tab <- table(x, useNA = "no")
      if (!length(tab)) return(NA_character_)
      return(names(tab)[which.max(tab)])
    }
    stats::median(as.numeric(x), na.rm = TRUE)
}

# helper: build a single-row reference profile for conditional predictions by
# taking the median or modal value of each adjustment covariate.
make_ref_profile <- function(data, adj_vars) {
  # Build a representative covariate profile for conditional predictions:
  # medians for numeric variables and most common levels for categorical ones.
  # Spline plots then vary only CO2 while all other predictors stay fixed.
  out <- lapply(adj_vars, function(v) mode_level(data[[v]]))
  names(out) <- adj_vars
  as.data.frame(out, stringsAsFactors = FALSE)
}

# helper: expand a reference profile over a grid of CO2 values for predicted
# probability calculations.
make_co2_grid <- function(co2_var, co2_vals, ref_df) {
  # Repeat the same reference profile across a sequence of CO2 values so the
  # plotted curve isolates the modeled effect of CO2 itself.
  grid <- data.frame(co2_vals)
  names(grid) <- co2_var
  stopifnot(!is.null(ref_df))
  stopifnot(nrow(ref_df) > 0L)
  ref_rep <- ref_df[rep(1L, nrow(grid)), , drop = FALSE]
  grid <- cbind(grid, ref_rep)




                                                           113
    grid
}

# helper: expand a reference profile over both a prediction grid and a single
# reference CO2 value for odds-ratio curve calculations.
make_co2_grid_ref <- function(co2_var, co2_vals, ref_df, co2_ref) {
  # The reference grid index defines where the odds-ratio curve is centered,
  # so OR = 1 at the chosen blood-gas-specific reference CO2 value.
  grid_vals <- c(co2_vals, co2_ref)
  grid_vals <- grid_vals[is.finite(grid_vals)]
  grid_vals <- sort(unique(as.numeric(grid_vals)))
  if (length(grid_vals) < 2) {
    fallback_center <- NA_real_
    if (is.finite(co2_ref)) {
      fallback_center <- co2_ref
    } else if (length(co2_vals) && is.finite(co2_vals[1])) {
      fallback_center <- co2_vals[1]
    }
    if (is.finite(fallback_center)) {
      grid_vals <- sort(unique(c(fallback_center - 1, fallback_center, fallback_center + 1)))
      grid_vals <- grid_vals[is.finite(grid_vals)]
    }
  }
  if (length(grid_vals) < 2) stop("CO2 grid is too small for ", co2_var, ".")
  grid <- make_co2_grid(co2_var, grid_vals, ref_df)
  ref_val <- if (is.finite(co2_ref)) co2_ref else stats::median(grid[[co2_var]], na.rm = TRUE)
  ref_idx <- match(ref_val, grid[[co2_var]])
  if (is.na(ref_idx)) {
    ref_idx <- which.min(abs(grid[[co2_var]] - ref_val))
  }
  if (any(diff(grid[[co2_var]]) <= 0)) {
    stop("CO2 grid is not strictly increasing for ", co2_var, ".")
  }
  list(grid = grid, ref_idx = ref_idx, co2_ref = grid[[co2_var]][ref_idx])
}




                                                         114
# helper: convert one fitted spline model into a pointwise odds-ratio curve
# relative to the chosen CO2 reference value.
predict_or_curve_from_fit <- function(fit, grid_df, ref_idx, co2_var) {
  # Build a model matrix consistent with the fitted model (handles factor levels)
  tt <- stats::delete.response(stats::terms(fit))
  xlev <- stats::.getXlevels(tt, stats::model.frame(fit))
  mf_new <- stats::model.frame(tt, grid_df, na.action = stats::na.pass, xlev = xlev)
  mm <- stats::model.matrix(tt, mf_new)
  beta <- stats::coef(fit)
  V <- stats::vcov(fit)

  # Align model matrix columns to coefficient names (fill missing with 0, drop extras)
  bn <- names(beta)
  if (is.null(bn) || any(!nzchar(bn))) {
    if (length(beta) == ncol(mm)) {
      bn <- colnames(mm)
      names(beta) <- bn
    } else {
      stop("predict_or_curve_from_fit: coefficient names missing and dimensions do not match.")
    }
  }
  if (!all(bn %in% colnames(mm))) {
    missing_cols <- setdiff(bn, colnames(mm))
    if (length(missing_cols)) {
      mm <- cbind(mm, matrix(0, nrow = nrow(mm), ncol = length(missing_cols),
                             dimnames = list(NULL, missing_cols)))
    }
  }
  mm <- mm[, bn, drop = FALSE]
  stopifnot(ncol(mm) == length(beta))

  eta <- as.numeric(mm %*% beta)
  mmV <- mm %*% V
  var_eta <- pmax(rowSums(mmV * mm), 0)
  se_eta <- sqrt(var_eta)




                                                         115
    mm_ref <- mm[ref_idx, , drop = FALSE]
    eta_ref <- eta[ref_idx]
    var_ref <- as.numeric(mm_ref %*% V %*% t(mm_ref))
    cov_ref <- as.numeric(mmV %*% t(mm_ref))

    logOR <- eta - eta_ref
    var_logOR <- var_eta + var_ref - 2 * cov_ref
    var_logOR <- pmax(var_logOR, 0)
    logOR[ref_idx] <- 0
    var_logOR[ref_idx] <- 0
    se <- sqrt(var_logOR)

    data.frame(
      grid_df,
      eta = eta,
      var_eta = var_eta,
      SE_eta = se_eta,
      p = plogis(eta),
      p_LCL = plogis(eta - 1.96 * se_eta),
      p_UCL = plogis(eta + 1.96 * se_eta),
      logOR = logOR,
      SE_logOR = se,
      var_logOR = var_logOR,
      OR = exp(logOR),
      LCL = exp(logOR - 1.96 * se),
      UCL = exp(logOR + 1.96 * se),
      co2_ref = grid_df[[co2_var]][ref_idx],
      ref_idx = ref_idx,
      row.names = NULL
    )
}

# Purpose: detect machine-local execution resources without changing analysis outputs.
parse_positive_int_env <- function(env_name) {
  raw_val <- trimws(Sys.getenv(env_name, unset = ""))
  if (!nzchar(raw_val)) return(NULL)
  parsed_val <- suppressWarnings(as.integer(raw_val))
  if (is.na(parsed_val) || parsed_val <= 0L) {
    stop(env_name, " must be a positive integer when set; got: '", raw_val, "'.")
  }
  parsed_val
}

detect_physical_ram_gb <- function(default_gb = 8L) {
  override_val <- parse_positive_int_env("ABGVBG_MI_RAM_GB")
  if (!is.null(override_val)) {
    return(list(value = override_val, source = "env:ABGVBG_MI_RAM_GB"))
  }

  sys_name <- Sys.info()[["sysname"]]
  ram_bytes <- NA_real_
  if (identical(sys_name, "Darwin")) {
    sysctl_out <- tryCatch(
      system2("sysctl", c("-n", "hw.memsize"), stdout = TRUE, stderr = FALSE),
      error = function(e) character()
    )
    if (length(sysctl_out) >= 1L) ram_bytes <- suppressWarnings(as.numeric(sysctl_out[[1L]]))
  } else if (identical(sys_name, "Linux")) {
    meminfo_path <- "/proc/meminfo"
    if (file.exists(meminfo_path)) {
      meminfo_line <- readLines(meminfo_path, n = 1L, warn = FALSE)



                                                         117
            ram_kb <- suppressWarnings(as.numeric(gsub("[^0-9]", "", meminfo_line)))
            if (is.finite(ram_kb)) ram_bytes <- ram_kb * 1024
        }
    }

    if (!is.finite(ram_bytes) || ram_bytes <= 0) {
      return(list(value = as.integer(default_gb), source = "default"))
    }

    ram_gb <- max(1L, as.integer(floor(ram_bytes / (1024^3))))
    list(value = ram_gb, source = paste0("auto:", sys_name))
}

choose_mi_batch_start <- function(ram_gb) {
  if (!is.finite(ram_gb) || ram_gb <= 0) stop("ram_gb must be a positive finite value.")
  if (ram_gb <= 8L) return(1L)
  if (ram_gb <= 16L) return(2L)
  5L
}

mi_ram_info <- detect_physical_ram_gb(default_gb = 8L)
MI_RAM_GB <- mi_ram_info$value
MI_RAM_GB_SOURCE <- mi_ram_info$source
MI_BATCH_START_OVERRIDE <- parse_positive_int_env("ABGVBG_MI_BATCH_START")
if (!is.null(MI_BATCH_START_OVERRIDE)) {
  MI_BATCH_START <- MI_BATCH_START_OVERRIDE
  MI_BATCH_START_SOURCE <- "env:ABGVBG_MI_BATCH_START"
} else {
  MI_BATCH_START <- choose_mi_batch_start(MI_RAM_GB)
  MI_BATCH_START_SOURCE <- paste0("auto:", MI_RAM_GB_SOURCE)
}

1.1.2 Outcome Variable Creation

# Purpose: derive death 60d.
subset_data <- subset_data %>%
  mutate(
    ## 1. Did the patient die?
    died = if_else(!is.na(death_date), 1L, 0L),

    ## 2. Absolute death date (if death_date is an offset)
    death_abs = if_else(!is.na(death_date),
                        encounter_date + death_date,
                        as.Date(NA)),

    ## 3. Year month (YM) for encounter and death
    enc_ym   = floor_date(encounter_date, unit = "month"),
    death_ym = floor_date(death_abs      , unit = "month"),

    ## 4. Reference censoring date: 1 Jun 2024
    ref_ym = ymd("2024-06-01"),

    ## 5. Months from encounter to death or censoring



                                                         122
   months_death_or_cens = case_when(
      !is.na(death_ym) ~ interval(enc_ym, death_ym) %/% months(1),
      TRUE             ~ interval(enc_ym, ref_ym)   %/% months(1)
   ),

   ## 6. Remove impossible values
   months_death_or_cens = if_else(
      months_death_or_cens < 0 | months_death_or_cens > 16,
      NA_integer_, months_death_or_cens
   ),

   ## 7. Death within one or two months
   died_1mo = if_else(died == 1 & months_death_or_cens < 1, 1L, 0L),
   died_2mo = if_else(died == 1 & months_death_or_cens <= 1, 1L, 0L),

   ## 8. Month of death (missing if censored)
   death_time = if_else(died == 1, months_death_or_cens, NA_integer_),

    ## 9. Death within 60 days (new variable)
    death_60d = if_else(died == 1 & death_abs <= (encounter_date + days(60)), 1L, 0L)
  ) %>%
  select(-enc_ym, -death_ym)

subset_data <- subset_data %>%
  mutate(
    death_60d = if_else(died == 1 & death_abs <= (encounter_date + days(60)), 1L, 0L)
  )

# Robust derivation of analysis variables + helper for Table 1 production
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

# helper: label binary 0/1 → "No"/"Yes"
bin_lab <- function(x) {
  y <- to01(x)
  if (all(is.na(y))) {
    return(factor(y, levels = c(0, 1), labels = c("No", "Yes")))
  }
  factor(y, levels = c(0, 1), labels = c("No", "Yes"))
}

# helper: preserve labeled factors if already present; otherwise map numeric codes
label_from_codes <- function(x, codes, labels) {
  if (is.factor(x)) {
    lev <- levels(x)
    if (all(lev %in% labels)) {
      return(factor(x, levels = labels))
    }
    lev_num <- suppressWarnings(as.numeric(lev))
    if (all(!is.na(lev_num)) && all(lev_num %in% codes)) {
      return(factor(as.numeric(as.character(x)), levels = codes, labels = labels))
    }
    return(x)
  }



                                                         124
    x_num <- suppressWarnings(as.numeric(as.character(x)))
    if (all(is.na(x_num))) return(factor(x, levels = labels))
    if (all(x_num %in% codes, na.rm = TRUE)) {
      return(factor(x_num, levels = codes, labels = labels))
    }
    factor(x)
}

subset_data <- subset_data %>%
  mutate(
    ## ensure 0/1 numerics (avoids factor‑level coercion)
    across(c(has_abg, has_vbg),
           ~ to01(.)),

     ## derive ABG / VBG status groups (binary test status only)
     abg_group = case_when(
        has_abg == 0 ~ "No ABG",
        has_abg == 1 ~ "ABG",
        TRUE         ~ "Missing"
     ),
     vbg_group = case_when(
        has_vbg == 0 ~ "No VBG",
        has_vbg == 1 ~ "VBG",
        TRUE         ~ "Missing"
     ),

     ## factorise groups with explicit NA/Missing level
     abg_group = factor(
        abg_group,
        levels = c("No ABG", "ABG", "Missing")
     ),
     vbg_group = factor(
        vbg_group,
        levels = c("No VBG", "VBG", "Missing")
     ),




                                                            125
      ## labelled covariates (robust to factor or numeric codes)
      sex_label = label_from_codes(sex, c(0, 1), c("Female", "Male")),
      race_ethnicity_label = label_from_codes(
         race_ethnicity,
         0:6,
         c("White", "Black or African American", "Hispanic",
           "Asian", "American Indian", "Pacific Islander", "Unknown")
      ),
      location_label = label_from_codes(
         location,
         0:3,
         c("South", "Northeast", "Midwest", "West")
      ),
      encounter_type_label = label_from_codes(
         encounter_type,
         c(2, 3),
         c("Emergency", "Inpatient")
      ),
      osa_label       = bin_lab(osa),
      asthma_label    = bin_lab(asthma),
      copd_label      = bin_lab(copd),
      chf_label       = bin_lab(chf),
      nmd_label       = bin_lab(nmd),
      phtn_label      = bin_lab(phtn),
      ckd_label       = bin_lab(ckd),
      diabetes_label = bin_lab(dm)
  )

  "age_at_encounter", "curr_bmi", "sex_label", "race_ethnicity_label", "location_label",
  "osa_label", "asthma_label", "copd_label", "chf_label", "nmd_label",
  "phtn_label", "ckd_label", "diabetes_label", "encounter_type_label", "vbg_co2", "paco2"
)

vars_abg <- c(vars_baseline, "paco2")

vars_vbg <- c(vars_baseline, "vbg_co2")

# Table 1 constructor
make_table1 <- function(data, group_var, caption = "") {
  group_sym <- rlang::sym(group_var)

  df <- data %>%
    filter(!is.na(!!group_sym),                   # drop explicit NA
           !!group_sym != "Missing") %>%          # drop “Missing” cohort
    mutate(!!group_sym := droplevels(!!group_sym)) %>% # only drop group levels
    select(all_of(c(group_var, vars_baseline)))

  empty_fac <- names(which(vapply(df, function(z) is.factor(z) && length(levels(z)) == 0L, logical(1))))
  if (length(empty_fac) > 0) {
    warning("0-level factor columns detected: ", paste(empty_fac, collapse = ", "),
            ". Converting to character to prevent gtsummary failure.", call. = FALSE)
    df[empty_fac] <- lapply(df[empty_fac], as.character)
  }

  df %>%
  gtsummary::tbl_summary(
    by    = !!group_sym,
    statistic = list(
       gtsummary::all_continuous() ~ "{mean} ± {sd}; {N_miss}/{N_obs} missing ({p_miss}%)",
       gtsummary::all_categorical() ~ "{n} ({p}%)"
    ),
    digits = list(gtsummary::all_continuous() ~ 1),
    missing = "no",
    label = list(
       age_at_encounter     ~ "Age",
       curr_bmi             ~ "BMI",
       sex_label            ~ "Sex",
       race_ethnicity_label ~ "Race/Ethnicity",
       location_label       ~ "Location",
       osa_label            ~ "OSA",
       asthma_label         ~ "Asthma",




                                                           127
        copd_label           ~ "COPD",
        chf_label            ~ "CHF",
        nmd_label            ~ "NMD",
        phtn_label           ~ "PHTN",
        ckd_label            ~ "CKD",
        diabetes_label       ~ "Diabetes",
        encounter_type_label ~ "Encounter Type"
      )
    ) %>%
    gtsummary::add_overall(last = FALSE) %>%
    gtsummary::modify_header(label = "Variable") %>%
    gtsummary::modify_caption(caption)
}

if (sum(!is.na(subset_data$sex_label)) == 0L || length(levels(subset_data$sex_label)) == 0L) {
  warning("sex_label is all NA or has zero levels; check sex normalization/mapping.", call. = FALSE)
  stopifnot("sex" %in% names(subset_data))
}

# Export machine-readable Table 1 artifacts from the same gtsummary objects
# used for manuscript rendering, so the notebook remains the single source
# of truth for final table outputs.
# gtsummary is convenient for display, but manuscript drafting and QA also need
# a plain rectangular file. We therefore reconstruct the displayed statistics
# from the hidden gtsummary body/header objects and align the ABG/VBG panels on
# their shared row structure before exporting a combined CSV/PDF version.
clean_gts_text <- function(x) {
  x <- as.character(x)
  x <- gsub("\\*\\*", "", x)
  x <- gsub("\\s*<br\\s*/?>\\s*", " ", x, perl = TRUE)
  x <- gsub("\\s*\\n\\s*", " ", x, perl = TRUE)
  trimws(x)
}

# helper: reconstruct a rectangular export table from one gtsummary object so
# manuscript tables can be audited outside the PDF.
extract_tbl_summary_csv <- function(tbl, panel_name) {
  body <- tbl$table_body |>
    dplyr::select(
      dplyr::any_of(c("variable", "var_type", "row_type", "var_label", "label")),
      dplyr::starts_with("stat_")
    ) |>
    dplyr::mutate(row_id = dplyr::row_number())

  header_map <- tbl$table_styling$header |>
    dplyr::filter(grepl("^stat_", .data$column)) |>
    dplyr::transmute(
      column = .data$column,
      group_label = clean_gts_text(.data$label)




                                                         133
     )

    body |>
      tidyr::pivot_longer(
        cols = dplyr::starts_with("stat_"),
        names_to = "column",
        values_to = "stat"
      ) |>
      dplyr::left_join(header_map, by = "column") |>
      dplyr::mutate(
        panel = panel_name,
        var_label = clean_gts_text(.data$var_label),
        label = clean_gts_text(.data$label)
      ) |>
      dplyr::select(
        .data$row_id, .data$panel, .data$variable, .data$var_type,
        .data$row_type, .data$var_label, .data$label,
        .data$group_label, .data$stat
      ) |>
      tidyr::pivot_wider(names_from = .data$group_label, values_from = .data$stat) |>
      dplyr::arrange(.data$row_id)
}

tbl1_abg_csv <- extract_tbl_summary_csv(tbl1_abg, "ABG status")
tbl1_vbg_csv <- extract_tbl_summary_csv(tbl1_vbg, "VBG status")

table1_key_cols <- c("row_id", "variable", "var_type", "row_type", "var_label", "label")
stopifnot(identical(
   tbl1_abg_csv[, table1_key_cols, drop = FALSE],
   tbl1_vbg_csv[, table1_key_cols, drop = FALSE]
))
stopifnot(identical(tbl1_abg_csv$Everyone, tbl1_vbg_csv$Everyone))

abg_group_cols <- setdiff(names(tbl1_abg_csv), c(table1_key_cols, "panel", "Everyone"))
vbg_group_cols <- setdiff(names(tbl1_vbg_csv), c(table1_key_cols, "panel", "Everyone"))
stopifnot(length(abg_group_cols) == 2L, length(vbg_group_cols) == 2L)




                                                           134
tbl1_combined_internal <- tbl1_abg_csv |>
  dplyr::select(
    .data$row_id, .data$panel, .data$variable, .data$var_type, .data$row_type,
    .data$var_label, .data$label, .data$Everyone, dplyr::all_of(abg_group_cols)
  ) |>
  dplyr::left_join(
    tbl1_vbg_csv |>
       dplyr::select(.data$row_id, dplyr::all_of(vbg_group_cols)),
    by = "row_id"
  ) |>
  dplyr::select(-.data$row_id)

tbl1_combined_csv <- tbl1_combined_internal |>
  dplyr::transmute(
    Characteristic = dplyr::if_else(
       .data$row_type == "level",
       paste0(" ", .data$label),
       .data$label
    ),
    Everyone = .data$Everyone,
    `Did not get ABG` = .data[[abg_group_cols[[1L]]]],
    `Did get ABG` = .data[[abg_group_cols[[2L]]]],
    `Did not get VBG` = .data[[vbg_group_cols[[1L]]]],
    `Did get VBG` = .data[[vbg_group_cols[[2L]]]]
  ) |>
  dplyr::mutate(dplyr::across(dplyr::everything(), ~ dplyr::if_else(is.na(.x), "", as.character(.x))))

write_csv_safely(tbl1_abg_csv, results_path("table1_abg_status.csv"), row_names = FALSE)
write_csv_safely(tbl1_vbg_csv, results_path("table1_vbg_status.csv"), row_names = FALSE)
write_csv_safely(tbl1_combined_internal, results_path("table1_combined_internal.csv"), row_names = FALSE)
write_csv_safely(tbl1_combined_csv, results_path("table1_combined.csv"), row_names = FALSE)

# Purpose: co2 category definitions.
ABG_CO2_VAR <- "paco2"

CO2_SPEC <- list(
  ABG = list(var = ABG_CO2_VAR, normal_lo = ABG_CO2_LOW, normal_hi = ABG_CO2_HIGH),
  VBG = list(var = VBG_CO2_VAR, normal_lo = VBG_CO2_LOW, normal_hi = VBG_CO2_HIGH)
)
CO2_SPEC$ABG$ref <- (CO2_SPEC$ABG$normal_lo + CO2_SPEC$ABG$normal_hi) / 2
CO2_SPEC$VBG$ref <- (CO2_SPEC$VBG$normal_lo + CO2_SPEC$VBG$normal_hi) / 2
# Reference values for spline OR curves (midpoint of normal range)
ABG_CO2_REF <- CO2_SPEC$ABG$ref
VBG_CO2_REF <- CO2_SPEC$VBG$ref
CO2_CAT_LEVELS <- c("Normal", "Low", "High")
CO2_CAT_CONTRAST_LEVELS <- setdiff(CO2_CAT_LEVELS, "Normal")

# helper: bucket a continuous CO2 value into the manuscript's low/normal/high
# three-level exposure definition.
make_co2_cat3 <- function(x, low_cut, high_cut) {
  x <- suppressWarnings(as.numeric(x))
  out <- dplyr::case_when(
    is.na(x)       ~ NA_character_,
    x < low_cut    ~ "Low",
    x > high_cut   ~ "High",
    TRUE           ~ "Normal"
  )
  factor(out, levels = CO2_CAT_LEVELS)
}

subset_data <- subset_data %>%



                                                         138
  mutate(
    pco2_cat_abg = make_co2_cat3(.data[[ABG_CO2_VAR]], ABG_CO2_LOW, ABG_CO2_HIGH),
    pco2_cat_vbg = make_co2_cat3(.data[[VBG_CO2_VAR]], VBG_CO2_LOW, VBG_CO2_HIGH)
  )

stopifnot("Normal" %in% levels(subset_data$pco2_cat_abg),
          "Normal" %in% levels(subset_data$pco2_cat_vbg))

# helper: warn when a tested-cohort category is sparse enough to make later
# categorical-model estimates unstable.
warn_low_counts <- function(cat, label) {
  tab <- table(cat, useNA = "no")
  if (length(tab) && any(tab < 10)) {
    warning(label, ": low counts in CO2 categories: ",
            paste(names(tab), tab, collapse = ", "), call. = FALSE)
  }
}
warn_low_counts(subset_data$pco2_cat_abg[subset_data$has_abg == 1 & !is.na(subset_data$paco2)],
                "ABG")
warn_low_counts(subset_data$pco2_cat_vbg[subset_data$has_vbg == 1 & !is.na(subset_data$vbg_co2)],
                "VBG")

if (any(grepl(pat_var, txt))) {
  stop("Binary CO2 indicator variable references remain in the QMD.")
}

rate_panel <- bind_rows(
  subset_data %>%
    filter(has_abg == 1) %>%
    select(all_of(outcome_vars), pco2_cat_abg) %>%
    tidyr::pivot_longer(all_of(outcome_vars), names_to = "outcome", values_to = "event") %>%
    group_by(pco2_cat_abg, outcome) %>%
    summarise(
      events = sum(event == 1, na.rm = TRUE),
      denom = sum(!is.na(event)),
      rate   = events / denom,
      .groups = "drop_last"
    ) %>%
    mutate(group = "ABG", co2_group = as.character(pco2_cat_abg)),
  subset_data %>%
    filter(has_vbg == 1) %>%
    select(all_of(outcome_vars), pco2_cat_vbg) %>%
    tidyr::pivot_longer(all_of(outcome_vars), names_to = "outcome", values_to = "event") %>%
    group_by(pco2_cat_vbg, outcome) %>%
    summarise(
      events = sum(event == 1, na.rm = TRUE),
      denom = sum(!is.na(event)),
      rate   = events / denom,
      .groups = "drop_last"
    ) %>%
    mutate(group = "VBG", co2_group = as.character(pco2_cat_vbg))
) %>%
  ungroup() %>%
  mutate(
    outcome      = recode(outcome, !!!outcome_labels),
    rate_fmt     = sprintf("%s/%s (%.1f%%)", events, denom, 100 * rate),




                                                         144
    co2_group    = factor(co2_group, levels = CO2_CAT_LEVELS)
  ) %>%
  select(group, outcome, co2_group, rate_fmt) %>%
  tidyr::pivot_wider(names_from = co2_group, values_from = rate_fmt) %>%
  arrange(factor(group, levels = c("ABG", "VBG")),
          factor(outcome, levels = c("IMV", "NIV", "Death (60d)", "Hypercapnic RF")))

1.3 Three-level PCO2 categories (unweighted)

Three groups using low/normal/high CO2 categories

# Purpose: or data three level unweighted.
stopifnot(all(c("pco2_cat_abg", "pco2_cat_vbg") %in% names(subset_data)))


# helper: fit one three-level categorical outcome model, optionally restricted
# to the tested cohort and optionally using sampling weights.
fit_cat3_model <- function(data, outcome, cat_var, group_name,
                           adj_vars = NULL,
                           analysis_variant = "unweighted",
                           weight_var = NULL,
                           treat_var = NULL) {
  stopifnot(outcome %in% names(data), cat_var %in% names(data))
  if (!is.null(weight_var)) stopifnot(weight_var %in% names(data))
  if (!is.null(treat_var)) stopifnot(treat_var %in% names(data))

  dat <- data
  if (!is.null(treat_var)) {
    dat <- dat |>
      dplyr::filter(.data[[treat_var]] == 1)



                                                         146
}

keep_vars <- unique(c(outcome, cat_var, adj_vars, weight_var))
dat <- dat |>
  dplyr::select(dplyr::all_of(keep_vars)) |>
  dplyr::mutate(
    !!cat_var := stats::relevel(
      factor(.data[[cat_var]], levels = CO2_CAT_LEVELS),
      ref = "Normal"
    ),
    !!outcome := to01(.data[[outcome]])
  ) |>
  dplyr::filter(!is.na(.data[[cat_var]]), !is.na(.data[[outcome]]))

if (nrow(dat) == 0L || dplyr::n_distinct(dat[[outcome]]) < 2L) {
  stop("fit_cat3_model: insufficient outcome variation after filtering for ", group_name, " / ", outcome)
}

rhs_terms <- c(cat_var, adj_vars)
f <- stats::reformulate(rhs_terms, response = outcome)
fit_call <- if (is.null(weight_var)) {
  function() glm(f, data = dat, family = binomial, control = glm.control(maxit = 50))
} else {
  dat <- dat |>
    dplyr::mutate(.wt_cat3 = suppressWarnings(as.numeric(.data[[weight_var]]))) |>
    dplyr::filter(is.finite(.wt_cat3), .wt_cat3 > 0)
  if (nrow(dat) == 0L) {
    stop("fit_cat3_model: no rows with finite positive weights for ", group_name, " / ", outcome)
  }
  function() {
    design <- survey::svydesign(ids = ~1, weights = ~.wt_cat3, data = dat)
    survey::svyglm(f, design = design, family = quasibinomial(),
                   control = glm.control(maxit = 50))
  }
}




                                                       147
    fit_res <- fit_with_diagnostics(
      fit_call,
      context = make_context(
        stage = "outcome",
        component = "cat3",
        analysis_variant = analysis_variant,
        model_type = "cat3",
        group = group_name,
        outcome = outcome,
        imputation = NA_integer_,
        batch = NA_integer_
      )
    )
    append_outcome_diag(fit_res$diag)
    if (is.null(fit_res$fit)) {
      stop("fit_cat3_model: model fit failed for outcome=", outcome,
           " cat_var=", cat_var, " group=", group_name)
    }
    fit_res$fit
}

# helper: pull the low/high-versus-normal odds-ratio rows out of one fitted
# three-level categorical model.
extract_cat3_or_terms <- function(fit_obj, outcome, cat_var, group_name, model_type) {
  broom::tidy(fit_obj, exponentiate = TRUE, conf.int = TRUE) |>
    dplyr::filter(term != "(Intercept)", startsWith(term, cat_var)) |>
    dplyr::mutate(
      outcome = outcome,
      group = group_name,
      model = model_type
    )
}

# helper: thin convenience wrapper retained for legacy unweighted categorical
# OR outputs built from the shared fitting helper above.
run_logit <- function(data, outcome, exposure, group_name, adj_vars = NULL, model_type = "Crude") {




                                                           148
    fit_obj <- fit_cat3_model(
      data = data,
      outcome = outcome,
      cat_var = exposure,
      group_name = group_name,
      adj_vars = adj_vars,
      analysis_variant = if (length(adj_vars)) "unweighted" else "crude"
    )
    extract_cat3_or_terms(fit_obj, outcome, exposure, group_name, model_type)
}

  "ABG 3-level: HCRF ~ CO2 category + X"     = reformulate(c("pco2_cat_abg", adj_core), response =
   ↪  "hypercap_resp_failure"),

# Purpose: standalone Supplementary Table S2 export for crude categorical associations.

  unw_results_crude,

    `Gas type` = group,

1.5 Restricted cubic spline regressions (unweighted)

Spline curves are shown as odds ratios relative to CO2_ref (midpoint of the normal range), holding covariates at the reference profile.

# ABG spline dataset
subset_data_abg <- subset_data %>%
  filter(has_abg == 1, !is.na(paco2)) %>%
  select(paco2, imv_proc, niv_proc, death_60d, hypercap_resp_failure, all_of(adj_core)) %>%
  filter(complete.cases(.))


1.5.1 Unweighted, Restricted Cubic Spline Regression - ABG by PaCO2

# Purpose: rcs abg unweighted models.
make_spline_fml <- function(outcome, co2_var, adj_vars) {
  spline_term <- if (SPLINE_BASIS == "rcs") {
    sprintf("rms::rcs(%s, %d)", co2_var, SPLINE_DF)
  } else {
    sprintf("splines::ns(%s, %d)", co2_var, SPLINE_DF)
  }
  stats::as.formula(
    paste0(outcome, " ~ ", spline_term,
           if (length(adj_vars)) paste0(" + ", paste(adj_vars, collapse = " + ")) else "")




                                                                     154
    )
}

#| code-block-title: "Unweighted ABG spline models (adjusted)"
abg_spline_forms <- list(
  "ABG spline (adjusted): IMV ~ CO2 spline + X"      = make_spline_fml("imv_proc", "paco2", adj_core),
  "ABG spline (adjusted): NIV ~ CO2 spline + X"      = make_spline_fml("niv_proc", "paco2", adj_core),
  "ABG spline (adjusted): Death60d ~ CO2 spline + X" = make_spline_fml("death_60d", "paco2", adj_core),
  "ABG spline (adjusted): HCRF ~ CO2 spline + X"     = make_spline_fml("hypercap_resp_failure", "paco2", adj_core)
)
register_model_diagrams(abg_spline_forms)

co2_seq_abg <- stats::quantile(subset_data_abg$paco2, probs = c(0.02, 0.98), na.rm = TRUE)
grid_abg_info_unw <- make_co2_grid_ref(
  "paco2",
  seq(co2_seq_abg[1], co2_seq_abg[2], length.out = SPLINE_GRID_N),
  x_ref_abg,
  ABG_CO2_REF
)
grid_abg_unw <- grid_abg_info_unw$grid
ref_idx_abg_unw <- grid_abg_info_unw$ref_idx
co2_ref_abg_unw <- grid_abg_info_unw$co2_ref

# helper: fit one adjusted spline logistic model for the complete-case
# unweighted analyses and record standardized diagnostics.
fit_spline_glm <- function(outcome, co2_var, data, group_label,
                            adj_vars = adj_core,
                            analysis_variant = "unweighted") {
  fit_res <- fit_with_diagnostics(
    function() glm(make_spline_fml(outcome, co2_var, adj_vars),
                   data = data, family = binomial,
                   control = glm.control(maxit = 50)),
    context = make_context(
      stage = "outcome",
      component = "spline",
      analysis_variant = analysis_variant,




                                                         155
       model_type = "spline",
       group = group_label,
       outcome = outcome,
       imputation = NA_integer_,
       batch = NA_integer_
      )
    )
    append_outcome_diag(fit_res$diag)
    fit_res$fit
}

fit_imv <- fit_spline_glm("imv_proc", "paco2", subset_data_abg, "ABG", adj_vars = adj_core)
fit_niv <- fit_spline_glm("niv_proc", "paco2", subset_data_abg, "ABG", adj_vars = adj_core)
fit_death <- fit_spline_glm("death_60d", "paco2", subset_data_abg, "ABG", adj_vars = adj_core)
fit_hcrf <- fit_spline_glm("hypercap_resp_failure", "paco2", subset_data_abg, "ABG", adj_vars = adj_core)
if (any(vapply(list(fit_imv, fit_niv, fit_death, fit_hcrf), is.null, logical(1)))) {
  stop("Unweighted ABG spline fits failed; see model_fit_diagnostics.csv.")
}

pred_imv <- predict_or_curve_from_fit(fit_imv, grid_abg_unw, ref_idx_abg_unw, "paco2")
pred_niv <- predict_or_curve_from_fit(fit_niv, grid_abg_unw, ref_idx_abg_unw, "paco2")
pred_death <- predict_or_curve_from_fit(fit_death, grid_abg_unw, ref_idx_abg_unw, "paco2")
pred_hcrf <- predict_or_curve_from_fit(fit_hcrf, grid_abg_unw, ref_idx_abg_unw, "paco2")

# helper: plot one unweighted ABG predicted-probability spline panel using the
# shared probability axis computed across outcomes.
plot_prob_abg <- function(dat, title_txt) {
  ggplot(dat, aes(x = paco2, y = p)) +
    geom_line(color = "#1f77b4", linewidth = 1.0) +
    geom_ribbon(aes(ymin = p_LCL, ymax = p_UCL), fill = "#1f77b4", alpha = 0.2) +
    prob_axis_scale(axis_unw_prob) +
    labs(
      title = title_txt,
      x = "PaCO2 (mmHg)",
      y = "Predicted probability",
      caption = paste0("Conditional on reference covariate profile X_ref; ref PaCO2 = ", co2_ref_abg_unw, " mmHg")
    ) +
    theme_pub()
}

# helper: plot one unweighted VBG predicted-probability spline panel using the

    geom_ribbon(aes(ymin = p_LCL, ymax = p_UCL), fill = "#d95f02", alpha = 0.2) +
    prob_axis_scale(axis_unw_prob) +

      title = title_txt,
      x = "VBG CO2 (mmHg)",
      y = "Predicted probability",

float_barrier("section")



                                                         161
2 Inverse Propensity Weighting (GBM)

IPW done using Gradient Boosting Methods (GBM) - a type of decision-tree based machine learning. “Random forests and GBM are
designed to automatically include relevant interactions for variables included in the model. As such, using a GBM to estimate the
PS model, can reduce model misspecification, since the analyst is not required to identify relevant interactions or nonlinearities.”
from this citation: PMID: 39947224. PMCID: PMC11825193.
Current propensity score uses covars_gbm (demographics, comorbidities, encounter type, vitals, labs) as defined above; in this block only
encounter_type is explicitly factored before weighting.
Note: for all these, I suggested new GBM adjustments that accomplish the following:

  1. Smaller GBM & balance‑based stopping (stop.method = “smd.max”) → faster fit, avoids over‑fitting, lighter tails (which lead to extreme
     weights that are problematic).
  2. Target balance compares weighted treated cohort to the full sample; aim for |SMD| < 0.1.
  3. Weight stabilization (divide by mean) mitigates a few huge weights. We use one‑sided truncation at very small propensities (caps large
     weights only).
  4. Uses robust variance estimation (e.g. allows the variances to change by PaCO2) for IP‑weighted GLM; works with splines via rcs(). This
     is a bit nuanced but I think good to change even though it adds complexity
  5. Deterministic seed ensures result replication.


2.0.1 ABG IPW weighting and diagnostics

# Already normalized globally; just drop unused levels
subset_data$encounter_type <- droplevels(subset_data$encounter_type)

GBM tuning is shared across ABG and VBG via gbm_params to keep symmetry; update there if needed.

# �� 1. fit GBM propensity model, ABG �����������������������������������������������
# Build a minimal modeling frame (treatment + covariates only).
# Including has_vbg preserves shared normalization checks used elsewhere.
set.seed(42)
gbm_df_abg <- subset_data[, c("has_abg", "has_vbg", covars_gbm), drop = FALSE]

# Normalize data types before fitting GBM so predictors are consistent.




                                                                   162
gbm_df_abg <- normalize_types(gbm_df_abg, levels_ref)
gbm_df_abg <- droplevels_all(gbm_df_abg)

# Log potential design-size problems and memory usage around model fit.
gbm_preflight(gbm_df_abg, covars_gbm, "unimp_abg")
append_mem_snapshot("gbm_unimp", "unimp_abg", "pre")

weight_model <- do.call(
  weightit,
  c(
    list(
       formula_abg,
       data         = gbm_df_abg,
       method       = "gbm",
       estimand     = "ATE",
       missing    = "ind",
       include.obj = FALSE
    ),
    gbm_params
  )
)
append_mem_snapshot("gbm_unimp", "unimp_abg", "post")

# �� 2. One‑sided IPSW (ABG observed only) + truncation of small propensities ��
# `compute_ipow_weights()` applies the project's one-sided weighting rule:
# treated rows receive inverse propensity weights, non-treated rows are anchors.
ipow_abg <- compute_ipow_weights(
  weight_model,
  treat = gbm_df_abg$has_abg,
  ps_floor_quantile = ps_trunc_quantile,
  stabilize = TRUE
)
w_abg <- ipow_abg$weights

# Balance diagnostics and treated-only outcome models are handled later.

Inverse Propensity-Weighted Logistic Regressions with CO2 predictor represented as a restricted cubic spline.
These are covariate-adjusted outcome models (outcome ~ spline(CO2) + X), fit separately for ABG and VBG cohorts using survey::svyglm
with robust (design-based) SEs. Spline curves are shown as odds ratios relative to CO2_ref (midpoint of the normal range).


2.0.2 ABG IPW spline models

# set.seed(42) # reproducible GBM fit

# # �� 1. inverse‑probability weights for receiving an ABG �����������������������

# # done in the last block, so not needed

# Model diagrams: IPW ABG spline models
ipw_abg_rcs_forms <- list(
  "ABG IPW spline (adjusted): IMV ~ CO2 spline + X"      = make_spline_fml("imv_proc", "paco2", adj_core),
  "ABG IPW spline (adjusted): NIV ~ CO2 spline + X"      = make_spline_fml("niv_proc", "paco2", adj_core),
  "ABG IPW spline (adjusted): Death60d ~ CO2 spline + X" = make_spline_fml("death_60d", "paco2", adj_core),
  "ABG IPW spline (adjusted): HCRF ~ CO2 spline + X"     = make_spline_fml("hypercap_resp_failure", "paco2", adj_core)
)
register_model_diagrams(ipw_abg_rcs_forms)

# �� 2. analysis sample: rows with a measured PaCO2 ����������������������������
subset_data_abg <- subset_data %>%
  filter(!is.na(paco2)) %>%                     # implies has_abg == 1
  select(paco2, imv_proc, niv_proc, death_60d,
          hypercap_resp_failure, w_abg, all_of(adj_core)) %>%



                                                                   164
  filter(complete.cases(.))


# �� 3. weighted logistic spline models with robust SEs �����������������������
# helper: fit one ABG IPW spline model with robust survey variance and attach
# standardized diagnostics.
fitfun <- function(formula, outcome) {
  fit_res <- fit_with_diagnostics(
     function() svyglm(
        formula,
        design = svydesign(ids = ~1, weights = ~w_abg, data = subset_data_abg),
        family = quasibinomial(),
        control = glm.control(maxit = 50)
     ),
     context = make_context(
        stage = "outcome",
        component = "spline",
        analysis_variant = "ipw",
        model_type = "spline",
        group = "ABG",
        outcome = outcome,
        imputation = NA_integer_,
        batch = NA_integer_
     )
  )
  append_outcome_diag(fit_res$diag)
  fit_res$fit
}

fit_imv_abg   <- fitfun(make_spline_fml("imv_proc", "paco2", adj_core), "imv_proc")
fit_niv_abg   <- fitfun(make_spline_fml("niv_proc", "paco2", adj_core), "niv_proc")
fit_death_abg <- fitfun(make_spline_fml("death_60d", "paco2", adj_core), "death_60d")
fit_hcrf_abg <- fitfun(make_spline_fml("hypercap_resp_failure", "paco2", adj_core),
                        "hypercap_resp_failure")
if (any(vapply(list(fit_imv_abg, fit_niv_abg, fit_death_abg, fit_hcrf_abg), is.null, logical(1)))) {
  stop("IPW ABG spline fits failed; see model_fit_diagnostics.csv.")




                                                           165
}

# �� 4. prediction helper �����������������������������������������������������
# helper: generate one ABG IPW spline odds-ratio curve over the observed CO2
# range while holding the reference profile fixed.
mkpred <- function(fit, data_ref, co2_var, ref_df, co2_ref) {
  co2_seq <- stats::quantile(data_ref[[co2_var]], probs = c(0.02, 0.98), na.rm = TRUE)
  grid_info <- make_co2_grid_ref(
     co2_var,
     seq(co2_seq[1], co2_seq[2], length.out = SPLINE_GRID_N),
     ref_df,
     co2_ref
  )
  predict_or_curve_from_fit(fit, grid_info$grid, grid_info$ref_idx, co2_var)
}

pred_imv_abg    <- mkpred(fit_imv_abg,                        subset_data_abg, "paco2", x_ref_abg, ABG_CO2_REF)
pred_niv_abg    <- mkpred(fit_niv_abg,                        subset_data_abg, "paco2", x_ref_abg, ABG_CO2_REF)
pred_death_abg <- mkpred(fit_death_abg, subset_data_abg, "paco2", x_ref_abg, ABG_CO2_REF)
pred_hcrf_abg <- mkpred(fit_hcrf_abg, subset_data_abg, "paco2", x_ref_abg, ABG_CO2_REF)
axis_abg_ipw_trim <- compute_or_axis_spec(
  list(pred_imv_abg, pred_niv_abg, pred_death_abg, pred_hcrf_abg),
  lo_col = "LCL", hi_col = "UCL"
)

# helper: generate one trimmed-range ABG IPW spline odds-ratio curve from a
# fitted survey-weighted model.
mkpred <- function(fit, data_ref, co2_var, ref_df, co2_ref) {
  q <- stats::quantile(data_ref[[co2_var]], probs = c(0.02, 0.98), na.rm = TRUE)
  grid_info <- make_co2_grid_ref(
     co2_var,
     seq(q[1], q[2], length.out = SPLINE_GRID_N),
     ref_df,
     co2_ref
  )
  predict_or_curve_from_fit(fit, grid_info$grid, grid_info$ref_idx, co2_var)
}

#   Inverse-propensity weighting & outcome modelling for **VBG** cohort
#     – mirrored 1-to-1 to the validated ABG workflow

set.seed(42)

# 1. IPW for VBG ---------------------------------------------------------------

# Mirror ABG logic: create a minimal design frame and normalize types first.
gbm_df_vbg <- subset_data[, c("has_abg", "has_vbg", covars_gbm), drop = FALSE]
gbm_df_vbg <- normalize_types(gbm_df_vbg, levels_ref)
gbm_df_vbg <- droplevels_all(gbm_df_vbg)

# Capture model-size and memory telemetry before/after fit.

append_mem_snapshot("gbm_unimp", "unimp_vbg", "pre")
w_vbg <- do.call(
  weightit,
  c(
    list(
      formula_vbg,
      data         = gbm_df_vbg,
      method       = "gbm",



                                                           170
      estimand    = "ATE",
      missing     = "ind",
      include.obj = FALSE
   ),
   gbm_params
  )
)

# One‑sided IPSW (VBG observed only) + truncation of small propensities
# Same weighting convention as ABG, but for VBG testing indicator.

  w_vbg,
  treat = gbm_df_vbg$has_vbg,
  ps_floor_quantile = ps_trunc_quantile,
  stabilize = TRUE
)

Three groups with weights and covariate adjustment

# �� 2. Function: weighted logistic regression & OR extraction ���������������
# helper: thin wrapper retained for the legacy GBM-weighted categorical OR
# figures while reusing the shared weighted categorical fitting helper.
run_weighted_or <- function(data, outcome, cat_var, weight_var, group_name,
                             treat_var, adj_vars) {
  fit_obj <- fit_cat3_model(
     data = data,
     outcome = outcome,



                                                              179
        cat_var = cat_var,
        group_name = group_name,
        adj_vars = adj_vars,
        analysis_variant = "ipw",
        weight_var = weight_var,
        treat_var = treat_var
    )

    extract_cat3_or_terms(fit_obj, outcome, cat_var, group_name, "GBM-weighted")
}

# �� 3. Run across outcomes & cohorts ����������������������������������������

# This chunk fits lightweight explainability GBM models for ABG/VBG

nonmi_shap_vbg_file <- results_path("shap_top10_ipw_gbm_vbg.csv")

if (RUN_SHAP && HAS_FASTSHAP) {
  # Build ABG/VBG design frames using the same covariates as propensity models.
  gbm_shap_df_abg <- subset_data[, c("has_abg", "has_vbg", covars_gbm), drop = FALSE]
  gbm_shap_df_abg <- normalize_types(gbm_shap_df_abg, levels_ref)
  gbm_shap_df_abg <- droplevels_all(gbm_shap_df_abg)

  gbm_shap_df_vbg <- subset_data[, c("has_abg", "has_vbg", covars_gbm), drop = FALSE]
  gbm_shap_df_vbg <- normalize_types(gbm_shap_df_vbg, levels_ref)
  gbm_shap_df_vbg <- droplevels_all(gbm_shap_df_vbg)

  # Fit separate GBM explainers for ABG and VBG testing models.
  set.seed(20251206)
  shap_fit_abg <- fit_weightit_gbm_for_shap(formula_abg, gbm_shap_df_abg)
  set.seed(30251206)
  shap_fit_vbg <- fit_weightit_gbm_for_shap(formula_vbg, gbm_shap_df_vbg)

  # Compute and rank mean |SHAP| values (top N per cohort).
  shap_top_abg <- extract_nonmi_gbm_shap_top(
    shap_fit_abg, gbm_shap_df_abg, covars_gbm, "ABG",
    nsim = SHAP_NSIM, top_n = SHAP_TOP_N
  )
  shap_top_vbg <- extract_nonmi_gbm_shap_top(
    shap_fit_vbg, gbm_shap_df_vbg, covars_gbm, "VBG",
    nsim = SHAP_NSIM, top_n = SHAP_TOP_N
  )

  write_csv_safely(shap_top_abg, nonmi_shap_abg_file, row_names = FALSE)
  write_csv_safely(shap_top_vbg, nonmi_shap_vbg_file, row_names = FALSE)

  # Draw publication figure: ABG panel on left, VBG panel on right.
  shap_top_nonmi <- dplyr::bind_rows(shap_top_abg, shap_top_vbg)
  if (nrow(shap_top_nonmi) > 0) {
    p_shap_nonmi <- plot_shap_top10_two_panel(
      shap_top_nonmi,




                                                         188
        "SHAP-style contribution summaries for gradient-boosted ABG and VBG test-ordering models",
        "Mean |SHAP value|"
      )
      # Save + register; display occurs after love plot for narrative flow.
      shap_file <- results_path("figs", "shap-top10-ipw-gbm-abg-vbg.png")
      save_diag_plot(p_shap_nonmi, shap_file, width = 9, height = 5, dpi = 300)
      register_plot_file("shap-top10-ipw-gbm-abg-vbg", shap_file)
  }

  rm(
    gbm_shap_df_abg, gbm_shap_df_vbg, shap_fit_abg, shap_fit_vbg,
    shap_top_abg, shap_top_vbg, shap_top_nonmi
  )
  invisible(gc())
} else {
  # Keep output schema stable even when SHAP is disabled/unavailable.
  write_csv_safely(data.frame(), nonmi_shap_abg_file, row_names = FALSE)
  write_csv_safely(data.frame(), nonmi_shap_vbg_file, row_names = FALSE)
}

# Purpose: manuscript Figure S6 love plot for GBM weighting.
# Produce a standard love-plot style balance display:
# raw |SMD| vs weighted |SMD| for ABG and VBG cohorts.
covars_balance <- intersect(covars_ps, names(subset_data))
# helper: convert one cobalt balance table into the long format used by the
# manuscript love plot.
love_data_from_bal <- function(data, treat_var, weights_vec, covars, group_label) {
  id_vars <- intersect(c("has_abg", "has_vbg"), names(data))
  bal_cols <- unique(c(id_vars, treat_var, covars))
  bal_df <- data[, bal_cols, drop = FALSE]
  weights_vec <- ifelse(is.finite(weights_vec) & !is.na(weights_vec), weights_vec, 1)
  if (nrow(bal_df) == 0L) {
    return(data.frame(group = character(), term = character(),
                      abs_smd_raw = numeric(), abs_smd_ipw = numeric(),
                      stringsAsFactors = FALSE))
  }
  treat_vals <- unique(stats::na.omit(bal_df[[treat_var]]))



                                                           189
    if (length(treat_vals) < 2L) {
      return(data.frame(group = character(), term = character(),
                        abs_smd_raw = numeric(), abs_smd_ipw = numeric(),
                        stringsAsFactors = FALSE))
    }
    bal_df <- normalize_types(bal_df, levels_ref)
    bal_df <- droplevels_all(bal_df)
    bal_formula <- stats::as.formula(paste(treat_var, "~", paste(covars, collapse = " + ")))
    bal_obj <- cobalt::bal.tab(
      bal_formula,
      data = bal_df,
      weights = weights_vec,
      un = TRUE,
      method = "weighting",
      estimand = "ATE",
      quick = FALSE
    )
    bal_tbl <- as.data.frame(bal_obj$Balance, stringsAsFactors = FALSE)
    bal_tbl$term <- rownames(bal_tbl)
    if (!("Diff.Un" %in% names(bal_tbl))) bal_tbl$Diff.Un <- NA_real_
    if (!("Diff.Adj" %in% names(bal_tbl))) bal_tbl$Diff.Adj <- NA_real_
    bal_tbl |>
      dplyr::transmute(
        group = group_label,
        term = term,
        abs_smd_raw = abs(.data$Diff.Un),
        abs_smd_ipw = abs(.data$Diff.Adj)
      )
}

lov_nonmi <- dplyr::bind_rows(
  love_data_from_bal(subset_data, "has_abg", subset_data$w_abg, covars_balance, "ABG"),
  love_data_from_bal(subset_data, "has_vbg", subset_data$w_vbg, covars_balance, "VBG")
)

lov_nonmi_long <- dplyr::bind_rows(




                                                           190
  lov_nonmi |>
    dplyr::transmute(group, term, sample = "Raw", abs_smd = abs_smd_raw, abs_smd_raw),
  lov_nonmi |>
    dplyr::transmute(group, term, sample = "IPW", abs_smd = abs_smd_ipw, abs_smd_raw)
)
lov_nonmi_long <- add_overall_love_rows(lov_nonmi_long)

write_csv_safely(lov_nonmi_long, results_path("loveplot_ipw_gbm_data.csv"), row_names = FALSE)
p_lov_nonmi <- loveplot_style(
  lov_nonmi_long,
  "Covariate balance after gradient-boosted propensity weighting for ABG and VBG test-ordering models"
)
print_plot_once(p_lov_nonmi, "loveplot-ipw-gbm-abg-vbg", width = 9, height = 6)

# Purpose: manuscript Figure S8 SHAP summary for GBM weighting.
# Read precomputed top-10 SHAP values and re-plot deterministically.
shap_abg_file <- results_path("shap_top10_ipw_gbm_abg.csv")
shap_vbg_file <- results_path("shap_top10_ipw_gbm_vbg.csv")

shap_abg <- utils::read.csv(shap_abg_file, stringsAsFactors = FALSE)
shap_vbg <- utils::read.csv(shap_vbg_file, stringsAsFactors = FALSE)
shap_abg$group <- "ABG"
shap_vbg$group <- "VBG"

shap_plot_df <- dplyr::bind_rows(shap_abg, shap_vbg) |>
  dplyr::filter(is.finite(mean_abs_shap)) |>
  dplyr::group_by(group) |>
  dplyr::arrange(dplyr::desc(mean_abs_shap), .by_group = TRUE) |>
  dplyr::slice_head(n = 10L) |>
  dplyr::ungroup()
