standardization_prediction_status_rows <- list()
record_standardization_prediction_status <- function(imp_index, group, outcome_var,
                                                     probability_family, status,
                                                     error_message = "",
                                                     n_available = NA_integer_,
                                                     n_standardized = NA_integer_,
                                                     n_grid = NA_integer_) {
  standardization_prediction_status_rows[[length(standardization_prediction_status_rows) + 1L]] <<- tibble::tibble(
    imp = imp_index,
    group = group,
    outcome = outcome_var,
    probability_family = probability_family,
    status = status,
    error_message = error_message,
    n_available = as.integer(n_available),
    n_standardized = as.integer(n_standardized),
    n_grid = as.integer(n_grid)
  )
  invisible(TRUE)
}

std_spline_imp_rows <- list()
std_cat3_imp_rows <- list()
for (imp_index in seq_len(imp_n)) {
  d_imp <- get_imp(imp_index)
  std_source_df <- build_common_std_source_df(d_imp, imp_index)
  n_available_i <- attr(std_source_df, "n_available")
  n_standardized_i <- nrow(std_source_df)




                                                         322
for (group_label in c("ABG", "VBG")) {
  co2_var <- if (identical(group_label, "ABG")) "paco2" else "vbg_co2"
  co2_values <- if (identical(group_label, "ABG")) grid_abg_mi$paco2 else grid_vbg_mi$vbg_co2
  spline_bank <- if (identical(group_label, "ABG")) spline_fits_abg else spline_fits_vbg
  cat3_bank <- if (identical(group_label, "ABG")) cat3_fits_abg else cat3_fits_vbg

 for (outcome_var in cat3_outcomes) {
   spline_fit <- compact_spline_fit(spline_bank[[outcome_var]][[imp_index]])
   if (is.null(spline_fit)) {
     record_standardization_prediction_status(
       imp_index, group_label, outcome_var, "spline",
       "skipped_no_compact_fit",
       "compact spline fit unavailable",
       n_available_i, n_standardized_i, length(co2_values)
     )
   } else {
     spline_try <- tryCatch(
       list(
         value = predict_prob_curve_marginal_standardized(
            spline_fit,
            source_df = std_source_df,
            co2_var = co2_var,
            co2_values = co2_values,
            outcome_var = outcome_var
         ),
         error = NULL
       ),
       error = function(e) list(value = NULL, error = conditionMessage(e))
     )
     if (is.null(spline_try$error) && is.data.frame(spline_try$value) && nrow(spline_try$value)) {
       std_spline_imp_rows[[length(std_spline_imp_rows) + 1L]] <- spline_try$value |>
         dplyr::mutate(
            imp = imp_index,
            group = group_label,
            outcome = outcome_var,
            co2_scale = co2_var,




                                                       323
          probability_method = "common_source_marginal_standardized"
        )
      record_standardization_prediction_status(
        imp_index, group_label, outcome_var, "spline",
        "completed", "", n_available_i, n_standardized_i, length(co2_values)
      )
    } else {
    record_standardization_prediction_status(
      imp_index, group_label, outcome_var, "spline",
      "failed_prediction",
      if (is.null(spline_try$error)) "prediction returned no rows" else spline_try$error,
      n_available_i, n_standardized_i, length(co2_values)
    )
}
}

cat3_fit <- cat3_bank[[outcome_var]][[imp_index]]
if (is.null(cat3_fit) || is.null(cat3_fit$coef) || is.null(cat3_fit$vcov)) {
  record_standardization_prediction_status(
    imp_index, group_label, outcome_var, "cat3",
    "skipped_no_compact_fit",
    "compact categorical fit unavailable",
    n_available_i, n_standardized_i, length(CO2_CAT_LEVELS)
  )
} else {
  cat3_try <- tryCatch(
    list(
      value = predict_prob_cat3_marginal_standardized(
         cat3_fit,
         source_df = std_source_df,
         outcome_var = outcome_var
      ),
      error = NULL
    ),
    error = function(e) list(value = NULL, error = conditionMessage(e))
  )




                                                     324
                if (is.null(cat3_try$error) && is.data.frame(cat3_try$value) && nrow(cat3_try$value)) {
                  std_cat3_imp_rows[[length(std_cat3_imp_rows) + 1L]] <- cat3_try$value |>
                    dplyr::mutate(
                      imp = imp_index,
                      group = group_label,
                      outcome = outcome_var,
                      probability_method = "common_source_marginal_standardized"
                    )
                  record_standardization_prediction_status(
                    imp_index, group_label, outcome_var, "cat3",
                    "completed", "", n_available_i, n_standardized_i, length(CO2_CAT_LEVELS)
                  )
                } else {
                record_standardization_prediction_status(
                  imp_index, group_label, outcome_var, "cat3",
                  "failed_prediction",
                  if (is.null(cat3_try$error)) "prediction returned no rows" else cat3_try$error,
                  n_available_i, n_standardized_i, length(CO2_CAT_LEVELS)
                )
            }
            }
        }
    }

    rm(d_imp, std_source_df)
    invisible(gc(FALSE))
}

standardization_prediction_status <- dplyr::bind_rows(standardization_prediction_status_rows)
standardization_prediction_summary <- standardization_prediction_status |>
  dplyr::group_by(probability_family, group, outcome) |>
  dplyr::summarise(
    m_used = sum(.data$status == "completed", na.rm = TRUE),
    m_total = imp_n,
    min_required = ceiling(common_std_min_ok_frac * imp_n),
    m_failed = sum(.data$status == "failed_prediction", na.rm = TRUE),




                                                                 325
   m_skipped = sum(.data$status == "skipped_no_compact_fit", na.rm = TRUE),
   first_error = {
      errors <- .data$error_message[nzchar(.data$error_message)]
      if (length(errors)) errors[[1L]] else ""
   },
   passed_threshold = .data$m_used >= .data$min_required,
   .groups = "drop"
  )
standardization_prediction_status <- standardization_prediction_status |>
    dplyr::left_join(
    standardization_prediction_summary |>
      dplyr::select(probability_family, group, outcome,
                    m_used, m_total, min_required, passed_threshold),
    by = c("probability_family", "group", "outcome")
  )
write_csv_safely(
  standardization_prediction_status,
  results_path("standardization_prediction_status.csv"),
  row_names = FALSE
)
write_csv_safely(
  standardization_prediction_summary,
  results_path("standardization_prediction_summary.csv"),
  row_names = FALSE
)

standardization_failures <- standardization_prediction_summary |>
  dplyr::filter(!.data$passed_threshold)
if (nrow(standardization_failures)) {
  record_standardization_status(
    "marginal_prediction_completion",
    "failed",
    paste0("Common-source marginal standardization failed completion threshold for ",
           paste(paste0(standardization_failures$probability_family, "/",
                        standardization_failures$group, "/",
                        standardization_failures$outcome, " ",




                                                         326
                       standardization_failures$m_used, "/",
                       standardization_failures$m_total), collapse = "; ")),
   "Results/standardization_prediction_status.csv"
  )
  write_csv_safely(
    dplyr::bind_rows(standardization_validation_rows),
    results_path("standardization_validation_status.csv"),
    row_names = FALSE
  )
  stop("Common-source marginal standardization failed; see Results/standardization_prediction_status.csv")
}
record_standardization_status(
  "marginal_prediction_completion",
  "completed",
  paste0("All primary spline and categorical marginal predictions met min_ok_frac = ",
         common_std_min_ok_frac, "."),

)

  prob_curve_marginal_standardized_abg |>
    dplyr::mutate(co2_value = .data$paco2),
  prob_curve_marginal_standardized_vbg |>
    dplyr::mutate(co2_value = .data$vbg_co2)
) |>
  dplyr::mutate(
    probability_method = factor(
      .data$probability_method,
      levels = c(
        "conditional_modality_specific_xref",
        "common_reference_profile",
        "common_source_marginal_standardized"
      ),
      labels = c(
        "Conditional modality-specific X_ref",
        "Common reference profile",
        "Common-source marginal standardized"




                                                           330
      )
   ),
   outcome_label = normalize_key_results_outcome(.data$outcome, context = "probability method comparison"),
   group = normalize_key_results_group(.data$group, context = "probability method comparison")
  )
write_csv_safely(
  probability_method_comparison_curves,
  results_path("probability_method_comparison_curves.csv"),
  row_names = FALSE
)

comparison_nearest_probability <- function(method_label, group_label, outcome_value, target_value) {
  curve_df <- probability_method_comparison_curves |>
    dplyr::filter(
      as.character(.data$probability_method) == method_label,
      as.character(.data$group) == group_label,
      .data$outcome == outcome_value
    )
  if (!nrow(curve_df) || !is.finite(target_value)) return(NA_real_)
  x <- suppressWarnings(as.numeric(curve_df$co2_value))
  ok <- is.finite(x)
  if (!any(ok)) return(NA_real_)
  idx <- which(ok)[which.min(abs(x[ok] - target_value))]
  suppressWarnings(as.numeric(curve_df$p[[idx]]))
}

comparison_relative_gap <- function(abg_value, vbg_value) {
  ifelse(
    is.finite(vbg_value) & abs(vbg_value) > 0,
    (abg_value - vbg_value) / abs(vbg_value),
    NA_real_
  )
}

probability_method_comparison_summary <- tidyr::crossing(
  outcome = cat3_outcomes,




                                                            331
  level = c("Low", "Normal", "High"),
  probability_method = levels(probability_method_comparison_curves$probability_method)
) |>
  dplyr::rowwise() |>
  dplyr::mutate(
    abg_target = dplyr::case_when(
       level == "Low" ~ ABG_CO2_LOW,
       level == "Normal" ~ co2_ref_abg_mi,
       TRUE ~ ABG_CO2_HIGH
    ),
    vbg_target = dplyr::case_when(
       level == "Low" ~ VBG_CO2_LOW,
       level == "Normal" ~ co2_ref_vbg_mi,
       TRUE ~ VBG_CO2_HIGH
    ),
    abg_probability = comparison_nearest_probability(probability_method, "ABG", outcome, abg_target),
    vbg_probability = comparison_nearest_probability(probability_method, "VBG", outcome, vbg_target),
    absolute_gap = abg_probability - vbg_probability,
    relative_gap = comparison_relative_gap(abg_probability, vbg_probability),
    outcome_label = as.character(normalize_key_results_outcome(outcome, context = "probability comparison summary"))
  ) |>
  dplyr::ungroup() |>
  dplyr::select(
    outcome, outcome_label, level, probability_method,
    abg_target, vbg_target, abg_probability, vbg_probability,
    absolute_gap, relative_gap
  )

3.4 Weighted outcome models within each imputation + pooling

Within each imputation, fit covariate‑adjusted CO2 spline outcome models only in the measured cohort (has_abg==1 for PaCO2;
has_vbg==1 for VBG CO2), using IPSW weights to address nonrandom testing. Curves are pooled pointwise across imputations (Rubin’s
rules on the log‑OR scale) and displayed as odds ratios relative to CO2_ref at a reference covariate profile.


3.4.1 Helper: fit + extract log‑OR and SE from svyglm

# helper: return an empty MI SHAP summary with the same schema as the populated
# outputs so downstream code can stay simple.
make_empty_mi_shap <- function() {
  data.frame(feature = character(), mean_abs_shap = numeric(), stringsAsFactors = FALSE)
}

# helper: approximate per-feature contribution magnitudes for one MI logistic
# propensity model using a sampled model matrix on the link scale.
calc_mi_glm_contrib <- function(meta, d_ps, feature_names, imp_index, group_label,
                                sample_n = MI_SHAP_SAMPLE_N,
                                max_terms = MI_SHAP_MAX_TERMS) {
  # Memory-safe contribution approximation for GLM PS:
  # sample rows first, build sparse model matrix, then aggregate |contribution|
  # by feature without constructing a full-N dense matrix.
  diag_row <- data.frame(
    imp = imp_index,
    group = group_label,
    sample_n = NA_integer_,
    n_terms_used = NA_integer_,
    seconds = NA_real_,
    vcells_pre_mb = NA_real_,




                                                         341
 vcells_post_mb = NA_real_,
 method_used = "sparse_sampled_glm_link",
 ok = FALSE,
 error_msg = NA_character_,
 stringsAsFactors = FALSE
)
t0 <- Sys.time()
mem_pre <- get_vcells_stats()
diag_row$vcells_pre_mb <- mem_pre$gc_vcells_used_mb

err_msg <- NA_character_
out <- tryCatch({
  if (is.null(meta$formula) || is.null(meta$coef) || !length(meta$coef)) {
    stop("Missing formula/coefficients in MI PS metadata.")
  }

 n_all <- nrow(d_ps)
 n_use <- min(as.integer(sample_n), n_all)
 if (!is.finite(n_use) || n_use < 2L) {
   stop("Insufficient rows available for MI SHAP sample.")
 }
 seed_offset <- if (toupper(group_label) == "ABG") 10000L else 20000L
 set.seed(20251206L + as.integer(imp_index) + seed_offset)
 idx <- if (n_all > n_use) sample.int(n_all, size = n_use, replace = FALSE) else seq_len(n_all)
 d_sample <- d_ps[idx, , drop = FALSE]
 diag_row$sample_n <- n_use

 form <- stats::as.formula(meta$formula)
 mm_model <- NULL
 mm_mode <- "dense_model_matrix"
 if (requireNamespace("Matrix", quietly = TRUE)) {
   mm_sparse_try <- tryCatch(
     Matrix::sparse.model.matrix(form, data = d_sample),
     error = function(e) NULL
   )
   if (!is.null(mm_sparse_try)) {




                                                       342
      mm_model <- mm_sparse_try
      mm_mode <- "sparse_sampled_glm_link"
  }
}
if (is.null(mm_model)) {
  mm_model <- stats::model.matrix(form, data = d_sample)
  mm_mode <- "dense_sampled_glm_link"
}
diag_row$method_used <- mm_mode

coef_vec <- meta$coef
canon_term <- function(x) {
  x <- gsub("`", "", x, fixed = TRUE)
  gsub("\\s+", "", x, perl = TRUE)
}
mm_terms <- colnames(mm_model)
coef_terms <- names(coef_vec)
mm_key <- canon_term(mm_terms)
coef_key <- canon_term(coef_terms)
coef_pos <- setNames(seq_along(coef_terms), coef_key)
keep_mm <- which(mm_key %in% names(coef_pos) & mm_terms != "(Intercept)")
if (!length(keep_mm)) {
  stop("No overlapping terms between sparse design matrix and coefficient vector.")
}

mm_model <- mm_model[, keep_mm, drop = FALSE]
diag_row$n_terms_used <- ncol(mm_model)
if (is.finite(max_terms) && ncol(mm_model) > as.integer(max_terms)) {
  stop(
    "MI SHAP term count (", ncol(mm_model), ") exceeded MI_SHAP_MAX_TERMS (",
    as.integer(max_terms), ")."
  )
}

mm_terms_kept <- colnames(mm_model)
mm_keys_kept <- canon_term(mm_terms_kept)




                                                     343
 coef_idx <- coef_pos[mm_keys_kept]
 beta <- as.numeric(coef_vec[coef_idx])
 names(beta) <- mm_terms_kept
 mu <- colMeans(mm_model, na.rm = TRUE)
 abs_beta <- abs(beta)
 term_abs <- vapply(
   seq_len(ncol(mm_model)),
   function(j) {
     xj <- mm_model[, j]
     if (!is.numeric(xj)) xj <- as.numeric(xj)
     mean(abs(xj - mu[j]), na.rm = TRUE) * abs_beta[j]
   },
   numeric(1)
 )
 names(term_abs) <- colnames(mm_model)
 rm(mm_model, mu, abs_beta)
 invisible(gc())

  out_tbl <- data.frame(
    term = names(term_abs),
    mean_abs = as.numeric(term_abs),
    stringsAsFactors = FALSE
  ) |>
    dplyr::mutate(feature = vapply(term, term_to_parent_feature, character(1), feature_names = feature_names)) |>
    dplyr::filter(!is.na(feature)) |>
    dplyr::group_by(feature) |>
    dplyr::summarise(mean_abs_shap = sum(mean_abs, na.rm = TRUE), .groups = "drop")
  if (!nrow(out_tbl)) {
    stop("No feature-mapped terms remained after contribution aggregation.")
  }
  out_tbl
}, error = function(e) {
  err_msg <<- conditionMessage(e)
  make_empty_mi_shap()
})




                                                         344
    mem_post <- get_vcells_stats()
    diag_row$vcells_post_mb <- mem_post$gc_vcells_used_mb
    diag_row$seconds <- as.numeric(difftime(Sys.time(), t0, units = "secs"))
    diag_row$ok <- nrow(out) > 0
    if (!isTRUE(diag_row$ok) && is.na(diag_row$error_msg)) {
      diag_row$error_msg <- err_msg
    }

    list(data = out, diag = diag_row)
}

# helper: fall back to absolute pooled coefficient magnitudes when sampled
# contribution calculations fail or are intentionally skipped.
calc_mi_coef_fallback <- function(meta_list, feature_names, group_label, top_n = SHAP_TOP_N) {
  # Fallback ranking using absolute coefficients if contribution matrix
  # cannot be computed (keeps figure/table generation robust).
  coef_rows <- lapply(seq_along(meta_list), function(i) {
    coef_vec <- meta_list[[i]]$coef
    if (is.null(coef_vec) || !length(coef_vec)) return(NULL)
    data.frame(
       imp = i,
       term = names(coef_vec),
       mean_abs = abs(as.numeric(coef_vec)),
       stringsAsFactors = FALSE
    )
  })
  coef_df <- dplyr::bind_rows(coef_rows)
  if (!nrow(coef_df)) {
    return(data.frame(feature = character(), mean_abs_shap = numeric(), group = character(), stringsAsFactors =
     ↪   FALSE))
  }
  coef_df |>
    dplyr::filter(term != "(Intercept)") |>
    dplyr::mutate(feature = vapply(term, term_to_parent_feature, character(1), feature_names = feature_names)) |>
    dplyr::filter(!is.na(feature)) |>
    dplyr::group_by(feature) |>




                                                           345
    dplyr::summarise(mean_abs_shap = mean(mean_abs, na.rm = TRUE), .groups = "drop") |>
    dplyr::arrange(dplyr::desc(mean_abs_shap)) |>
    dplyr::slice_head(n = top_n) |>
    dplyr::mutate(group = group_label)
}

if (RUN_SHAP) {
  # Streaming accumulator avoids storing per-imputation SHAP tables in memory.
  update_feature_accum <- function(accum, contrib_df) {
    if (!nrow(contrib_df)) return(accum)
    vals <- stats::setNames(contrib_df$mean_abs_shap, contrib_df$feature)
    feats <- names(vals)
    new_feats <- setdiff(feats, names(accum$sum))
    if (length(new_feats)) {
      accum$sum[new_feats] <- 0
      accum$count[new_feats] <- 0
    }
    accum$sum[feats] <- accum$sum[feats] + vals
    accum$count[feats] <- accum$count[feats] + 1L
    accum
  }
  finalize_feature_accum <- function(accum, group_label) {
    if (!length(accum$sum)) {
      return(data.frame(feature = character(), mean_abs_shap = numeric(), group = character(), stringsAsFactors =
       ↪  FALSE))
    }
    keep <- accum$count > 0
    data.frame(
      feature = names(accum$sum)[keep],
      mean_abs_shap = as.numeric(accum$sum[keep] / accum$count[keep]),
      group = group_label,
      stringsAsFactors = FALSE
    ) |>
      dplyr::arrange(dplyr::desc(mean_abs_shap)) |>
      dplyr::slice_head(n = SHAP_TOP_N)
  }

infer_primary_method <- function(diag_df, grp, fallback_method) {
  if (identical(fallback_method, "coef_fallback")) return("coef_fallback")
  diag_grp <- diag_df |>
    dplyr::filter(group == grp, ok %in% TRUE, !is.na(method_used), nzchar(method_used))
  if (!nrow(diag_grp)) return(fallback_method)
  names(sort(table(diag_grp$method_used), decreasing = TRUE))[1]
}

# helper: verify that each imputation still has at least two observed CO2
# categories within the tested cohort before categorical modeling proceeds.
check_cat <- function(d, co2, grp, low_cut, high_cut) {
  x   <- suppressWarnings(as.numeric(d[[co2]]))
  fac <- make_co2_cat3(x, low_cut, high_cut)
  tab <- table(fac, useNA = "ifany")
  message(grp, ": ", paste(names(tab), tab, collapse = " | "))
  obs_levels <- names(tab)[!is.na(names(tab))]
  stopifnot(sum(tab[obs_levels] > 0) >= 2)
}



                                                         350
invisible(lapply(seq_len(imp_n), function(i) {
  di <- get_imp(i)
  stopifnot("paco2" %in% names(di))
  check_cat(di[di$has_abg == 1, , drop = FALSE], "paco2",
            sprintf("ABG imp %d", i), low_cut = ABG_CO2_LOW, high_cut = ABG_CO2_HIGH)
}))

invisible(lapply(seq_len(imp_n), function(i) {
  di <- get_imp(i)
  stopifnot("vbg_co2" %in% names(di))
  check_cat(di[di$has_vbg == 1, , drop = FALSE], "vbg_co2",
            sprintf("VBG imp %d", i), low_cut = VBG_CO2_LOW, high_cut = VBG_CO2_HIGH)
}))

3.7.4 Summary: adjusted CO2-category associations across analysis tracks

# Purpose: table summary adjusted threelevel.
# Build the canonical categorical key-results table across all requested tracks,
# while retaining the narrower adjusted-only legacy summary outputs.
label_outcome <- function(x) {
  dplyr::recode(
    x,
    imv_proc = "IMV",
    niv_proc = "NIV",
    death_60d = "Death (60d)",
    hypercap_resp_failure = "Hypercapnic RF",
    IMV = "IMV",
    NIV = "NIV",
    Death60d = "Death (60d)",
    HCRF = "Hypercapnic RF"
  )
}




                                                               354
# helper: format one categorical OR and confidence interval for compact table
# display.
format_cat3_ci <- function(estimate, lcl, ucl) {
  sprintf("%.2f (%.2f, %.2f)", estimate, lcl, ucl)
}

# helper: count the effective modeled sample and number of events for one
# complete-case categorical model specification.
count_model <- function(data, outcome, exposure, adj_vars = NULL,
                        treat_var = NULL, weight_var = NULL) {
  d <- data
  if (!is.null(treat_var)) d <- d[d[[treat_var]] == 1, , drop = FALSE]
  vars <- unique(c(outcome, exposure, adj_vars, weight_var))
  if (!is.null(weight_var)) vars <- c(vars, weight_var)
  d <- d[, vars, drop = FALSE]
  d <- d[complete.cases(d), , drop = FALSE]
  if (!is.null(weight_var)) {
    w <- suppressWarnings(as.numeric(d[[weight_var]]))
    d <- d[is.finite(w) & w > 0, , drop = FALSE]
  }
  if (nrow(d) == 0L) {
    return(tibble::tibble(n_model = 0L, events = 0L))
  }
  d[[outcome]] <- to01(d[[outcome]])
  tibble::tibble(
    n_model = nrow(d),
    events = sum(d[[outcome]] == 1, na.rm = TRUE)
  )
}

# helper: count complete-case modeled rows/events for the non-MI categorical
# tracks so the summary table reports the right denominator for each cohort.
count_group <- function(group, method) {
  exp_var   <- if (group == "ABG") "pco2_cat_abg" else "pco2_cat_vbg"
  treat_var <- if (group == "ABG") "has_abg" else "has_vbg"




                                                         355
    adj_vars <- switch(
      method,
      "Crude" = NULL,
      "Adjusted" = adj_core,
      "GBM-weighted" = adj_core,
      stop("Unsupported non-MI count method: ", method)
    )
    weight_var <- switch(
      method,
      "Crude" = NULL,
      "Adjusted" = NULL,
      "GBM-weighted" = if (group == "ABG") "w_abg" else "w_vbg",
      stop("Unsupported non-MI count method: ", method)
    )
    outcomes <- c("imv_proc", "niv_proc", "death_60d", "hypercap_resp_failure")
    purrr::map_dfr(outcomes, function(outcome) {
      cnt <- count_model(subset_data, outcome, exp_var, adj_vars,
                         treat_var = treat_var, weight_var = weight_var)
      dplyr::mutate(cnt,
                    method = method,
                    group = group,
                    outcome = label_outcome(outcome))
    })
}

# helper: return zero-row MI count summaries for one cohort when an imputation
# contributes no analyzable tested encounters after the required filtering.
empty_mi_count_rows <- function(group, outcomes) {
  tidyr::expand_grid(
    method = c("Imputed", "Weighted and adjusted"),
    outcome = label_outcome(outcomes)
  ) |>
    dplyr::mutate(
       group = group,
       n_model = 0L,
       events = 0L




                                                           356
     ) |>
     dplyr::relocate(method, group, outcome, n_model, events)
}

# helper: compute MI modeled counts for both the imputed-only and weighted MI
# categorical tracks in one pass for one cohort within one imputed dataset.
# This avoids reloading the same full imputation hundreds of times inside the
# manuscript table summary chunk.
compute_mi_count_group_all_methods <- function(d, group, weights, outcomes) {
  if (group == "ABG") {
    co2_var <- "paco2"
    treat_var <- "has_abg"
    low_cut <- ABG_CO2_LOW
    high_cut <- ABG_CO2_HIGH
  } else {
    co2_var <- "vbg_co2"
    treat_var <- "has_vbg"
    low_cut <- VBG_CO2_LOW
    high_cut <- VBG_CO2_HIGH
  }

    d[[co2_var]] <- suppressWarnings(as.numeric(d[[co2_var]]))
    keep <- d[[treat_var]] == 1 & is.finite(d[[co2_var]])
    if (!any(keep)) {
      return(empty_mi_count_rows(group, outcomes))
    }

    d2 <- d[keep, c(outcomes, adj_core, co2_var), drop = FALSE]
    w2 <- weights[keep]
    d2$co2_cat <- make_co2_cat3(d2[[co2_var]], low_cut, high_cut)

    keep2 <- !is.na(d2$co2_cat)
    d2 <- d2[keep2, , drop = FALSE]
    w2 <- w2[keep2]
    if (nrow(d2) == 0L) {
      return(empty_mi_count_rows(group, outcomes))




                                                           357
    }

    purrr::map_dfr(outcomes, function(outcome) {
      outcome_complete <- complete.cases(d2[, c(outcome, adj_core, "co2_cat"), drop = FALSE])
      outcome_vals <- to01(d2[[outcome]])
      weighted_keep <- outcome_complete & is.finite(w2) & w2 > 0

      tibble::tibble(
        method = c("Imputed", "Weighted and adjusted"),
        group = group,
        outcome = label_outcome(outcome),
        n_model = c(
          sum(outcome_complete),
          sum(weighted_keep)
        ),
        events = c(
          sum(outcome_vals[outcome_complete] == 1, na.rm = TRUE),
          sum(outcome_vals[weighted_keep] == 1, na.rm = TRUE)
        )
      )
    })
}

# helper: summarize MI modeled sample size and events across imputations for all
# categorical outcomes and both cohorts using a single pass over each imputed
# dataset. This preserves the original median-across-imputations definition
# while removing a major full-run bottleneck.
build_mi_counts_cat3 <- function() {
  outcomes <- c("imv_proc", "niv_proc", "death_60d", "hypercap_resp_failure")
  per_imp_counts <- vector("list", imp$m)

    for (i in seq_len(imp$m)) {
      d <- get_imp(i)
      w_abg <- get_mi_weight("ABG", i)
      w_vbg <- get_mi_weight("VBG", i)




                                                           358
        per_imp_counts[[i]] <- dplyr::bind_rows(
          compute_mi_count_group_all_methods(d, "ABG", w_abg, outcomes),
          compute_mi_count_group_all_methods(d, "VBG", w_vbg, outcomes)
        ) |>
          dplyr::mutate(imp = i)

        rm(d, w_abg, w_vbg)
        invisible(gc(FALSE))
    }

    dplyr::bind_rows(per_imp_counts) |>
      dplyr::group_by(method, group, outcome) |>
      dplyr::summarise(
        n_model = round(stats::median(n_model, na.rm = TRUE)),
        events = round(stats::median(events, na.rm = TRUE)),
        .groups = "drop"
      )
}

# helper: build one harmonized predicted-probability export for a full
# categorical analysis track across both ABG and VBG cohorts.
predict_cat3_track_probs <- function(fit_list_abg, fit_list_vbg, method,
                                     ref_abg, ref_vbg,
                                     adj_vars = adj_core,
                                     cat_var_abg = "pco2_cat_abg",
                                     cat_var_vbg = "pco2_cat_vbg") {
  prob_abg <- dplyr::bind_rows(lapply(names(fit_list_abg), function(outcome_var) {
    predict_cat3_prob_from_fit(
      fit_list_abg[[outcome_var]],
      ref_df = ref_abg,
      outcome_var = outcome_var,
      cat_var = cat_var_abg,
      adj_vars = adj_vars
    ) |>
      dplyr::mutate(outcome = outcome_var, group = "ABG")
  }))




                                                             359
    prob_vbg <- dplyr::bind_rows(lapply(names(fit_list_vbg), function(outcome_var) {
      predict_cat3_prob_from_fit(
        fit_list_vbg[[outcome_var]],
        ref_df = ref_vbg,
        outcome_var = outcome_var,
        cat_var = cat_var_vbg,
        adj_vars = adj_vars
      ) |>
        dplyr::mutate(outcome = outcome_var, group = "VBG")
    }))

    normalize_cat3_key_results_prob_df(
      dplyr::bind_rows(prob_abg, prob_vbg),
      method = method,
      outcome_col = "outcome",
      group_col = "group",
      category_col = "category",
      p_col = "p",
      lcl_col = "p_LCL",
      ucl_col = "p_UCL",
      context = paste0("categorical track probabilities: ", method)
    )
}

  "Predicted probabilities are conditional on the reference covariate profile X_ref within each test-specific cohort."
)

  "MI-pooled categorical odds ratios use the normal CO2 category as the reference. ",
  "Predicted probabilities are pooled on the link scale and are conditional on X_ref within each test-specific
   ↪  cohort."
)

  "MI-pooled, MI-logistic IPSW-adjusted categorical odds ratios use the normal CO2 category as the reference. ",

   ↪  source-population covariate distribution."
)

3.9 Observed outcome rates by CO2 bin (MI-logistic IPSW)

# Purpose: pool weighted 1-mmHg bin rates across imputations using summary-only objects.
stopifnot(exists("imp"), imp$m > 0)
stopifnot(exists("get_imp"), exists("get_mi_weight"))

co2_rate_mi_rows_abg <- vector("list", imp$m)
co2_rate_mi_rows_vbg <- vector("list", imp$m)

for (i in seq_len(imp$m)) {
  d_i <- get_imp(i)
  w_abg_i <- get_mi_weight("ABG", i)
  w_vbg_i <- get_mi_weight("VBG", i)

  d_abg_i <- d_i[, c("has_abg", "paco2", CO2_RATE_OUTCOMES), drop = FALSE]
  d_abg_i$w_rate <- w_abg_i
  d_vbg_i <- d_i[, c("has_vbg", "vbg_co2", CO2_RATE_OUTCOMES), drop = FALSE]
  d_vbg_i$w_rate <- w_vbg_i

  co2_rate_mi_rows_abg[[i]] <- compute_co2_bin_rates(
    df = d_abg_i |> dplyr::filter(has_abg == 1),
    co2_var = "paco2",
    outcomes = CO2_RATE_OUTCOMES,
    outcome_labels = CO2_RATE_OUTCOME_LABELS,



                                                         374
      weight_var = "w_rate",
      q = c(0.02, 0.98),
      bin_width = 1,
      cohort_label = "ABG"
    ) |> dplyr::mutate(imp = i)

    co2_rate_mi_rows_vbg[[i]] <- compute_co2_bin_rates(
      df = d_vbg_i |> dplyr::filter(has_vbg == 1),
      co2_var = "vbg_co2",
      outcomes = CO2_RATE_OUTCOMES,
      outcome_labels = CO2_RATE_OUTCOME_LABELS,
      weight_var = "w_rate",
      q = c(0.02, 0.98),
      bin_width = 1,
      cohort_label = "VBG"
    ) |> dplyr::mutate(imp = i)

    rm(d_i, d_abg_i, d_vbg_i, w_abg_i, w_vbg_i)
    invisible(gc(FALSE))
}

co2_rate_mi_abg <- pool_mi_bin_rates(dplyr::bind_rows(co2_rate_mi_rows_abg))
co2_rate_mi_vbg <- pool_mi_bin_rates(dplyr::bind_rows(co2_rate_mi_rows_vbg))

write_csv_safely(co2_rate_mi_abg, results_path("co2_binned_rates_mi_ipw_abg.csv"), row_names = FALSE)
write_csv_safely(co2_rate_mi_vbg, results_path("co2_binned_rates_mi_ipw_vbg.csv"), row_names = FALSE)

p_co2_rate_mi_abg <- plot_co2_bin_rate_panel(
  co2_rate_mi_abg,
  title = paste0("Observed outcome rates by ABG CO2 bin (MI-logistic IPSW, m = ", imp$m, ")"),
  x_label = "ABG CO2 (mmHg)",
  vline_at = 45
)
p_co2_rate_mi_vbg <- plot_co2_bin_rate_panel(
  co2_rate_mi_vbg,
  title = paste0("Observed outcome rates by VBG CO2 bin (MI-logistic IPSW, m = ", imp$m, ")"),




                                                          375
    x_label = "VBG CO2 (mmHg)",
    vline_at = 50
)

print_plot_once(p_co2_rate_mi_abg, "co2-binned-rates-mi-ipw-abg", width = 8.5, height = 6.0)
print_plot_once(p_co2_rate_mi_vbg, "co2-binned-rates-mi-ipw-vbg", width = 8.5, height = 6.0)

rm(co2_rate_mi_rows_abg, co2_rate_mi_rows_vbg, co2_rate_mi_abg, co2_rate_mi_vbg,
   p_co2_rate_mi_abg, p_co2_rate_mi_vbg)
invisible(gc(FALSE))


3.10 Manuscript outputs summary

# Use full-cohort flow counts here so manuscript-facing sample sizes remain
# stable in pilot renders and stay synchronized with Figure 1.
flow_tbl <- tibble::tibble(
  metric = c(
    "Extracted encounter cohort",
    "Ambulatory encounters excluded",
    "Analytic ED/inpatient cohort",
    "ABG-tested encounters",
    "VBG-tested encounters",
    "Both ABG and VBG",
    "ABG only",
    "VBG only",
    "Neither ABG nor VBG",
    "ABG with observed PaCO2",
    "VBG with observed CO2"
  ),
  n = c(
    cohort_flow_counts$total_extracted,
    cohort_flow_counts$excluded_ambulatory,
    cohort_flow_counts$analytic_ed_inpatient,
    cohort_flow_counts$abg_tested,

# Purpose: manuscript Figure S2 propensity-score overlap under the MI logistic IPSW models.
# Build an imputation-averaged propensity histogram for ABG and VBG.
# This mirrors the non-MI propensity display while respecting MI variability.
stopifnot(exists("imp"))
stopifnot(exists("mi_logistic_ps_abg_list"), exists("mi_logistic_ps_vbg_list"))

bin_edges <- seq(0, 1, length.out = 31)
bin_width <- diff(bin_edges)[1]
bin_centers <- head(bin_edges, -1) + bin_width / 2
treat_abg_all <- to01(imp$data$has_abg)
treat_vbg_all <- to01(imp$data$has_vbg)




                                                         382
# helper: collapse one imputation's propensity scores into comparable histogram
# bins so the manuscript figure can average densities across imputations without
# overplotting dozens of raw curves.
mi_ps_hist_one <- function(ps_vec, treat_vec, score_type, imp_index) {
  # Use integer bin IDs to avoid floating-point matching issues during complete().
  df <- data.frame(
    ps = as.numeric(ps_vec),
    treat = as.integer(treat_vec),
    stringsAsFactors = FALSE
  ) |>
    dplyr::filter(is.finite(ps), !is.na(treat), ps >= 0, ps <= 1) |>
    dplyr::mutate(
       treat = factor(treat, levels = c(0L, 1L), labels = c("No Test", "Test")),
       bin_id = cut(
         ps,
         breaks = bin_edges,
         include.lowest = TRUE,
         right = FALSE,
         labels = FALSE
       )
    )

  if (nrow(df) == 0 || all(is.na(df$bin_id))) return(data.frame())

  df |>
    dplyr::filter(!is.na(bin_id)) |>
    dplyr::count(treat, bin_id, .drop = FALSE, name = "n") |>
    tidyr::complete(treat, bin_id = seq_along(bin_centers), fill = list(n = 0L)) |>
    dplyr::group_by(treat) |>
    dplyr::mutate(
      n_total = sum(n, na.rm = TRUE),
      density = dplyr::if_else(n_total > 0, n / (n_total * bin_width), 0)
    ) |>
    dplyr::ungroup() |>
    dplyr::mutate(
      ScoreType = score_type,




                                                         383
      imp = imp_index,
      bin_mid = bin_centers[bin_id]
    ) |>
    dplyr::select(ScoreType, imp, treat, bin_mid, density)
}

mi_ps_hist_rows <- vector("list", imp$m * 2L)
row_idx <- 0L
for (i in seq_len(imp$m)) {
  # Aggregate ABG and VBG bin-level densities for each imputation.
  row_idx <- row_idx + 1L
  mi_ps_hist_rows[[row_idx]] <- mi_ps_hist_one(get_mi_ps("ABG", i), treat_abg_all, "ABG", i)
  row_idx <- row_idx + 1L
  mi_ps_hist_rows[[row_idx]] <- mi_ps_hist_one(get_mi_ps("VBG", i), treat_vbg_all, "VBG", i)
}

# Average densities across imputations to avoid overplotting 80+ curves.
mi_ps_hist <- dplyr::bind_rows(mi_ps_hist_rows) |>
  dplyr::group_by(ScoreType, treat, bin_mid) |>
  dplyr::summarise(density = mean(density, na.rm = TRUE), .groups = "drop") |>
  dplyr::mutate(ScoreType = factor(ScoreType, levels = c("ABG", "VBG")))

if (nrow(mi_ps_hist) > 0 && any(is.finite(mi_ps_hist$density) & mi_ps_hist$density > 0)) {
  # Render side-by-side ABG/VBG density histograms with shared x-range [0,1].
  mi_ps_hist_plot <- ggplot(mi_ps_hist, aes(x = bin_mid, y = density, fill = treat)) +
    geom_col(position = "identity", alpha = 0.5, width = bin_width * 0.95) +
    facet_wrap(~ ScoreType, scales = "free_y") +
    coord_cartesian(xlim = c(0, 1)) +
    scale_fill_manual(values = c("No Test" = "steelblue", "Test" = "tomato")) +
    labs(
      title = "Propensity-score overlap for MI logistic ABG and VBG test-ordering models",
      subtitle = paste0("Averaged across ", imp$m, " imputations"),
      x = "Propensity score",
      y = "Density",
      fill = "Group"
    ) +




                                                         384
   theme_pub(base_size = 12)

  print_plot_once(mi_ps_hist_plot, "propensity-histograms-mi-logistic", width = 8.5, height = 5)
} else {
  warning("MI propensity histogram has no positive density values; inspect mi_logistic_ps_* artifacts.", call. =
   ↪  FALSE)
}

fit_death_crude_abg <- fit_spline_glm("death_60d", "paco2", subset_data_abg, "ABG",
                                      adj_vars = NULL, analysis_variant = "crude")
fit_hcrf_crude_abg <- fit_spline_glm("hypercap_resp_failure", "paco2", subset_data_abg, "ABG",
                                     adj_vars = NULL, analysis_variant = "crude")
fit_imv_crude_vbg <- fit_spline_glm("imv_proc", "vbg_co2", subset_data_vbg, "VBG",
                                    adj_vars = NULL, analysis_variant = "crude")
fit_niv_crude_vbg <- fit_spline_glm("niv_proc", "vbg_co2", subset_data_vbg, "VBG",
                                    adj_vars = NULL, analysis_variant = "crude")
fit_death_crude_vbg <- fit_spline_glm("death_60d", "vbg_co2", subset_data_vbg, "VBG",
                                      adj_vars = NULL, analysis_variant = "crude")
fit_hcrf_crude_vbg <- fit_spline_glm("hypercap_resp_failure", "vbg_co2", subset_data_vbg, "VBG",
                                     adj_vars = NULL, analysis_variant = "crude")

if (any(vapply(
  list(
    fit_imv_crude_abg, fit_niv_crude_abg, fit_death_crude_abg, fit_hcrf_crude_abg,
    fit_imv_crude_vbg, fit_niv_crude_vbg, fit_death_crude_vbg, fit_hcrf_crude_vbg
  ),
  is.null,
  logical(1)
))) {
  stop("Crude key-results spline fits failed; see model_fit_diagnostics.csv.")
}

# helper: test whether one parity-audit artifact is present in the expected
# figures or results directory.
artifact_exists <- function(name, type) {
  if (is.na(name) || !nzchar(name)) return(FALSE)
  if (type == "figure") {
    fig_path <- results_path("figs", name)
    if (grepl("[*?\\[]", name)) return(length(Sys.glob(fig_path)) > 0)
    return(file.exists(fig_path))
  }
  file.exists(results_path(name))
}

parity_tbl <- dplyr::full_join(
  dplyr::rename(non_mi_ipw_outputs, non_mi_artifact = artifact_name, artifact_type_non_mi = artifact_type),
  dplyr::rename(mi_ipw_outputs, mi_artifact = artifact_name, artifact_type_mi = artifact_type),
  by = "parity_key"
) |>
  dplyr::mutate(
    artifact_type = dplyr::coalesce(artifact_type_non_mi, artifact_type_mi),
    present_non_mi = mapply(artifact_exists, non_mi_artifact, artifact_type, USE.NAMES = FALSE),
    present_mi = mapply(artifact_exists, mi_artifact, artifact_type, USE.NAMES = FALSE),




                                                           399
    parity_status = dplyr::case_when(
       present_non_mi & present_mi ~ "both",
       present_non_mi & !present_mi ~ "non_mi_only",
       !present_non_mi & present_mi ~ "mi_only",
       TRUE ~ "unknown"
    ),
    recommended_action = dplyr::case_when(
       parity_status == "both" ~ "none",
       parity_status == "non_mi_only" ~ "add MI equivalent output",
       parity_status == "mi_only" ~ "add non-MI equivalent output",
       TRUE ~ "review manually"
    )
  ) |>
  dplyr::arrange(artifact_type, parity_key) |>
  dplyr::select(parity_key, artifact_type, non_mi_artifact, mi_artifact,
                 present_non_mi, present_mi, parity_status, recommended_action)

write_csv_safely(parity_tbl, results_path("ipw_output_parity.csv"), row_names = FALSE)

parity_unknown <- parity_tbl |>
  dplyr::filter(parity_status == "unknown")
write_csv_safely(parity_unknown, results_path("ipw_output_parity_unknown.csv"), row_names = FALSE)
if (RUN_MODE == "full" && nrow(parity_unknown) > 0) {
  stop("Parity audit has unknown rows; see ", results_path("ipw_output_parity_unknown.csv"))
}

parity_one_sided <- parity_tbl |>
  dplyr::filter(parity_status != "both")

write_csv_safely(parity_one_sided, results_path("ipw_output_parity_diffs.csv"), row_names = FALSE)

  file_stub = "ipw_output_parity_one_sided",
  digits = 0,




                                                          400
    show = FALSE
)

role_for_var <- function(v) {
  roles <- character()
  if (v %in% adj_core) roles <- c(roles, "direct adjustment")
  if (v %in% covars_ps) roles <- c(roles, "PS model")
  if (!length(roles)) roles <- "auxiliary"
  paste(unique(roles), collapse = "; ")
}

  dplyr::select(.data$variable, .data$pct_missing)

  dplyr::left_join(missing_lookup, by = "variable") |>
  dplyr::mutate(
    variable = dplyr::recode(.data$variable, !!!baseline_role_labels, .default = .data$variable),
    `Analysis role` = vapply(baseline_role_vars, role_for_var, character(1L)),
    `% missing` = sprintf("%.1f%%", .data$pct_missing),
    `Imputed in primary MI` = dplyr::if_else(
       dplyr::coalesce(meth[baseline_role_vars], "") != "",
       "Yes",
       "No"
    )
  ) |>
  dplyr::select(.data$variable, .data$`Analysis role`, .data$`% missing`, .data$`Imputed in primary MI`) |>
  dplyr::rename(Variable = variable)

  grepl("separat", diag_df_for_s5$top_warning, ignore.case = TRUE)

  (diag_df_for_s5$max_phat > 1 - PROB_EPS)

  dplyr::coalesce(!as.logical(diag_df_for_s5$converged), FALSE)

safe_max <- function(x) {
  x <- x[is.finite(x)]
  if (!length(x)) return(NA_real_)
  max(x)
}

# Purpose: freeze manuscript-facing numbering, paths, aliases, and targeted duplicate cleanup.
# helper: delete only the known duplicate spill files for mapped supplement
# artifacts, leaving unrelated historical files untouched.
cleanup_targeted_supplement_duplicates <- function() {
  duplicate_map <- tibble::tribble(
    ~canonical_file, ~duplicate_file,
    results_path("figs", "propensity-histograms-conditional.png"), results_path("figs",
     ↪  "propensity-histograms-conditional-1.png"),
    results_path("figs", "shap-top10-ipw-gbm-abg-vbg.png"), results_path("figs", "shap-top10-ipw-gbm-display-1.png")



                                                           408
    )

    duplicate_map |>
      dplyr::rowwise() |>
      dplyr::mutate(
        remove_ok = file.exists(canonical_file) && file.exists(duplicate_file)
      ) |>
      dplyr::ungroup() |>
      dplyr::filter(remove_ok) |>
      dplyr::pull(duplicate_file) |>
      unique() |>
      (\(paths) {
        if (length(paths)) fs::file_delete(paths)
        invisible(paths)
      })()
}

cleanup_targeted_supplement_duplicates()

# helper: convert an internal absolute artifact path into the shorter manifest
# path used in CSV audits and drafting.
format_manifest_path <- function(path) {
  if (is.null(path) || is.na(path) || !nzchar(path)) return("")
  pretty_path(path)
}

# helper: split comma-separated extension declarations into a stable vector.
split_expected_extensions <- function(x) {
  if (is.null(x) || is.na(x) || !nzchar(x)) return(character(0))
  trimws(strsplit(x, ",", fixed = TRUE)[[1]]) |>
    (\(vals) vals[nzchar(vals)])()
}

# helper: write markdown reports without prepending the diagnostics log header.
write_markdown_report <- function(lines, path) {
  writeLines(lines, con = path)




                                                           409
    invisible(TRUE)
}

# helper: collapse repeated strings for compact audit detail columns.
collapse_unique_text <- function(x) {
  x <- unique(as.character(x))
  x <- x[!is.na(x) & nzchar(x)]
  paste(x, collapse = "; ")
}

# helper: write the manuscript-facing alias file(s) for one registered asset.
materialize_manuscript_alias <- function(kind, canonical_stub, alias_stub,
                                         canonical_subdir, alias_subdir) {
  if (kind == "figure") {
    return(write_plot_alias(canonical_stub, alias_stub, canonical_subdir, alias_subdir))
  }
  if (kind == "table") {
    return(write_table_alias(canonical_stub, alias_stub, canonical_subdir, alias_subdir))
  }
  stop("Unsupported artifact kind for manuscript alias: ", kind)
}

manuscript_asset_manifest_internal <- manuscript_asset_manifest_internal |>
  dplyr::rowwise() |>
  dplyr::mutate(




                                                         413
    alias_written = list(
       if (
         identical(status, "generated") &&
         !is.na(alias_stub) && nzchar(alias_stub) &&
         !is.na(canonical_stub) && nzchar(canonical_stub)
       ) {
         materialize_manuscript_alias(kind, canonical_stub, alias_stub, canonical_subdir, alias_subdir)
       } else {
         character(0)
       }
    )
  ) |>
  dplyr::ungroup() |>
  dplyr::mutate(
    canonical_artifact_path = vapply(canonical_artifact_file, format_manifest_path, character(1L)),
    alias_artifact_path = vapply(alias_artifact_file, format_manifest_path, character(1L))
  )

active_manuscript_assets <- manuscript_asset_manifest_internal |>
  dplyr::filter(status != "draft_only")

generated_manuscript_assets <- active_manuscript_assets |>
  dplyr::filter(status == "generated")

numbering_conflicts <- active_manuscript_assets |>
  dplyr::count(numbering_slot, name = "n_assets") |>
  dplyr::filter(n_assets > 1L)

alias_conflicts <- generated_manuscript_assets |>
  dplyr::filter(!is.na(alias_stub), nzchar(alias_stub)) |>
  dplyr::count(alias_subdir, alias_stub, name = "n_assets") |>
  dplyr::filter(n_assets > 1L)

  dplyr::count(canonical_subdir, canonical_stub, name = "n_assets") |>

duplicate_asset_audit <- dplyr::bind_rows(
  tibble::tibble(
    audit_scope = "numbering_slot",
    audit_key = if (nrow(numbering_conflicts)) numbering_conflicts$numbering_slot else "all_active_slots",
    status = if (nrow(numbering_conflicts)) "conflict" else "pass",
    severity = if (nrow(numbering_conflicts)) "high" else "none",
    n_rows = if (nrow(numbering_conflicts)) numbering_conflicts$n_assets else 0L,
    detail = if (nrow(numbering_conflicts)) "Multiple active assets share one manuscript numbering slot." else "No
     ↪  contradictory active numbering slots detected."
  ),
  tibble::tibble(
    audit_scope = "alias_stub",
    audit_key = if (nrow(alias_conflicts)) paste0(alias_conflicts$alias_subdir, "::", alias_conflicts$alias_stub) else
     ↪  "all_aliases",
    status = if (nrow(alias_conflicts)) "conflict" else "pass",
    severity = if (nrow(alias_conflicts)) "high" else "none",
    n_rows = if (nrow(alias_conflicts)) alias_conflicts$n_assets else 0L,
    detail = if (nrow(alias_conflicts)) "Multiple active assets share one manuscript-facing alias." else "No
     ↪  conflicting manuscript alias stubs detected."
  ),
  tibble::tibble(
    audit_scope = "canonical_stub",
    audit_key = if (nrow(canonical_conflicts)) paste0(canonical_conflicts$canonical_subdir, "::",
     ↪  canonical_conflicts$canonical_stub) else "all_canonical_stubs",




                                                         415
      status = if (nrow(canonical_conflicts)) "conflict" else "pass",
      severity = if (nrow(canonical_conflicts)) "high" else "none",
      n_rows = if (nrow(canonical_conflicts)) canonical_conflicts$n_assets else 0L,
      detail = if (nrow(canonical_conflicts)) "Multiple active assets share one canonical artifact stub." else "No
       ↪  conflicting canonical artifact stubs detected."
    ),
    tibble::tibble(
      audit_scope = "deprecated_slot",
      audit_key = "Figure 3",

       ↪  else "Deprecated Figure 3 numbering is suppressed."

build_artifact_check_rows <- function(row) {
  row <- as.list(row)
  if (identical(row$status, "generated")) {
    roles <- list(
      canonical = list(stub = row$canonical_stub, subdir = row$canonical_subdir),
      alias = list(stub = row$alias_stub, subdir = row$alias_subdir)
    )
    return(
      purrr::imap_dfr(roles, function(info, artifact_role) {
        if (is.null(info$stub) || is.na(info$stub) || !nzchar(info$stub)) {
          return(tibble::tibble())
        }
        purrr::map_dfr(row$expected_extension_list[[1]], function(ext) {




                                                         417
          artifact_path <- artifact_file_path(info$stub, ext, info$subdir)
          exists_flag <- file.exists(artifact_path)
          tibble::tibble(
            manuscript_label = row$manuscript_label_safe,
            numbering_slot = row$numbering_slot,
            kind = row$kind,
            section = row$section,
            artifact_role = artifact_role,
            ext = ext,
            artifact_path = format_manifest_path(artifact_path),
            exists = exists_flag,
            source_type = row$source_type,
            required_in_validation = row$required_in_validation,
            pdf_display = row$pdf_display,
            allowed_missing = FALSE,
            check_status = dplyr::if_else(exists_flag, "present", "missing_required"),
            severity = dplyr::if_else(exists_flag, "none", row$missing_artifact_severity),
            notes = row$notes
          )
     })
   })
  )
}
if (identical(row$status, "external/manual")) {
  return(
    tibble::tibble(
      manuscript_label = row$manuscript_label_safe,
      numbering_slot = row$numbering_slot,
      kind = row$kind,
      section = row$section,
      artifact_role = "external/manual",
      ext = "",
      artifact_path = "",
      exists = NA,
      source_type = row$source_type,
      required_in_validation = row$required_in_validation,




                                                         418
             pdf_display = row$pdf_display,
             allowed_missing = TRUE,
             check_status = "external_manual_declared",
             severity = row$missing_artifact_severity,
             notes = row$notes
         )
     )
    }
    tibble::tibble(
      manuscript_label = row$manuscript_label_safe,
      numbering_slot = row$numbering_slot,
      kind = row$kind,
      section = row$section,
      artifact_role = "suppressed",
      ext = "",
      artifact_path = "",
      exists = NA,
      source_type = row$source_type,
      required_in_validation = row$required_in_validation,
      pdf_display = row$pdf_display,
      allowed_missing = TRUE,
      check_status = "suppressed_draft_only",
      severity = "none",
      notes = row$notes
    )
}

                                                           424
# Purpose: define the canonical manuscript-facing display helpers used later in the validation section.
manifest_row <- function(label) {
  row <- manuscript_asset_manifest_internal |>
    dplyr::filter(manuscript_label_safe == safe_manuscript_text(label))
  if (nrow(row) != 1L) stop("Expected exactly one manifest row for ", label)
  row
}

# helper: resolve the display-ready figure path for one manifest label.
# LaTeX/PDF renders must fail fast if the manuscript PDF artifact is missing.
manifest_figure_path <- function(label) {
  row <- manifest_row(label)
  ext <- if (knitr::is_latex_output()) "pdf" else "png"
  stub <- if (!is.na(row$alias_stub) && nzchar(row$alias_stub)) row$alias_stub else row$canonical_stub
  subdir <- if (!is.na(row$alias_subdir) && nzchar(row$alias_subdir)) row$alias_subdir else row$canonical_subdir
  path <- artifact_file_path(stub, ext, subdir)
  if (knitr::is_latex_output() && !file.exists(path)) {
    stop("Missing PDF display artifact for ", label, ": ", path)
  }
  if (!file.exists(path)) stop("Missing display artifact for ", label, ": ", path)
  path
}

manuscript_figure_notes <- list(
  "Figure 2" = key_results_caption_main,
  "Figure S4" = key_results_cat3_caption_main,
  "Figure S5" = key_results_caption_adjusted
)

# helper: render explanatory manuscript notes as Quarto text below figures
# instead of embedding long text inside the plot canvas.
render_manuscript_note <- function(label) {
  note <- manuscript_figure_notes[[label]]
  if (is.null(note) || !nzchar(note)) return("")
  note <- paste0("Note: ", note)
  if (knitr::is_latex_output()) {




                                                         425
     return(paste0(
        "\\par\\vspace{0.5em}\\noindent\\footnotesize ",
        latex_safe_table_text(escape_latex_text(note)),
        "\\normalsize"
     ))
    }
    paste0("*", note, "*")
}

# helper: insert one manifest-registered figure into the rendered notebook in
# official manuscript order, independent of generation chunk order.
render_manuscript_figure <- function(label, width = "0.88\\linewidth") {
  row <- manifest_row(label)
  fig_path <- manifest_figure_path(label)
  caption_text <- row$caption_safe[[1]]
  if (knitr::is_latex_output()) {
    latex_caption <- escape_latex_text(caption_text)
    latex_path <- display_path(fig_path)
    out <- c(
      "\\clearpage",
      "\\begin{center}",
      "\\begin{minipage}{\\linewidth}",
      "\\centering",
      sprintf("\\small %s\\par", latex_caption),
      "\\vspace{0.5em}",
      sprintf("\\includegraphics[width=%s,height=0.82\\textheight,keepaspectratio]{%s}", width, latex_path),
      render_manuscript_note(label),
      "\\end{minipage}",
      "\\end{center}"
    )
    knitr::asis_output(paste(out, collapse = "\n"))
  } else {
    knitr::asis_output(
      paste0("![](", display_path(fig_path), ")\n\n*", caption_text, "*\n\n", render_manuscript_note(label), "\n")
    )
  }




                                                           426
}

# helper: render one manifest-registered table with its manuscript label and
# title while reusing the standard standalone-table path.
render_manifest_table <- function(label, df, file_stub, wide = FALSE, digits = 2,
                                  max_cols = 6, landscape = NULL) {
  row <- manifest_row(label)
  render_table_pdf(
    df,
    caption = row$title_safe[[1]],
    file_stub = file_stub,
    wide = wide,
    digits = digits,
    max_cols = max_cols,
    landscape = landscape,
    display_label = label,
    caption_mode = "plain",
    page_break_before = TRUE
  )
}

render_manifest_panel_table <- function(label, panels, file_stub, digits = 2,
                                        landscape = TRUE, csv_df = NULL) {
  row <- manifest_row(label)
  render_panel_table_pdf(
    panels,
    caption = row$title_safe[[1]],
    file_stub = file_stub,
    digits = digits,
    display_label = label,
    landscape = landscape,
    page_break_before = TRUE,
    csv_df = csv_df
  )
}

# helper: coerce manifest tables into a stable all-character form before
# comparison so NA handling and tibble/data.frame differences do not create
# false assertion failures.
normalize_manifest_strings <- function(df) {
  tibble::as_tibble(df) |>
    dplyr::mutate(
      dplyr::across(
        dplyr::everything(),
        ~ dplyr::if_else(is.na(.x), "", as.character(.x))
      )
    )
}
supplement_manifest_analysis_family_ok <- "analysis_family" %in% names(supplement_manifest_actual) &&




                                                         431
  all(nzchar(as.character(supplement_manifest_actual$analysis_family)))
supplement_manifest_matches <- supplement_manifest_analysis_family_ok && all(
  supplement_manifest_compare_cols %in% names(supplement_manifest_actual)
) && identical(
  normalize_manifest_strings(dplyr::select(supplement_manifest_expected,
   ↪  dplyr::all_of(supplement_manifest_compare_cols))),
  normalize_manifest_strings(supplement_manifest_actual) |>
    dplyr::select(dplyr::all_of(supplement_manifest_compare_cols))
)

4.0.2 MI stability across m

# Purpose: diagnostics mi stability.
stopifnot(exists("imp"))
stopifnot(exists("mi_logistic_ps_abg_list"), exists("mi_logistic_ps_vbg_list"))

# helper: trim a `mids` object down to its first `m_keep` imputations for
# stability diagnostics across different values of m.
subset_mids <- function(imp_obj, m_keep) {
  if (imp_obj$m == m_keep) return(imp_obj)
  idx <- seq_len(m_keep)
  imp_new <- imp_obj
  imp_new$imp <- lapply(imp_obj$imp, function(x) x[, idx, drop = FALSE])
  imp_new$m <- m_keep
  imp_new
}

m_vals <- sort(unique(c(20, 50, M_IMP)))
m_vals <- m_vals[m_vals <= imp$m]

med_abg <- median(subset_data$paco2[subset_data$has_abg == 1 & !is.na(subset_data$paco2)], na.rm = TRUE)
med_vbg <- median(subset_data$vbg_co2[subset_data$has_vbg == 1 & !is.na(subset_data$vbg_co2)], na.rm = TRUE)
if (!is.finite(med_abg)) med_abg <- ABG_CO2_REF
if (!is.finite(med_vbg)) med_vbg <- VBG_CO2_REF
grid_abg_info_m <- make_co2_grid_ref("paco2", c(med_abg, ABG_CO2_REF), x_ref_abg, ABG_CO2_REF)
grid_vbg_info_m <- make_co2_grid_ref("vbg_co2", c(med_vbg, VBG_CO2_REF), x_ref_vbg, VBG_CO2_REF)
grid_abg_m <- grid_abg_info_m$grid
grid_vbg_m <- grid_vbg_info_m$grid
ref_idx_abg_m <- grid_abg_info_m$ref_idx
ref_idx_vbg_m <- grid_vbg_info_m$ref_idx
med_idx_abg <- match(med_abg, grid_abg_m$paco2)
med_idx_vbg <- match(med_vbg, grid_vbg_m$vbg_co2)
if (is.na(med_idx_abg)) med_idx_abg <- which.min(abs(grid_abg_m$paco2 - med_abg))
if (is.na(med_idx_vbg)) med_idx_vbg <- which.min(abs(grid_vbg_m$vbg_co2 - med_vbg))



                                                         438
stab_rows <- lapply(m_vals, function(mv) {
  imp_m <- subset_mids(imp, mv)
  get_imp_m <- function(i) normalize_types(mice::complete(imp_m, action = i), levels_ref)

  fits_abg <- lapply(seq_len(mv), function(i) {
    d <- get_imp_m(i)
    d <- d[, c("imv_proc", "has_abg", "paco2", adj_core), drop = FALSE]
    tryCatch(
      fit_spline_imp(
        d, get_mi_weight("ABG", i), "imv_proc", "paco2", "has_abg",
        adj_vars = adj_core,
        spline_df = SPLINE_DF, spline_basis = SPLINE_BASIS, grid_df = grid_abg_m,
        ref_idx = ref_idx_abg_m,
        imp_index = i
      ),
      error = function(e) list(error = conditionMessage(e))
    )
  })
  collect_warnings_from_list(fits_abg)
  curve_abg <- pool_spline_curve(fits_abg, grid_abg_m, ref_idx_abg_m, ABG_CO2_REF,
                                 min_ok_frac = 0.9)

  fits_vbg <- lapply(seq_len(mv), function(i) {
    d <- get_imp_m(i)
    d <- d[, c("imv_proc", "has_vbg", "vbg_co2", adj_core), drop = FALSE]
    tryCatch(
      fit_spline_imp(
        d, get_mi_weight("VBG", i), "imv_proc", "vbg_co2", "has_vbg",
        adj_vars = adj_core,
        spline_df = SPLINE_DF, spline_basis = SPLINE_BASIS, grid_df = grid_vbg_m,
        ref_idx = ref_idx_vbg_m,
        imp_index = i
      ),
      error = function(e) list(error = conditionMessage(e))
    )




                                                         439
     })
     collect_warnings_from_list(fits_vbg)
     curve_vbg <- pool_spline_curve(fits_vbg, grid_vbg_m, ref_idx_vbg_m, VBG_CO2_REF,
                                    min_ok_frac = 0.9)

     bind_rows(
       tibble::tibble(group = "ABG", m = mv, OR = curve_abg$OR[med_idx_abg]),
       tibble::tibble(group = "VBG", m = mv, OR = curve_vbg$OR[med_idx_vbg])
     )
})

stab_df <- bind_rows(stab_rows)
ref <- stab_df |> filter(m == max(m_vals)) |> select(group, OR) |> rename(OR_ref = OR)
stab_df <- stab_df |>
  left_join(ref, by = "group") |>
  mutate(abs_diff = OR - OR_ref,
         pct_diff = 100 * (OR - OR_ref) / OR_ref)

stab_file <- results_path("mi_m_stability.csv")
write_csv_safely(stab_df, stab_file, row_names = FALSE)

# FMI / relative efficiency for a representative unweighted model
append_mem_snapshot("diagnostics", "mi_fmi_glm", "pre")
# This diagnostic previously used with(imp, glm(...)) which can materialize large
# completed-data objects. We pool a single coefficient via pool.scalar() instead.
fmi_formula <- imv_proc ~ has_abg + age_at_encounter + sex
fmi_vars <- all.vars(fmi_formula)
qhat <- rep(NA_real_, imp$m)
uhat <- rep(NA_real_, imp$m)
for (i in seq_len(imp$m)) {
  d_i <- mice::complete(imp, action = i)
  d_i <- d_i[, intersect(fmi_vars, names(d_i)), drop = FALSE]
  if (!all(c("imv_proc", "has_abg", "age_at_encounter", "sex") %in% names(d_i))) {
    next
  }
  cap_fit <- capture_warnings(




                                                            440
 glm(
    formula = fmi_formula,
    data = d_i,
    family = binomial(),
    model = FALSE,
    x = FALSE,
    y = FALSE
 ),
 context = make_context(
    stage = "diagnostics",
    component = "mi_fmi_glm",
    analysis_variant = "mi",
    model_type = "glm",
    group = NA_character_,
    outcome = "imv_proc",
    imputation = i,
    batch = NA_integer_
 )
)
append_warnings(cap_fit$warnings)
fit_i <- cap_fit$value
if (!is.null(fit_i)) {
  coef_i <- stats::coef(fit_i)
  vcov_i <- tryCatch(stats::vcov(fit_i), error = function(e) NULL)
  if (
    "has_abg" %in% names(coef_i) &&
    !is.null(vcov_i) &&
    "has_abg" %in% rownames(vcov_i) &&
    "has_abg" %in% colnames(vcov_i)
  ) {
    qhat[i] <- unname(coef_i[["has_abg"]])
    uhat[i] <- unname(vcov_i["has_abg", "has_abg"])
  }
}
rm(list = intersect(c("d_i", "cap_fit", "fit_i", "coef_i", "vcov_i"), ls()))
invisible(gc(FALSE))




                                                       441
}
ok <- is.finite(qhat) & is.finite(uhat) & uhat > 0
if (sum(ok) >= 2) {
  ps <- mice::pool.scalar(
    Q = qhat[ok],
    U = uhat[ok],
    n = sum(subset_data$has_abg == 1, na.rm = TRUE),
    k = 1
  )
  fmi_abg <- tibble::tibble(
    term = "has_abg",
    estimate = ps$qbar,
    std.error = sqrt(ps$t),
    fmi = ps$fmi,
    m_used = sum(ok)
  )
} else {
  warning("FMI not available from pooled scalar diagnostic; leaving FMI as NA.", call. = FALSE)
  fmi_abg <- tibble::tibble(
    term = "has_abg",
    estimate = NA_real_,
    std.error = NA_real_,
    fmi = NA_real_,
    m_used = sum(ok)
  )
}
fmi_abg$rel_eff <- if (is.finite(fmi_abg$fmi[1])) 1 / (1 + fmi_abg$fmi[1] / M_IMP) else NA_real_
append_mem_snapshot("diagnostics", "mi_fmi_glm", "post")

mean_across_imps <- function(imp_obj, var) {
  means <- vapply(seq_len(imp_obj$m), function(i) {
    d <- mice::complete(imp_obj, action = i)
    mean(d[[var]], na.rm = TRUE)
  }, numeric(1))
  mean(means, na.rm = TRUE)
}




                                                       444
    key_vars <- intersect(c("curr_bmi", "serum_hco3", "sodium", "serum_cr"), names(mi_df_sens))
    sens_df <- lapply(key_vars, function(v) {
      m_short <- mean_across_imps(imp_short, v)
      m_long <- mean_across_imps(imp_long, v)
      data.frame(
        variable = v,
        mean_short = m_short,
        mean_long = m_long,
        diff       = m_long - m_short,
        stringsAsFactors = FALSE
      )
    }) |> bind_rows()

    sens_file <- results_path("mi_maxit_sensitivity.csv")
    write_csv_safely(sens_df, sens_file, row_names = FALSE)
}

# helper: summarize propensity-score overlap numerically for one tested cohort.
ps_stat <- function(ps, group) {
  ps_ok <- ps[is.finite(ps)]
  if (!length(ps_ok)) {
    return(data.frame(
       group = group,
       ps_min = NA_real_,
       ps_p01 = NA_real_,
       ps_p50 = NA_real_,
       ps_p99 = NA_real_,
       ps_max = NA_real_,
       stringsAsFactors = FALSE
    ))
  }
  data.frame(
    group = group,
    ps_min = min(ps_ok, na.rm = TRUE),
    ps_p01 = stats::quantile(ps_ok, 0.01, na.rm = TRUE),
    ps_p50 = stats::median(ps_ok, na.rm = TRUE),
    ps_p99 = stats::quantile(ps_ok, 0.99, na.rm = TRUE),
    ps_max = max(ps_ok, na.rm = TRUE),
    stringsAsFactors = FALSE
  )
}

ps_summary <- dplyr::bind_rows(
  ps_stat(ps_abg, "ABG"),
  ps_stat(ps_vbg, "VBG")
)
write_csv_safely(ps_summary, results_path("ps_overlap_summary.csv"), row_names = FALSE)
render_table_pdf_maybe(
  ps_summary,
  caption = "GBM IPSW propensity-score overlap summary (tested cohort)",
  file_stub = "ps_overlap_summary",

                                                         446

# helper: draw a simple histogram of stabilized weights for one cohort.
plot_hist <- function(df, title) {
  ggplot(df, aes(x = weight)) +
    geom_histogram(bins = 40, fill = "grey70", color = "white") +
    labs(title = title, x = "Weight", y = "Count") +
    theme_pub(base_size = 10)
}

p_hist_abg <- plot_hist(filter(wt_df, group == "ABG"), "ABG weight distribution")
p_hist_vbg <- plot_hist(filter(wt_df, group == "VBG"), "VBG weight distribution")
save_diag_plot(p_hist_abg, results_path("figs", "diag-wt-weights-hist-abg.png"), width = 7, height = 5)
save_diag_plot(p_hist_vbg, results_path("figs", "diag-wt-weights-hist-vbg.png"), width = 7, height = 5)

# helper: visualize the relationship between propensities and resulting weights
# while highlighting the most extreme weights.
plot_scatter <- function(df, title) {
  top_wt <- df |>
    slice_max(order_by = weight, n = min(20, nrow(df)))
  ggplot(df, aes(x = ps, y = weight)) +
    geom_point(alpha = 0.3, size = 0.7) +
    geom_point(data = top_wt, color = "red", size = 1.2) +
    scale_y_log10() +
    labs(title = title, x = "Propensity score", y = "Weight (log10)") +
    theme_pub(base_size = 10)
}

p_scatter_abg <- plot_scatter(filter(wt_df, group == "ABG"),




                                                         447
                              "ABG weights vs propensity (top 20 highlighted)")

                              "VBG weights vs propensity (top 20 highlighted)")

4.0.4 Balance diagnostics

# Purpose: diagnostics balance.
stopifnot(exists("target_balance_table"))

covars_use <- intersect(covars_ps, names(subset_data))

bal_target_abg <- target_balance_table(subset_data, "has_abg", subset_data$w_abg, covars_use, levels_ref) |>
  mutate(group = "ABG")
bal_target_vbg <- target_balance_table(subset_data, "has_vbg", subset_data$w_vbg, covars_use, levels_ref) |>
  mutate(group = "VBG")

bal_target <- bind_rows(bal_target_abg, bal_target_vbg)
write_csv_safely(bal_target, results_path("balance_table.csv"), row_names = FALSE)

bal_target_sum <- bal_target |>
  group_by(group, variable) |>
  summarise(
    max_abs_pre = max(abs(smd_pre), na.rm = TRUE),
    max_abs_post = max(abs(smd_post), na.rm = TRUE),
    .groups = "drop"
  )
bal_worst <- bal_target_sum |>
  group_by(group) |>

runtime_proj_total_hrs <- NA_real_



                                                          452
if (is.finite(PILOT_FRAC) && PILOT_FRAC > 0 && PILOT_FRAC < 1) {
  runtime_log_curr <- runtime_log
  runtime_log_curr <- runtime_log_curr[runtime_log_curr$run_id == runtime_run_id, , drop = FALSE]
  scalable_steps <- c("mice_imputation", "mi_single_pass")
  scalable_secs <- runtime_log_curr |>
    dplyr::filter(step_name %in% scalable_steps) |>
    dplyr::summarise(total = sum(seconds, na.rm = TRUE)) |>
    dplyr::pull(total)
  if (length(scalable_secs) && is.finite(scalable_secs)) {
    runtime_proj_total_hrs <- scalable_secs / PILOT_FRAC / 3600
  }
}

# helper: pull one group's summary row out of the weight diagnostics table and
# fail loudly if it is missing.
get_wt_row <- function(group) {
  row <- wt_sum[wt_sum$group == group, , drop = FALSE]
  if (nrow(row) == 0L) {
    stop("Weight summary missing for group: ", group)
  }
  row[, c("ps_floor", "p01", "p05", "p95", "p99", "max", "sum_w", "ess",
          "top01_weight_share", "trunc_rate"), drop = FALSE]
}

audit_lines <- c(
  "# Diagnostics Audit",
  "",
  "## A1. MI workflow",
  "- Impute -> single-pass per‑imputation loop (weights, target balance, 3‑level outcomes, spline outcomes) -> pool
   ↪  curves and coefficients with Rubin’s rules (chunk: `mi-single-pass`; downstream MI display chunks read those
   ↪  objects).",
  "## A2. MI settings",
  paste0("- m = ", M_IMP, ", maxit = ", MAXIT_MI, ", seed = ", MI_SEED,
         "; treatments/outcomes/PaCO2/VBG CO2 are not imputed but are predictors (`mi-exec`)."),
  "## A3. Propensity weighting",
  "- Unimputed weighting uses WeightIt with method = \"gbm\" and balance-based stopping (stop.method = \"smd.max\");
   ↪  no AUC-based tuning (`propensity-config`, `ipw-abg-weighting`, `ipw-vbg-workflow`).",
  "- MI weighting uses logistic PS with restricted cubic splines (glm + rcs); no SHAP is computed for MI.",
  "## A4. One-sided IPSW + truncation",
  "- Weights are 1/ps for observed tests (ABG or VBG), truncated only for very small propensities (ps floor = 1st
   ↪  percentile), then stabilized by the mean; controls receive weight 1 for balance diagnostics only.",
  "## A5. Robust variance",
  "- Outcome models are survey::svyglm with svydesign (robust SEs), using spline(CO2) + X adjustment; ABG and VBG are
   ↪  fit separately within the measured cohort.",
  "## A6. Pooling",
  "- mitools::MIcombine pools coefficients and robust vcov from svyglm; spline curves are pooled pointwise on log-OR
   ↪  (relative to CO2_ref) and on eta for predicted-probability curves (helpers defined in `mi-single-pass`).",
  "",
  "## Potential mismatches / risks",
  "- Target balance diagnostics compare weighted treated cohort to the full analytic sample (no treated-vs-control
   ↪  balance).",
  "- MI stability across m uses subsets of the first m imputations from the main mids object (not full re-imputation
   ↪  at each m).",
  "- Unweighted analyses remain earlier in the notebook for context; primary inference is based on weighted spline
   ↪  models."
)
audit_file <- results_path("diagnostics_audit.md")

    .groups = "drop"
  )

5 Analysis of the discordance between predicted probabilities and OR for NIV and IMV

This section is diagnostic and additive. It does not change the primary manuscript estimates; instead it reproduces the NIV/IMV probability-
OR discordance and checks whether it is explained by reference profiles, probability scale, residual capture/missingness, sentinel procedure
capture, support, setting/site, subgroup, or timing structure.


5.1 Pilot validation and scope

# Purpose: additive diagnostics for NIV/IMV probability-OR discordance.
discordance_outcome_vars <- c("imv_proc", "niv_proc")
discordance_outcome_labels <- c(imv_proc = "IMV", niv_proc = "NIV")
discordance_groups <- c("ABG", "VBG")

safe_relative_gap <- function(abg_value, vbg_value) {
  ifelse(is.finite(vbg_value) & abs(vbg_value) > 0,
         (abg_value - vbg_value) / abs(vbg_value),
         NA_real_)
}

weighted_mean_safe <- function(x, w = NULL) {
  x <- suppressWarnings(as.numeric(x))
  if (is.null(w)) {
    return(mean(x, na.rm = TRUE))
  }
  w <- suppressWarnings(as.numeric(w))
  ok <- is.finite(x) & is.finite(w) & w > 0




                                                           466
    if (!any(ok)) return(NA_real_)
    sum(w[ok] * x[ok]) / sum(w[ok])
}

weighted_ess <- function(w) {
  w <- suppressWarnings(as.numeric(w))
  w <- w[is.finite(w) & w > 0]
  if (!length(w)) return(NA_real_)
  sum(w)^2 / sum(w^2)
}

first_existing_col <- function(candidates, data_names) {
  hits <- candidates[candidates %in% data_names]
  if (length(hits)) hits[[1L]] else NA_character_
}

candidate_cols <- function(data_names, pattern, exclude = character(), max_n = Inf) {
  out <- grep(pattern, data_names, value = TRUE, ignore.case = TRUE, perl = TRUE)
  out <- setdiff(out, exclude)
  unique(utils::head(out, max_n))
}

safe_max_numeric <- function(x) {
  x <- suppressWarnings(as.numeric(x))
  x <- x[is.finite(x)]
  if (!length(x)) return(NA_real_)
  max(x)
}

safe_max_abs_numeric <- function(x) {
  x <- suppressWarnings(as.numeric(x))
  x <- x[is.finite(x)]
  if (!length(x)) return(NA_real_)
  max(abs(x))
}




                                                           467

  x <- suppressWarnings(as.numeric(x))
  x <- x[is.finite(x)]
  if (!length(x)) return(NA_real_)
  stats::median(x)
}
