parse_discordance_time_detail <- function(x, field = "", reference_date = NULL) {
  empty_time <- as.POSIXct(rep(NA_character_, length(x)), tz = "UTC")
  n_present <- sum(!is.na(x))
  status_for <- function(parsed) {
    dplyr::case_when(
      n_present == 0L ~ "all_missing",
      sum(!is.na(parsed)) > 0L ~ "parsed",
      TRUE ~ "unparsed"
    )
  }

  if (inherits(x, "POSIXt")) {
    parsed <- as.POSIXct(x, tz = "UTC")
    return(list(parsed = parsed, parse_method = "posix_input", parse_status = status_for(parsed)))
  }
  if (inherits(x, "Date")) {
    parsed <- as.POSIXct(x, tz = "UTC")
    return(list(parsed = parsed, parse_method = "date_input", parse_status = status_for(parsed)))
  }

  if (is.numeric(x)) {
    x_num <- suppressWarnings(as.numeric(x))
    field_label <- attr(x, "label", exact = TRUE)
    if (is.null(field_label)) field_label <- ""




                                                         468
    field_text <- tolower(paste(field, field_label, collapse = " "))
    date_like_field <- grepl("date|time|timestamp|datetime", field, ignore.case = TRUE)
    encounter_offset_hint <- grepl(
      "encounter.?day|during the encounter|relative to encounter|\\(encounter|encounter-year-month",
      field_text,
      perl = TRUE
    )
    has_reference_date <- !is.null(reference_date) && length(reference_date) == length(x)
    small_day_offset <- any(is.finite(x_num)) &&
      suppressWarnings(max(abs(x_num[is.finite(x_num)]), na.rm = TRUE)) <= 3660

    if (has_reference_date && date_like_field && (encounter_offset_hint || small_day_offset)) {
      parsed <- as.POSIXct(as.Date(reference_date) + x_num, tz = "UTC")
      return(list(parsed = parsed, parse_method = "numeric_encounter_day_offset", parse_status = status_for(parsed)))
    }
    if (date_like_field && any(is.finite(x_num)) &&
        suppressWarnings(stats::median(x_num[is.finite(x_num)], na.rm = TRUE)) > 1000 &&
        suppressWarnings(stats::median(x_num[is.finite(x_num)], na.rm = TRUE)) < 50000) {
      parsed <- as.POSIXct(as.Date(x_num, origin = "1960-01-01"), tz = "UTC")
      return(list(parsed = parsed, parse_method = "numeric_stata_date", parse_status = status_for(parsed)))
    }
    if (date_like_field && any(is.finite(x_num)) &&
        suppressWarnings(stats::median(x_num[is.finite(x_num)], na.rm = TRUE)) > 1e11) {
      parsed <- as.POSIXct(x_num / 1000, origin = "1970-01-01", tz = "UTC")
      return(list(parsed = parsed, parse_method = "numeric_unix_milliseconds", parse_status = status_for(parsed)))
    }
    if (date_like_field && any(is.finite(x_num)) &&
        suppressWarnings(stats::median(x_num[is.finite(x_num)], na.rm = TRUE)) > 1e8) {
      parsed <- as.POSIXct(x_num, origin = "1970-01-01", tz = "UTC")
      return(list(parsed = parsed, parse_method = "numeric_unix_seconds", parse_status = status_for(parsed)))
    }
    return(list(parsed = empty_time, parse_method = "unparsed_numeric", parse_status = status_for(empty_time)))
}

x_chr <- trimws(as.character(x))
x_chr[!nzchar(x_chr)] <- NA_character_




                                                         469
    parsed <- tryCatch(
      suppressWarnings(as.POSIXct(x_chr, tz = "UTC")),
      error = function(e) empty_time
    )
    parse_method <- "character_posix"
    if (all(is.na(parsed)) && any(!is.na(x_chr))) {
      parsed <- tryCatch(
        suppressWarnings(as.POSIXct(as.Date(x_chr), tz = "UTC")),
        error = function(e) empty_time
      )
      parse_method <- "character_date"
    }
    if (all(is.na(parsed)) && any(!is.na(x_chr))) parse_method <- "unparsed_character"
    list(parsed = parsed, parse_method = parse_method, parse_status = status_for(parsed))
}

parse_discordance_time <- function(x, field = "", reference_date = NULL) {
  parse_discordance_time_detail(x, field = field, reference_date = reference_date)$parsed
}

discordance_field_activity <- function(x, field = "", role = c("activity", "timestamp"), reference_date = NULL) {
  role <- match.arg(role)
  if (role == "timestamp") {
    return(as.numeric(!is.na(parse_discordance_time(x, field = field, reference_date = reference_date))))
  }
  if (is.logical(x)) {
    return(as.numeric(!is.na(x) & x))
  }
  if (is.factor(x) || is.character(x)) {
    raw <- trimws(as.character(x))
    raw_lower <- tolower(raw)
    inactive <- is.na(raw) | !nzchar(raw) |
      raw_lower %in% c("0", "0.0", "no", "false", "absent", "none", "na", "n/a", "unknown")
    num <- suppressWarnings(as.numeric(raw))
    return(as.numeric(!inactive & (is.na(num) | num > 0)))
  }




                                                           470
    num <- suppressWarnings(as.numeric(x))
    as.numeric(is.finite(num) & num > 0)
}

count_active_fields <- function(data, fields, role = c("activity", "timestamp"), reference_date = NULL) {
  if (!length(fields)) return(rep(NA_real_, nrow(data)))
  role <- match.arg(role)
  active <- do.call(
    cbind,
    lapply(
      fields,
      function(field) discordance_field_activity(data[[field]], field = field, role = role, reference_date =
       ↪   reference_date)
    )
  )
  rowSums(active, na.rm = TRUE)
}

any_active_fields <- function(data, fields, role = c("activity", "timestamp"), reference_date = NULL) {
  if (!length(fields)) return(rep(NA_real_, nrow(data)))
  role <- match.arg(role)
  as.numeric(count_active_fields(data, fields, role = role, reference_date = reference_date) > 0)
}

compact_spline_fit <- function(x) {
  if (is.list(x) && !is.null(x$fit) && is.list(x$fit) &&
      !is.null(x$fit$coef) && !is.null(x$fit$vcov)) {
    return(x$fit)
  }
  if (is.list(x) && !is.null(x$coef) && !is.null(x$vcov)) {
    return(x)
  }
  NULL
}

predict_spline_prob_from_compact <- function(fit_compact, grid_df,




                                                         471
                                           outcome_var,
                                           co2_var,
                                           adj_vars = adj_core) {
stopifnot(is.list(fit_compact), !is.null(fit_compact$coef), !is.null(fit_compact$vcov))
stopifnot(is.data.frame(grid_df), co2_var %in% names(grid_df))

beta <- fit_compact$coef
V <- fit_compact$vcov
bn <- names(beta)
if (is.null(bn) || any(!nzchar(bn))) {
  stop("predict_spline_prob_from_compact: coefficient names are required.")
}

if (!is.null(fit_compact$terms)) {
  tt <- fit_compact$terms
  if (!identical(attr(tt, ".Environment"), baseenv())) {
    stop("predict_spline_prob_from_compact: compact terms retain a non-base environment.")
  }
  mf_new <- stats::model.frame(
    tt,
    data = grid_df,
    na.action = stats::na.pass,
    xlev = fit_compact$xlevels
  )
  mm <- stats::model.matrix(tt, mf_new, contrasts.arg = fit_compact$contrasts)
} else {
  rhs_terms <- c(sprintf("splines::ns(%s, %d)", co2_var, SPLINE_DF), adj_vars)
  fml <- stats::as.formula(paste(outcome_var, "~", paste(rhs_terms, collapse = " + ")))
  tt <- stats::delete.response(stats::terms(fml))
  mm <- stats::model.matrix(tt, data = grid_df)
}

missing_cols <- setdiff(bn, colnames(mm))
if (length(missing_cols)) {
  mm <- cbind(
    mm,




                                                       472
       matrix(
         0,
         nrow = nrow(mm),
         ncol = length(missing_cols),
         dimnames = list(NULL, missing_cols)
       )
      )
    }
    mm <- mm[, bn, drop = FALSE]

    if (!is.null(rownames(V)) && all(bn %in% rownames(V)) && all(bn %in% colnames(V))) {
      V <- V[bn, bn, drop = FALSE]
    }

    eta <- as.numeric(mm %*% beta)
    mmV <- mm %*% V
    var_eta <- pmax(rowSums(mmV * mm), 0)
    se_eta <- sqrt(var_eta)

    tibble::as_tibble(grid_df) |>
      dplyr::mutate(
        eta = eta,
        SE_eta = se_eta,
        var_eta = var_eta,
        p = stats::plogis(eta),
        p_LCL = stats::plogis(eta - 1.96 * se_eta),
        p_UCL = stats::plogis(eta + 1.96 * se_eta)
      )
}

pool_spline_prob_curve_from_compact <- function(fit_list, grid_df,
                                                outcome_var,
                                                co2_var,
                                                co2_ref,
                                                min_ok_frac = 0.9) {
  pred_list <- lapply(fit_list, function(x) {




                                                           473
  fit_compact <- compact_spline_fit(x)
  if (is.null(fit_compact)) return(NULL)
  tryCatch(
    predict_spline_prob_from_compact(
      fit_compact,
      grid_df = grid_df,
      outcome_var = outcome_var,
      co2_var = co2_var
    ),
    error = function(e) NULL
  )
})

n_grid <- nrow(grid_df)
ok <- vapply(pred_list, function(x) {
  is.data.frame(x) &&
    nrow(x) == n_grid &&
    all(c("eta", "var_eta") %in% names(x))
}, logical(1L))
m_tot <- length(ok)
m_ok <- sum(ok)
if (m_ok < ceiling(min_ok_frac * m_tot)) {
  stop("Too many failed compact spline predictions: m_ok=", m_ok, " / m_total=", m_tot)
}

eta_mat <- matrix(NA_real_, nrow = n_grid, ncol = m_ok)
var_mat <- matrix(NA_real_, nrow = n_grid, ncol = m_ok)
ok_idx <- which(ok)
for (j in seq_along(ok_idx)) {
  pred_j <- pred_list[[ok_idx[[j]]]]
  eta_mat[, j] <- pred_j$eta
  var_mat[, j] <- pred_j$var_eta
}

qbar <- rowMeans(eta_mat, na.rm = TRUE)
ubar <- rowMeans(var_mat, na.rm = TRUE)




                                                          474
    bvar <- apply(eta_mat, 1, stats::var, na.rm = TRUE)
    tvar <- ubar + (1 + 1 / m_ok) * bvar
    se_eta <- sqrt(pmax(tvar, 0))

    tibble::as_tibble(grid_df) |>
      dplyr::mutate(
        eta = qbar,
        SE_eta = se_eta,
        var_eta = tvar,
        p = stats::plogis(qbar),
        p_LCL = stats::plogis(qbar - 1.96 * se_eta),
        p_UCL = stats::plogis(qbar + 1.96 * se_eta),
        co2_ref = co2_ref,
        m_used = m_ok,
        m_total = m_tot
      )
}

nearest_curve_value <- function(curve_df, co2_var, target_value, value_col) {
  if (!nrow(curve_df) || !(co2_var %in% names(curve_df)) || !(value_col %in% names(curve_df))) {
    return(NA_real_)
  }
  x <- suppressWarnings(as.numeric(curve_df[[co2_var]]))
  ok <- is.finite(x)
  if (!any(ok) || !is.finite(target_value)) return(NA_real_)
  idx <- which(ok)[which.min(abs(x[ok] - target_value))]
  suppressWarnings(as.numeric(curve_df[[value_col]][[idx]]))
}

co2_level_targets <- function(group) {
  if (identical(group, "ABG")) {
    return(c(Low = ABG_CO2_LOW, Normal = co2_ref_abg_mi, High = ABG_CO2_HIGH))
  }
  c(Low = VBG_CO2_LOW, Normal = co2_ref_vbg_mi, High = VBG_CO2_HIGH)
}




                                                          475
cat_prob_value <- function(group, outcome_label, category, value_col = "p") {
  group_i <- group
  outcome_i <- outcome_label
  category_i <- category
  out <- main_cat3_probs_conditional_xref |>
    dplyr::filter(
      .data$group == .env$group_i,
      .data$outcome == .env$outcome_i,
      .data$category == .env$category_i
    ) |>
    dplyr::slice_head(n = 1) |>
    dplyr::pull(dplyr::all_of(value_col))
  if (length(out)) suppressWarnings(as.numeric(out[[1L]])) else NA_real_
}

cat_or_value <- function(group, outcome_label, contrast, value_col = "OR") {
  group_i <- group
  outcome_i <- outcome_label
  contrast_i <- contrast
  out <- main_cat3_results |>
    dplyr::filter(
      .data$group == .env$group_i,
      .data$outcome == .env$outcome_i,
      .data$contrast == .env$contrast_i
    ) |>
    dplyr::slice_head(n = 1) |>
    dplyr::pull(dplyr::all_of(value_col))
  if (length(out)) suppressWarnings(as.numeric(out[[1L]])) else NA_real_
}

spline_current_summary_one <- function(group, outcome_var) {
  outcome_label <- discordance_outcome_labels[[outcome_var]]
  co2_var <- if (identical(group, "ABG")) "paco2" else "vbg_co2"
  or_df <- if (identical(group, "ABG")) abg_curves else vbg_curves
  prob_df <- if (identical(group, "ABG")) abg_prob_curves_conditional_xref else vbg_prob_curves_conditional_xref
  or_df <- or_df |>




                                                         476
      dplyr::filter(.data$group == group, .data$outcome == outcome_var)
    prob_df <- prob_df |>
      dplyr::filter(.data$group == group, .data$outcome == outcome_var)
    targets <- co2_level_targets(group)

    tibble::tibble(
      outcome = outcome_label,
      modality = group,
      analysis_family = "MI-logistic IPSW",
      co2_representation = "spline",
      or_low_vs_normal = nearest_curve_value(or_df, co2_var, targets[["Low"]], "OR"),
      or_high_vs_normal = nearest_curve_value(or_df, co2_var, targets[["High"]], "OR"),
      prob_normal = nearest_curve_value(prob_df, co2_var, targets[["Normal"]], "p"),
      prob_low = nearest_curve_value(prob_df, co2_var, targets[["Low"]], "p"),
      prob_high = nearest_curve_value(prob_df, co2_var, targets[["High"]], "p"),
      notes = "Current modality-specific reference profile."
    )
}

cat_current_summary <- tidyr::crossing(

    prob_normal = cat_prob_value(modality, outcome, "Normal"),
    prob_low = cat_prob_value(modality, outcome, "Low"),
    prob_high = cat_prob_value(modality, outcome, "High"),
    notes = "Current categorical ORs and predicted probabilities."
  ) |>

                                                           477
  dplyr::select(
    outcome, modality, analysis_family, co2_representation,
    or_low_vs_normal, or_high_vs_normal, prob_normal, prob_low, prob_high, notes
  )

spline_current_summary <- purrr::map_dfr(discordance_groups, function(group) {
   purrr::map_dfr(discordance_outcome_vars, function(outcome_var) {
     spline_current_summary_one(group, outcome_var)

common_ref_source <- subset_data |>
  dplyr::filter(
    (.data$has_abg == 1 & is.finite(suppressWarnings(as.numeric(.data$paco2)))) |
      (.data$has_vbg == 1 & is.finite(suppressWarnings(as.numeric(.data$vbg_co2))))
  )
if (!nrow(common_ref_source)) common_ref_source <- subset_data
x_ref_common <- make_ref_profile(common_ref_source, adj_core)

grid_abg_common_info <- make_co2_grid_ref(
  "paco2",
  grid_abg_mi$paco2,
  x_ref_common,
  co2_ref_abg_mi
)
grid_vbg_common_info <- make_co2_grid_ref(
  "vbg_co2",
  grid_vbg_mi$vbg_co2,
  x_ref_common,
  co2_ref_vbg_mi
)

common_ref_curve_one <- function(group, outcome_var) {
  fit_list <- if (identical(group, "ABG")) spline_fits_abg[[outcome_var]] else spline_fits_vbg[[outcome_var]]
  grid_info <- if (identical(group, "ABG")) grid_abg_common_info else grid_vbg_common_info
  co2_var <- if (identical(group, "ABG")) "paco2" else "vbg_co2"
  co2_ref <- if (identical(group, "ABG")) co2_ref_abg_mi else co2_ref_vbg_mi
  pool_spline_prob_curve_from_compact(
    fit_list,
    grid_df = grid_info$grid,
    outcome_var = outcome_var,
    co2_var = co2_var,
    co2_ref = co2_ref
  ) |>
    dplyr::mutate(
       outcome = discordance_outcome_labels[[outcome_var]],




                                                         483
        outcome_var = outcome_var,
        group = group,
        strategy = "common_reference",
        co2_scale = co2_var,
        co2_value = .data[[co2_var]]
    )
}

discordance_xref_common_prob_curves <- purrr::map_dfr(discordance_groups, function(group) {
   purrr::map_dfr(discordance_outcome_vars, function(outcome_var) {
     common_ref_curve_one(group, outcome_var)
   })
})
write_csv_safely(
   discordance_xref_common_prob_curves,
   results_path("discordance_xref_common_prob_curves.csv"),
   row_names = FALSE
)

standardization_sample_cap <- common_std_sample_cap
min_marginal_ok_frac <- 0.9
min_marginal_required <- ceiling(min_marginal_ok_frac * imp_n)
standardization_source_rows <- function(d, imp_index) {
  d <- d[, intersect(c(adj_core, "has_abg", "has_vbg"), names(d)), drop = FALSE]
  d <- d[stats::complete.cases(d[, adj_core, drop = FALSE]), , drop = FALSE]
  if (nrow(d) <= standardization_sample_cap) return(d)
  set.seed(7100L + imp_index)
  d[sample.int(nrow(d), standardization_sample_cap), , drop = FALSE]
}

marginal_predict_compact <- function(fit_compact, source_df, co2_var,
                                     co2_values, outcome_var) {
  purrr::map_dfr(co2_values, function(co2_value) {
    nd <- source_df
    nd[[co2_var]] <- co2_value
    pred <- predict_spline_prob_from_compact(




                                                         484
       fit_compact,
       grid_df = nd,
       outcome_var = outcome_var,
       co2_var = co2_var
      )
      tibble::tibble(
        co2_value = co2_value,
        p_imp = mean(pred$p, na.rm = TRUE),
        n_standardized = nrow(nd)
      )
    })
}

marginal_rows <- list()
marginal_status_rows <- list()

record_marginal_status <- function(imp_index, group, outcome_var, co2_var,
                                   status, error_message = "",
                                   n_standardized = NA_integer_,
                                   n_grid = NA_integer_) {
  marginal_status_rows[[length(marginal_status_rows) + 1L]] <<- tibble::tibble(
    imp = imp_index,
    group = group,
    outcome = discordance_outcome_labels[[outcome_var]],
    outcome_var = outcome_var,
    co2_scale = co2_var,
    status = status,
    error_message = error_message,
    n_standardized = as.integer(n_standardized),
    n_grid = as.integer(n_grid)
  )
  invisible(TRUE)
}

for (imp_index in seq_len(imp_n)) {
  d_imp <- get_imp(imp_index)




                                                         485
source_imp <- standardization_source_rows(d_imp, imp_index)
for (group in discordance_groups) {
  co2_var <- if (identical(group, "ABG")) "paco2" else "vbg_co2"
  co2_values <- if (identical(group, "ABG")) grid_abg_mi$paco2 else grid_vbg_mi$vbg_co2
  fit_bank <- if (identical(group, "ABG")) spline_fits_abg else spline_fits_vbg
  for (outcome_var in discordance_outcome_vars) {
    fit_compact <- compact_spline_fit(fit_bank[[outcome_var]][[imp_index]])
    if (is.null(fit_compact)) {
      record_marginal_status(
         imp_index,
         group,
         outcome_var,
         co2_var,
         status = "skipped_no_compact_fit",
         error_message = "compact spline fit unavailable",
         n_standardized = nrow(source_imp),
         n_grid = length(co2_values)
      )
      next
    }
    pred_try <- tryCatch(
      list(
         value = marginal_predict_compact(
           fit_compact,
           source_df = source_imp,
           co2_var = co2_var,
           co2_values = co2_values,
           outcome_var = outcome_var
         ),
         error = NULL
      ),
      error = function(e) list(value = NULL, error = conditionMessage(e))
    )
    if (!is.null(pred_try$error) || is.null(pred_try$value) || !nrow(pred_try$value)) {
      error_message <- if (is.null(pred_try$error)) {
         "prediction returned no rows"




                                                       486
         } else {
           pred_try$error
         }
         record_marginal_status(
           imp_index,
           group,
           outcome_var,
           co2_var,
           status = "failed_prediction",
           error_message = error_message,
           n_standardized = nrow(source_imp),
           n_grid = length(co2_values)
         )
         next
        }
        pred_imp <- pred_try$value
        record_marginal_status(
          imp_index,
          group,
          outcome_var,
          co2_var,
          status = "completed",
          n_standardized = nrow(source_imp),
          n_grid = nrow(pred_imp)
        )
        marginal_rows[[length(marginal_rows) + 1L]] <- pred_imp |>
          dplyr::mutate(
            imp = imp_index,
            outcome = discordance_outcome_labels[[outcome_var]],
            outcome_var = outcome_var,
            group = group,
            co2_scale = co2_var,
            strategy = "marginal_standardized"
          )
    }
}




                                                           487
    rm(d_imp, source_imp)
    invisible(gc(FALSE))
}

marginal_status_raw <- dplyr::bind_rows(marginal_status_rows)
required_marginal_combos <- tidyr::crossing(
  group = discordance_groups,
  outcome_var = discordance_outcome_vars
) |>
  dplyr::mutate(
    outcome = unname(discordance_outcome_labels[outcome_var]),
    m_total = imp_n,
    min_required = min_marginal_required
  )
marginal_completion_summary <- marginal_status_raw |>
  dplyr::group_by(group, outcome_var, outcome) |>
  dplyr::summarise(
    m_used = sum(.data$status == "completed", na.rm = TRUE),
    m_failed = sum(.data$status == "failed_prediction", na.rm = TRUE),
    m_skipped_no_compact_fit = sum(.data$status == "skipped_no_compact_fit", na.rm = TRUE),
    m_attempted = dplyr::n(),
    first_error = {
       errors <- .data$error_message[nzchar(.data$error_message)]
       if (length(errors)) errors[[1L]] else ""
    },
    .groups = "drop"
  ) |>
  dplyr::right_join(
    required_marginal_combos,
    by = c("group", "outcome_var", "outcome")
  ) |>
  dplyr::mutate(
    dplyr::across(
       c(m_used, m_failed, m_skipped_no_compact_fit, m_attempted),
       ~ tidyr::replace_na(.x, 0L)
    ),




                                                         488
   first_error = tidyr::replace_na(.data$first_error, ""),
   passed_threshold = .data$m_used >= .data$min_required
  )
marginal_status_df <- marginal_status_raw |>
  dplyr::left_join(
    marginal_completion_summary |>
      dplyr::select(
        group, outcome_var, m_used, m_total, min_required,
        passed_threshold
      ),
    by = c("group", "outcome_var")
  )
write_csv_safely(
  marginal_status_df,
  results_path("discordance_marginal_standardization_status.csv"),
  row_names = FALSE
)

marginal_threshold_failures <- marginal_completion_summary |>
  dplyr::filter(!.data$passed_threshold)
if (nrow(marginal_threshold_failures)) {
  record_discordance_status(
    "marginal_standardization",
    "failed",
    paste0(
      "Marginal standardization did not meet min_marginal_ok_frac = ",
      min_marginal_ok_frac,
      " for: ",
      paste(
        paste0(
          marginal_threshold_failures$group,
          "/",
          marginal_threshold_failures$outcome,
          " (",
          marginal_threshold_failures$m_used,
          "/",




                                                         489
            marginal_threshold_failures$m_total,
            ")"
          ),
          collapse = "; "
      )
   ),
   "Results/discordance_marginal_standardization_status.csv"
  )
  write_discordance_status()
  stop(
    "Discordance marginal standardization failed the completion threshold: ",
    paste(
      paste0(
        marginal_threshold_failures$group,
        "/",
        marginal_threshold_failures$outcome,
        "=",
        marginal_threshold_failures$m_used,
        "/",
        marginal_threshold_failures$m_total
      ),
      collapse = ", "
    )
  )
}
record_discordance_status(

representative_prob <- function(curves, strategy_name, group, outcome_var, level) {
  strategy_i <- strategy_name
  group_i <- group
  outcome_i <- outcome_var
  co2_var <- if (identical(group, "ABG")) "paco2" else "vbg_co2"
  target <- co2_level_targets(group)[[level]]
  df <- curves |>
    dplyr::filter(
      as.character(.data$strategy) == .env$strategy_i,
      .data$group == .env$group_i,
      .data$outcome_var == .env$outcome_i
    )
  nearest_curve_value(df, "co2_value", target, "p")




                                                         492
}

standardization_summary_rows <- tidyr::crossing(
  outcome_var = discordance_outcome_vars,
  co2_level = c("Low", "Normal", "High")
) |>
  dplyr::mutate(outcome = unname(discordance_outcome_labels[outcome_var])) |>
  dplyr::rowwise() |>
  dplyr::mutate(
    gap_current_ref = representative_prob(
       standardization_curves_for_plot,
       "Current reference",
       "ABG",
       outcome_var,
       co2_level
    ) - representative_prob(
       standardization_curves_for_plot,
       "Current reference",
       "VBG",
       outcome_var,
       co2_level
    ),
    gap_common_ref = representative_prob(
       standardization_curves_for_plot,
       "Common reference",
       "ABG",
       outcome_var,
       co2_level
    ) - representative_prob(
       standardization_curves_for_plot,
       "Common reference",
       "VBG",
       outcome_var,
       co2_level
    ),
    gap_marginal_standardized = representative_prob(




                                                         493
     standardization_curves_for_plot,
     "Marginal standardized",
     "ABG",
     outcome_var,
     co2_level
  ) - representative_prob(
     standardization_curves_for_plot,
     "Marginal standardized",
     "VBG",
     outcome_var,
     co2_level
  ),
  standardization_sample_cap = standardization_sample_cap,
  interpretation = dplyr::case_when(
     is.finite(gap_current_ref) &
       is.finite(gap_common_ref) &
       abs(gap_common_ref) <= 0.75 * abs(gap_current_ref) ~ "Common reference shrinks the current probability gap.",
     is.finite(gap_current_ref) &
       is.finite(gap_marginal_standardized) &
       abs(gap_marginal_standardized) <= 0.75 * abs(gap_current_ref) ~ "Marginal standardization shrinks the current
        ↪  probability gap.",
     TRUE ~ "Standardization did not materially shrink the current probability gap."
  )
) |>
dplyr::ungroup() |>
dplyr::left_join(
  marginal_completion_summary |>
     dplyr::group_by(outcome_var, outcome) |>
     dplyr::summarise(
       m_used = min(.data$m_used, na.rm = TRUE),
       m_total = max(.data$m_total, na.rm = TRUE),
       min_required = max(.data$min_required, na.rm = TRUE),
       .groups = "drop"
     ),
  by = c("outcome_var", "outcome")
) |>




                                                        494
  dplyr::select(
    outcome, co2_level, gap_current_ref, gap_common_ref,
    gap_marginal_standardized, standardization_sample_cap,
    m_used, m_total, min_required, interpretation
  )

discordance_scale_summary <- tidyr::crossing(
  outcome_var = discordance_outcome_vars,
  contrast = c("Low vs normal", "High vs normal")
) |>
  dplyr::mutate(
    outcome = unname(discordance_outcome_labels[outcome_var]),
    category = dplyr::if_else(contrast == "Low vs normal", "Low", "High")
  ) |>



                                                         497
  dplyr::rowwise() |>
  dplyr::mutate(
    abg_or = cat_or_value("ABG", outcome, contrast),
    vbg_or = cat_or_value("VBG", outcome, contrast),
    abg_prob = cat_prob_value("ABG", outcome, category),
    vbg_prob = cat_prob_value("VBG", outcome, category),
    abg_prob_ref = cat_prob_value("ABG", outcome, "Normal"),
    vbg_prob_ref = cat_prob_value("VBG", outcome, "Normal"),
    abg_rd = abg_prob - abg_prob_ref,
    vbg_rd = vbg_prob - vbg_prob_ref,
    abg_rr = ifelse(is.finite(abg_prob_ref) & abg_prob_ref > 0, abg_prob / abg_prob_ref, NA_real_),
    vbg_rr = ifelse(is.finite(vbg_prob_ref) & vbg_prob_ref > 0, vbg_prob / vbg_prob_ref, NA_real_),
    comment = dplyr::case_when(
       is.finite(abg_or) & is.finite(vbg_or) &
         abs(log(abg_or) - log(vbg_or)) < abs(abg_rd - vbg_rd) ~
         "Relative odds are closer than absolute risk differences.",
       TRUE ~ "Scale check does not show clearly closer ORs."
    )
  ) |>
  dplyr::ungroup() |>
  dplyr::select(
    outcome, contrast, abg_or, vbg_or, abg_prob, vbg_prob,
    abg_rd, vbg_rd, abg_rr, vbg_rr, comment
  )
write_csv_safely(
  discordance_scale_summary,
  results_path("discordance_scale_summary.csv"),
  row_names = FALSE
)
record_discordance_status(
  "scale_noncollapsibility",
  "completed",
  "OR, risk-difference, risk-ratio, and predicted-probability scale summaries were computed.",
  "Results/discordance_scale_summary.csv"
)

missing_indicator_vars <- covars_ps[covars_ps %in% names(subset_data_raw)]
missing_indicator_vars <- missing_indicator_vars[
  vapply(missing_indicator_vars, function(v) any(is.na(subset_data_raw[[v]])), logical(1L))
]

if (!length(missing_indicator_vars)) {
  discordance_missing_indicator_balance <- tibble::tibble(
    variable = NA_character_,
    group = NA_character_,
    smd_pre = NA_real_,
    smd_post = NA_real_,
    component_status = "skipped",
    reason = "no_missing_baseline_indicators"
  )
} else {
  miss_bal_rows <- list()
  target_missing <- lapply(missing_indicator_vars, function(v) as.integer(is.na(subset_data_raw[[v]])))
  names(target_missing) <- missing_indicator_vars
  for (imp_index in seq_len(imp_n)) {
    for (group in discordance_groups) {
      treat_var <- if (identical(group, "ABG")) "has_abg" else "has_vbg"
      treat <- subset_data[[treat_var]] == 1
      weights_i <- get_mi_weight(group, imp_index)
      for (v in missing_indicator_vars) {
        x <- target_missing[[v]]
        target_p <- mean(x, na.rm = TRUE)
        target_sd <- sqrt(target_p * (1 - target_p))
        pre <- mean(x[treat], na.rm = TRUE)
        post <- weighted_mean_safe(x[treat], weights_i[treat])
        miss_bal_rows[[length(miss_bal_rows) + 1L]] <- tibble::tibble(
          imp = imp_index,
          variable = v,




                                                           502
              group = group,
              missing_target = target_p,
              missing_tested = pre,
              missing_weighted = post,
              smd_pre = ifelse(is.finite(target_sd) & target_sd > 0, (pre - target_p) / target_sd, NA_real_),
              smd_post = ifelse(is.finite(target_sd) & target_sd > 0, (post - target_p) / target_sd, NA_real_)
          )
      }
    }
  }
  discordance_missing_indicator_balance <- dplyr::bind_rows(miss_bal_rows) |>
    dplyr::group_by(variable, group) |>
    dplyr::summarise(
      missing_target = stats::median(missing_target, na.rm = TRUE),
      missing_tested = stats::median(missing_tested, na.rm = TRUE),
      missing_weighted = stats::median(missing_weighted, na.rm = TRUE),
      smd_pre = stats::median(smd_pre, na.rm = TRUE),
      smd_post = stats::median(smd_post, na.rm = TRUE),
      .groups = "drop"
    ) |>
    dplyr::mutate(component_status = "completed", reason = "baseline_missingness_indicators_available")
}
write_csv_safely(
  discordance_missing_indicator_balance,
  results_path("discordance_missing_indicator_balance.csv"),
  row_names = FALSE
)

  ~sentinel_concept, ~priority_rank, ~matched_pattern,
  "ECG/EKG", 1L, "(ecg|ekg|electrocard)",
  "Chest radiograph", 2L, "(cxr|chest.*(xray|x_ray|radiograph)|xray.*chest|x_ray.*chest)",
  "Transthoracic echocardiography", 3L, "(tte|transthoracic|echo)",
  "CT chest / CT pulmonary angiography", 4L,
   ↪  "(ctc|ct_chest|ct.*chest|pulmonary.*angio|ctpa|cta.*chest|ct.*pulmonary)",
  "Central venous catheter placement", 5L, "(central.*ven|central.*line|cvc|cvp)",
  "Urinary catheter placement", 6L, "(urinary.*catheter|foley)",
  "Blood transfusion", 7L, "(transfusion|blood.*transfus|rbc|prbc)",
  "Hemodialysis initiation", 8L, "(hemodialysis|dialysis|renal.*replacement|crrt)",
  "Bronchoscopy", 9L, "(bronch)"
)




                                                         512
sentinel_excluded_fields <- c(
  "imv_proc", "niv_proc", "vent_proc",
  "meas_arterial_gas_proc", "meas_venous_o2_proc"
)
sentinel_candidate_names <- union(names(subset_data), names(subset_data_raw))
sentinel_binary_names <- setdiff(
  sentinel_candidate_names,
  grep("(date|time|timestamp|datetime)|_(first|last)_date", sentinel_candidate_names,
       value = TRUE, ignore.case = TRUE, perl = TRUE)
)
sentinel_binary_names <- setdiff(sentinel_binary_names, sentinel_excluded_fields)
sentinel_binary_names <- sentinel_binary_names[
  !grepl("(abg|vbg|blood_gas|gas|paco2|co2|po2|o2sat|hco3|ph|lactate)",
         sentinel_binary_names, ignore.case = TRUE, perl = TRUE)
]

sentinel_indicator <- function(x) {
  if (is.factor(x) || is.character(x)) {
    raw <- trimws(as.character(x))
    raw_lower <- tolower(raw)
    num <- suppressWarnings(as.numeric(raw))
    if (all(is.na(num[!is.na(raw) & nzchar(raw)]))) {
      return(as.integer(!is.na(raw) & nzchar(raw) &
                          !raw_lower %in% c("0", "no", "false", "absent", "none")))
    }
    return(as.integer(is.finite(num) & num > 0))
  }
  num <- suppressWarnings(as.numeric(x))
  as.integer(is.finite(num) & num > 0)
}

sentinel_source_vector <- function(field, d_imp = NULL) {
  if (!is.null(d_imp) && field %in% names(d_imp)) {
    x <- d_imp[[field]]
  } else if (field %in% names(subset_data)) {
    x <- subset_data[[field]]




                                                            513
    } else if (field %in% names(subset_data_raw)) {
      x <- subset_data_raw[[field]]
    } else {
      stop("Sentinel field not found in analysis or raw data: ", field, call. = FALSE)
    }
    if (length(x) != nrow(subset_data)) {
      stop("Sentinel field has unexpected row count: ", field, call. = FALSE)
    }
    x
}

sentinel_date_stems <- function(binary_field) {
  stripped_stem <- sub("(_0|_dur|_duration)$", "", binary_field, perl = TRUE)
  stems <- unique(c(binary_field, stripped_stem))
  stems[nzchar(stems)]
}

sentinel_date_field_for <- function(binary_field, pattern) {
  force(pattern)
  raw_names <- names(subset_data_raw)
  stems <- sentinel_date_stems(binary_field)
  direct_candidates <- unique(unlist(
    lapply(stems, function(stem) {
      c(
        paste0(stem, "_first_date"),
        paste0(stem, "_last_date")
      )
    }),
    use.names = FALSE
  ))
  date_like_names <- raw_names[
    grepl("(date|time|timestamp|datetime)", raw_names, ignore.case = TRUE, perl = TRUE)
  ]
  stem_timestamp_candidates <- unique(unlist(
    lapply(stems, function(stem) {
      date_like_names[startsWith(date_like_names, paste0(stem, "_"))]




                                                           514
      }),
      use.names = FALSE
    ))
    hits <- unique(c(direct_candidates, stem_timestamp_candidates))
    hits <- setdiff(hits, binary_field)
    hits <- hits[grepl("(date|time|timestamp|datetime)", hits, ignore.case = TRUE, perl = TRUE)]
    hits <- hits[hits %in% raw_names]
    if (length(hits)) hits[[1L]] else NA_character_
}

sentinel_inventory_rows <- purrr::map_dfr(seq_len(nrow(sentinel_specs)), function(idx) {
  spec <- sentinel_specs[idx, ]
  matched_fields <- grep(
    spec$matched_pattern,
    sentinel_binary_names,
    value = TRUE,
    ignore.case = TRUE,
    perl = TRUE
  )
  matched_fields <- unique(matched_fields)
  if (!length(matched_fields)) {
    return(tibble::tibble(
      sentinel_concept = spec$sentinel_concept,
      candidate_field = NA_character_,
      field_role = "binary_indicator",
      matched_pattern = spec$matched_pattern,
      present = FALSE,
      class = NA_character_,
      n_nonmissing = 0L,
      prevalence_overall = NA_real_,
      prevalence_abg_tested = NA_real_,
      prevalence_vbg_tested = NA_real_,
      events_abg_tested = 0L,
      events_vbg_tested = 0L,
      date_field = NA_character_,
      date_missing_abg_tested = NA_real_,




                                                           515
   date_missing_vbg_tested = NA_real_,
   priority_rank = spec$priority_rank,
   selection_reason = "no_matching_binary_field"
  ))
}
purrr::map_dfr(matched_fields, function(field) {
  source_vec <- sentinel_source_vector(field)
  y <- sentinel_indicator(source_vec)
  date_field <- sentinel_date_field_for(field, spec$matched_pattern)
  date_vec <- if (!is.na(date_field)) subset_data_raw[[date_field]] else rep(NA, nrow(subset_data_raw))
  abg_tested <- subset_data$has_abg == 1
  vbg_tested <- subset_data$has_vbg == 1
  tibble::tibble(
     sentinel_concept = spec$sentinel_concept,
     candidate_field = field,
     field_role = ifelse(field %in% names(subset_data), "analysis_indicator", "raw_indicator"),
     matched_pattern = spec$matched_pattern,
     present = TRUE,
     class = paste(class(source_vec), collapse = "/"),
     n_nonmissing = sum(!is.na(source_vec)),
     prevalence_overall = mean(y == 1, na.rm = TRUE),
     prevalence_abg_tested = mean(y[abg_tested] == 1, na.rm = TRUE),
     prevalence_vbg_tested = mean(y[vbg_tested] == 1, na.rm = TRUE),
     events_abg_tested = sum(y[abg_tested] == 1, na.rm = TRUE),
     events_vbg_tested = sum(y[vbg_tested] == 1, na.rm = TRUE),
     date_field = ifelse(is.na(date_field), "", date_field),
     date_missing_abg_tested = ifelse(
       is.na(date_field) || !any(abg_tested & y == 1, na.rm = TRUE),
       NA_real_,
       mean(is.na(date_vec[abg_tested & y == 1]))
     ),
     date_missing_vbg_tested = ifelse(
       is.na(date_field) || !any(vbg_tested & y == 1, na.rm = TRUE),
       NA_real_,
       mean(is.na(date_vec[vbg_tested & y == 1]))
     ),




                                                       516
           priority_rank = spec$priority_rank,
           selection_reason = "candidate_detected"
       )
     })
})

sentinel_min_events <- if (IS_PILOT) 20L else 100L
sentinel_selection_scored <- sentinel_inventory_rows |>
  dplyr::rowwise() |>
  dplyr::mutate(
    prevalence_for_selection = suppressWarnings(max(
       c(prevalence_abg_tested, prevalence_vbg_tested),
       na.rm = TRUE
    )),
    event_count_for_selection = suppressWarnings(max(
       c(events_abg_tested, events_vbg_tested),
       na.rm = TRUE
    ))
  ) |>
  dplyr::ungroup() |>
  dplyr::mutate(
    prevalence_for_selection = ifelse(is.infinite(prevalence_for_selection), NA_real_, prevalence_for_selection),
    event_count_for_selection = ifelse(is.infinite(event_count_for_selection), 0L, event_count_for_selection),
    eligible = .data$present &
       is.finite(.data$prevalence_for_selection) &
       .data$prevalence_for_selection >= 0.01 &
       .data$prevalence_for_selection <= 0.60 &
       .data$event_count_for_selection >= sentinel_min_events,
    selection_reason = dplyr::case_when(
       !.data$present ~ "no_matching_binary_field",
       !is.finite(.data$prevalence_for_selection) ~ "prevalence_unavailable",
       .data$prevalence_for_selection < 0.01 ~ "prevalence_below_1_percent",
       .data$prevalence_for_selection > 0.60 ~ "prevalence_above_60_percent",
       .data$event_count_for_selection < sentinel_min_events ~ "insufficient_events",
       TRUE ~ "eligible"
    ),




                                                         517
      sentinel_key = paste(.data$sentinel_concept, .data$candidate_field, sep = "::")
  )

sentinel_best_by_concept <- sentinel_selection_scored |>
  dplyr::arrange(.data$priority_rank, dplyr::desc(.data$eligible), dplyr::desc(.data$prevalence_for_selection)) |>
  dplyr::group_by(.data$sentinel_concept) |>
  dplyr::slice_head(n = 1) |>
  dplyr::ungroup()

sentinel_selected_keys <- sentinel_best_by_concept |>
  dplyr::filter(.data$eligible) |>
  dplyr::arrange(.data$priority_rank) |>
  dplyr::slice_head(n = 4) |>
  dplyr::pull(.data$sentinel_key)

sentinel_balance_rows <- list()
if (nrow(selected_sentinels)) {
  for (imp_index in seq_len(imp_n)) {
    d_imp <- get_imp(imp_index)
    for (row_idx in seq_len(nrow(selected_sentinels))) {
      sentinel_i <- selected_sentinels[row_idx, ]
      binary_field <- sentinel_i$binary_field
      date_field <- sentinel_i$date_field
      y <- sentinel_indicator(sentinel_source_vector(binary_field, d_imp))
      date_vec <- if (nzchar(date_field) && date_field %in% names(subset_data_raw)) {
        subset_data_raw[[date_field]]
      } else {
        rep(NA, nrow(subset_data_raw))
      }
      for (group in discordance_groups) {
        treat_var <- if (identical(group, "ABG")) "has_abg" else "has_vbg"
        weights_i <- get_mi_weight(group, imp_index)
        tested <- d_imp[[treat_var]] == 1
        event_rows <- tested & y == 1
        sentinel_balance_rows[[length(sentinel_balance_rows) + 1L]] <- tibble::tibble(
          sentinel_concept = sentinel_i$sentinel_concept,




                                                         519
              group = group,
              imp = imp_index,
              n_tested = sum(tested, na.rm = TRUE),
              events = sum(event_rows, na.rm = TRUE),
              unweighted_rate = mean(y[tested] == 1, na.rm = TRUE),
              weighted_rate = weighted_mean_safe(y[tested], weights_i[tested]),
              weighted_n = sum(weights_i[tested], na.rm = TRUE),
              ess = weighted_ess(weights_i[tested]),
              date_missing_fraction = ifelse(
                nzchar(date_field) && any(event_rows, na.rm = TRUE),
                mean(is.na(date_vec[event_rows])),
                NA_real_
              )
          )
      }
   }
   rm(d_imp)
   invisible(gc(FALSE))
  }
  discordance_sentinel_procedure_balance <- dplyr::bind_rows(sentinel_balance_rows)
} else {
  discordance_sentinel_procedure_balance <- tibble::tibble(
    sentinel_concept = NA_character_,
    group = NA_character_,
    imp = NA_integer_,
    n_tested = NA_integer_,
    events = NA_integer_,
    unweighted_rate = NA_real_,
    weighted_rate = NA_real_,
    weighted_n = NA_real_,
    ess = NA_real_,
    date_missing_fraction = NA_real_,
    component_status = "skipped",
    reason = "no_sentinel_procedure_selected"
  )
}

sentinel_metric_summary <- if (nrow(selected_sentinels)) {
  discordance_sentinel_procedure_balance |>
    dplyr::group_by(.data$sentinel_concept, .data$group) |>
    dplyr::summarise(
      weighted_rate = stats::median(.data$weighted_rate, na.rm = TRUE),
      date_missing_fraction = stats::median(.data$date_missing_fraction, na.rm = TRUE),
      m_used = dplyr::n_distinct(.data$imp),
      .groups = "drop"
    ) |>
    tidyr::pivot_wider(
      names_from = group,
      values_from = c(weighted_rate, date_missing_fraction, m_used)
    ) |>
    dplyr::transmute(
      sentinel_concept,
      abg_weighted_rate = .data$weighted_rate_ABG,
      vbg_weighted_rate = .data$weighted_rate_VBG,
      weighted_abs_diff = .data$abg_weighted_rate - .data$vbg_weighted_rate,
      weighted_relative_diff = safe_relative_gap(.data$abg_weighted_rate, .data$vbg_weighted_rate),
      date_missing_abs_diff = abs(.data$date_missing_fraction_ABG - .data$date_missing_fraction_VBG),
      m_used = pmin(.data$m_used_ABG, .data$m_used_VBG, na.rm = TRUE),
      m_used = ifelse(is.infinite(.data$m_used), NA_integer_, as.integer(.data$m_used))
    )
} else {
  tibble::tibble(
    sentinel_concept = character(),
    abg_weighted_rate = numeric(),
    vbg_weighted_rate = numeric(),
    weighted_abs_diff = numeric(),
    weighted_relative_diff = numeric(),




                                                         521
        date_missing_abs_diff = numeric(),
        m_used = integer()
    )
}

discordance_sentinel_procedure_summary <- discordance_sentinel_procedure_selection |>
  dplyr::select(sentinel_concept, selected, selection_status, selection_reason) |>
  dplyr::left_join(sentinel_metric_summary, by = "sentinel_concept") |>
  dplyr::mutate(
    interpretation = dplyr::case_when(
       !.data$selected ~ .data$selection_status,
       is.finite(.data$date_missing_abs_diff) & .data$date_missing_abs_diff > 0.05 ~
         "Sentinel procedure timestamp completeness differs by >5 percentage points.",
       is.finite(.data$weighted_abs_diff) & abs(.data$weighted_abs_diff) > 0.05 ~
         "Sentinel procedure weighted capture rates differ by >5 percentage points.",
       TRUE ~ "Selected sentinel does not show a large ABG-VBG capture/completeness gap."
    )
  ) |>
  dplyr::select(
    sentinel_concept, selected, abg_weighted_rate, vbg_weighted_rate,
    weighted_abs_diff, weighted_relative_diff, date_missing_abs_diff,
    m_used, interpretation
  )
write_csv_safely(
  discordance_sentinel_procedure_summary,
  results_path("discordance_sentinel_procedure_summary.csv"),
  row_names = FALSE
)

    dplyr::group_by(.data$sentinel_concept, .data$binary_field, .data$date_field, .data$group) |>
    dplyr::summarise(
      weighted_rate = stats::median(.data$weighted_rate, na.rm = TRUE),
      date_missing_fraction = stats::median(.data$date_missing_fraction, na.rm = TRUE),
      m_used = dplyr::n_distinct(.data$imp),
      .groups = "drop"
    ) |>
    tidyr::pivot_wider(




                                                             527
      names_from = group,
      values_from = c(weighted_rate, date_missing_fraction, m_used)
    ) |>
    dplyr::transmute(
      sentinel_concept,
      binary_field,
      date_field,
      abg_weighted_rate = .data$weighted_rate_ABG,
      vbg_weighted_rate = .data$weighted_rate_VBG,
      weighted_abs_diff = .data$abg_weighted_rate - .data$vbg_weighted_rate,
      weighted_relative_diff = safe_relative_gap(.data$abg_weighted_rate, .data$vbg_weighted_rate),
      date_missing_abs_diff = abs(.data$date_missing_fraction_ABG - .data$date_missing_fraction_VBG),
      m_used = pmin(.data$m_used_ABG, .data$m_used_VBG, na.rm = TRUE),
      m_used = ifelse(is.infinite(.data$m_used), NA_integer_, as.integer(.data$m_used))
    )
} else {
  tibble::tibble(
    sentinel_concept = character(),
    binary_field = character(),
    date_field = character(),
    abg_weighted_rate = numeric(),
    vbg_weighted_rate = numeric(),
    weighted_abs_diff = numeric(),
    weighted_relative_diff = numeric(),
    date_missing_abs_diff = numeric(),
    m_used = integer()
  )
}

      is.finite(.data$date_missing_abs_diff) & .data$date_missing_abs_diff > 0.05 ~
        "V2 sentinel timestamp completeness differs by >5 percentage points for the selected candidate field.",
      is.finite(.data$weighted_abs_diff) & abs(.data$weighted_abs_diff) > 0.05 ~
        "V2 sentinel weighted capture rates differ by >5 percentage points for the selected candidate field.",
      TRUE ~ "Selected v2 sentinel does not show a large ABG-VBG capture/completeness gap."
    )
  ) |>
  dplyr::select(
    sentinel_concept, binary_field, date_field, selected, abg_weighted_rate,
    vbg_weighted_rate, weighted_abs_diff, weighted_relative_diff,
    date_missing_abs_diff, m_used, interpretation
  )

## Support, tail, and positivity diagnostics
make_quantile_bin <- function(x) {
  probs <- c(0, 0.02, 0.25, 0.75, 0.98, 1)
  cuts <- unique(stats::quantile(x, probs = probs, na.rm = TRUE, names = FALSE))
  if (length(cuts) < 3L) return(factor(rep(NA_character_, length(x))))
  cut(x, breaks = cuts, include.lowest = TRUE, ordered_result = TRUE)
}

tail_support_rows <- list()
for (imp_index in seq_len(imp_n)) {
  d_imp <- get_imp(imp_index)
  for (group in discordance_groups) {
    co2_var <- if (identical(group, "ABG")) "paco2" else "vbg_co2"
    treat_var <- if (identical(group, "ABG")) "has_abg" else "has_vbg"
    low_cut <- if (identical(group, "ABG")) ABG_CO2_LOW else VBG_CO2_LOW
    high_cut <- if (identical(group, "ABG")) ABG_CO2_HIGH else VBG_CO2_HIGH
    weights_i <- get_mi_weight(group, imp_index)
    tested <- d_imp[[treat_var]] == 1 & is.finite(suppressWarnings(as.numeric(d_imp[[co2_var]])))
    co2_x <- suppressWarnings(as.numeric(d_imp[[co2_var]]))
    clinical_bin <- make_co2_cat3(co2_x, low_cut, high_cut)
    clinical_bin <- factor(clinical_bin, levels = c("Low", "Normal", "High"), ordered = TRUE)
    quantile_bin <- rep(NA, nrow(d_imp))
    quantile_bin[tested] <- as.character(make_quantile_bin(co2_x[tested]))
    bin_df <- dplyr::bind_rows(
      tibble::tibble(bin_type = "clinical_cat3", bin = as.character(clinical_bin)),
      tibble::tibble(bin_type = "quantile_support", bin = as.character(quantile_bin))
    ) |>
      dplyr::mutate(row_id = rep(seq_len(nrow(d_imp)), times = 2L))

     for (outcome_var in discordance_outcome_vars) {
       y <- to01(d_imp[[outcome_var]])
       for (bin_type_i in unique(bin_df$bin_type)) {
         rows_i <- bin_df |>




                                                         531
               dplyr::filter(.data$bin_type == bin_type_i) |>
               dplyr::mutate(
                 tested = tested[row_id],
                 y = y[row_id],
                 w = weights_i[row_id],
                 co2 = co2_x[row_id]
               ) |>
               dplyr::filter(.data$tested, !is.na(.data$bin))
             if (!nrow(rows_i)) next
             tail_support_rows[[length(tail_support_rows) + 1L]] <- rows_i |>
               dplyr::group_by(bin_type, bin) |>
               dplyr::summarise(
                 n_unweighted = dplyr::n(),
                 co2_min = min(co2, na.rm = TRUE),
                 co2_max = max(co2, na.rm = TRUE),
                 weighted_n = sum(w, na.rm = TRUE),
                 weighted_events = sum(w * y, na.rm = TRUE),
                 weighted_event_rate = ifelse(weighted_n > 0, weighted_events / weighted_n, NA_real_),
                 ess = weighted_ess(w),
                 .groups = "drop"
               ) |>
               dplyr::mutate(
                 imp = imp_index,
                 group = group,
                 outcome = discordance_outcome_labels[[outcome_var]],
                 outcome_var = outcome_var
               )
         }
     }
    }
    rm(d_imp)
    invisible(gc(FALSE))
}

discordance_tail_support_by_bin <- dplyr::bind_rows(tail_support_rows) |>
  dplyr::group_by(group, outcome, outcome_var, bin_type, bin) |>




                                                              532
  dplyr::summarise(
    n_unweighted = stats::median(n_unweighted, na.rm = TRUE),
    co2_min = stats::median(co2_min, na.rm = TRUE),
    co2_max = stats::median(co2_max, na.rm = TRUE),
    weighted_n = stats::median(weighted_n, na.rm = TRUE),
    weighted_events = stats::median(weighted_events, na.rm = TRUE),
    weighted_event_rate = stats::median(weighted_event_rate, na.rm = TRUE),
    ess = stats::median(ess, na.rm = TRUE),
    m_used = dplyr::n_distinct(imp),
    .groups = "drop"
  )
write_csv_safely(
  discordance_tail_support_by_bin,
  results_path("discordance_tail_support_by_bin.csv"),
  row_names = FALSE
)

            weighted_event_rate = weighted_mean_safe(y, w),
            ess = weighted_ess(w),
            .groups = "drop"
          ) |>

            imp = imp_index,

            outcome = discordance_outcome_labels[[outcome_var]],
            setting_var = setting_var




                                                         536

         }
     }

## IMV-focused setting and site heterogeneity diagnostics
imv_setting_vars <- intersect(c("encounter_type", "location"), setting_vars)
imv_setting_level_specs <- purrr::map_dfr(imv_setting_vars, function(setting_var) {
  level_df <- tibble::tibble(
    setting_var = setting_var,
    setting_level = as.character(subset_data[[setting_var]]),
    has_abg = subset_data$has_abg == 1,
    has_vbg = subset_data$has_vbg == 1
  ) |>
    dplyr::filter(!is.na(.data$setting_level), nzchar(.data$setting_level)) |>
    dplyr::group_by(.data$setting_var, .data$setting_level) |>
    dplyr::summarise(
       n_total = dplyr::n(),
       n_abg = sum(.data$has_abg, na.rm = TRUE),




                                                         539
         n_vbg = sum(.data$has_vbg, na.rm = TRUE),
         .groups = "drop"
       ) |>
       dplyr::filter(.data$n_abg >= 10L, .data$n_vbg >= 10L) |>
       dplyr::arrange(dplyr::desc(.data$n_total))
     if (identical(setting_var, "location")) {
       level_df <- dplyr::slice_head(level_df, n = 8)
     }
     level_df
})

imv_setting_prediction_rows <- list()
if (nrow(imv_setting_level_specs)) {
  for (imp_index in seq_len(imp_n)) {
    d_imp <- get_imp(imp_index)
    for (spec_idx in seq_len(nrow(imv_setting_level_specs))) {
      spec_i <- imv_setting_level_specs[spec_idx, ]
      row_in_setting <- !is.na(d_imp[[spec_i$setting_var]]) &
        as.character(d_imp[[spec_i$setting_var]]) == spec_i$setting_level
      source_setting <- standardization_source_rows(d_imp[row_in_setting, , drop = FALSE], imp_index)
      if (!nrow(source_setting)) next
      for (group in discordance_groups) {
        co2_var <- if (identical(group, "ABG")) "paco2" else "vbg_co2"
        co2_targets <- co2_level_targets(group)
        fit_bank <- if (identical(group, "ABG")) spline_fits_abg else spline_fits_vbg
        fit_compact <- compact_spline_fit(fit_bank[["imv_proc"]][[imp_index]])
        if (is.null(fit_compact)) next
        pred_try <- tryCatch(
          marginal_predict_compact(
            fit_compact,
            source_df = source_setting,
            co2_var = co2_var,
            co2_values = unname(co2_targets),
            outcome_var = "imv_proc"
          ),
          error = function(e) NULL




                                                            540
              )
              if (is.null(pred_try) || !nrow(pred_try)) next
              imv_setting_prediction_rows[[length(imv_setting_prediction_rows) + 1L]] <- pred_try |>
                dplyr::mutate(
                  imp = imp_index,
                  group = group,
                  outcome = "IMV",
                  outcome_var = "imv_proc",
                  setting_var = spec_i$setting_var,
                  setting_level = spec_i$setting_level,
                  co2_level = names(co2_targets)[seq_len(dplyr::n())],
                  n_setting_total = spec_i$n_total,
                  n_setting_abg = spec_i$n_abg,
                  n_setting_vbg = spec_i$n_vbg
                )
          }
        }
        rm(d_imp)
        invisible(gc(FALSE))
    }
}

    both_modality_site = NA,
    component_status = "skipped",
    reason = "No separate site/facility identifier with 2-50 levels was found."
  )
} else {
  site_counts <- tibble::tibble(
    site_level = as.character(subset_data[[site_field]]),
    has_abg = subset_data$has_abg == 1,
    has_vbg = subset_data$has_vbg == 1
  ) |>
    dplyr::filter(!is.na(.data$site_level), nzchar(.data$site_level)) |>
    dplyr::group_by(.data$site_level) |>
    dplyr::summarise(
       site_n_abg = sum(.data$has_abg, na.rm = TRUE),
       site_n_vbg = sum(.data$has_vbg, na.rm = TRUE),
       both_modality_site = .data$site_n_abg >= 20L & .data$site_n_vbg >= 20L,
       .groups = "drop"
    )
  discordance_imv_site_sensitivity <- discordance_setting_sensitivity |>
    dplyr::filter(.data$setting_var == .env$site_field, .data$outcome == "IMV") |>
    dplyr::rename(site_level = setting_level) |>
    dplyr::left_join(site_counts, by = "site_level") |>




                                                           543
   dplyr::mutate(
     site_field = .env$site_field,
     component_status = "completed",
     reason = "IMV site-level weighted event-rate sensitivity."
   ) |>
   dplyr::select(
     site_field, site_level, group, outcome, n_unweighted, weighted_n,
     weighted_event_rate, ess, m_used, site_n_abg, site_n_vbg,
     both_modality_site, component_status, reason
   )
}
write_csv_safely(
  discordance_imv_site_sensitivity,
  results_path("discordance_imv_site_sensitivity.csv"),
  row_names = FALSE
)
record_discordance_status(
  "imv_site_sensitivity",
  ifelse(any(discordance_imv_site_sensitivity$component_status == "completed", na.rm = TRUE), "completed", "skipped"),
  ifelse(is.na(site_field), "IMV site sensitivity skipped because no feasible site identifier was found.", "IMV
   ↪  site-level sensitivity was generated."),
  "Results/discordance_imv_site_sensitivity.csv",
  optional = is.na(site_field)
)

imv_setting_gap_wide <- discordance_imv_setting_standardized |>
  dplyr::filter(.data$component_status == "completed") |>
  dplyr::select(setting_var, setting_level, co2_level, group, p, m_used) |>
  tidyr::pivot_wider(names_from = group, values_from = c(p, m_used))
if (!"p_ABG" %in% names(imv_setting_gap_wide)) imv_setting_gap_wide$p_ABG <- NA_real_
if (!"p_VBG" %in% names(imv_setting_gap_wide)) imv_setting_gap_wide$p_VBG <- NA_real_
if (!"m_used_ABG" %in% names(imv_setting_gap_wide)) imv_setting_gap_wide$m_used_ABG <- NA_integer_
if (!"m_used_VBG" %in% names(imv_setting_gap_wide)) imv_setting_gap_wide$m_used_VBG <- NA_integer_

  dplyr::mutate(
    abg_vbg_gap = .data$p_ABG - .data$p_VBG,




                                                         544
      abs_gap = abs(.data$abg_vbg_gap),

      m_used_min = ifelse(is.infinite(.data$m_used_min), NA_real_, .data$m_used_min)
  )

overall_imv_gap <- discordance_standardization_summary |>
   dplyr::filter(.data$outcome == "IMV") |>
   dplyr::summarise(max_abs_overall_gap = safe_max_abs_numeric(.data$gap_marginal_standardized)) |>
   dplyr::pull(.data$max_abs_overall_gap)
within_imv_gap <- safe_max_abs_numeric(imv_setting_gap_wide$abg_vbg_gap)

   dplyr::filter(.data$outcome == "IMV") |>
   dplyr::summarise(max_setting_rate_range = safe_max_numeric(.data$rate_range)) |>
   dplyr::pull(.data$max_setting_rate_range)
site_imv_signal <- if (any(discordance_imv_site_sensitivity$component_status == "completed", na.rm = TRUE)) {
   discordance_imv_site_sensitivity |>
     dplyr::group_by(.data$site_level, .data$outcome) |>
     dplyr::summarise(site_range = max(.data$weighted_event_rate, na.rm = TRUE) - min(.data$weighted_event_rate, na.rm
 ↪   = TRUE), .groups = "drop") |>
     dplyr::summarise(max_site_range = safe_max_numeric(.data$site_range)) |>
     dplyr::pull(.data$max_site_range)
} else {
   NA_real_
}

discordance_imv_heterogeneity_summary <- tibble::tibble(
  component = c("overall_marginal_standardized_gap", "within_setting_standardized_gap", "setting_rate_range",
   ↪   "site_sensitivity_range"),
  value = c(overall_imv_gap, within_imv_gap, setting_imv_rate_range, site_imv_signal),
  evidence_status = c(
    ifelse(is.finite(overall_imv_gap) & overall_imv_gap > 0.05, "residual_gap_present", "no_large_residual_gap"),
    ifelse(is.finite(within_imv_gap) & is.finite(overall_imv_gap) & within_imv_gap >= 0.75 * overall_imv_gap,
     ↪   "within_setting_persists", "within_setting_attenuated_or_unavailable"),
    ifelse(is.finite(setting_imv_rate_range) & setting_imv_rate_range > 0.10, "setting_heterogeneity_present",
     ↪   "setting_heterogeneity_not_large"),
    ifelse(is.finite(site_imv_signal) & site_imv_signal > 0.05, "site_signal_present",
     ↪   "site_signal_unavailable_or_not_large")



                                                           545
  ),
  interpretation = c(
    "Maximum absolute IMV ABG-VBG gap after common-source marginal standardization.",
    "Maximum absolute IMV ABG-VBG gap after restricting the standardization source to feasible settings.",
    "Maximum within-modality IMV weighted event-rate range across setting variables.",
    "Maximum site-level IMV ABG-VBG weighted event-rate range among feasible sites."
  )
) |>
  dplyr::mutate(
    overall_classification = dplyr::case_when(
      !is.finite(overall_imv_gap) ~ "unresolved_no_overall_gap_estimate",
      is.finite(within_imv_gap) & within_imv_gap >= 0.75 * overall_imv_gap ~
       ↪  "residual_imv_gap_persists_within_settings",
      is.finite(setting_imv_rate_range) & setting_imv_rate_range > 0.10 ~
       ↪  "setting_workflow_contributes_to_residual_imv_gap",
      is.finite(site_imv_signal) & site_imv_signal > 0.05 ~ "site_level_heterogeneity_may_contribute",
      TRUE ~ "residual_imv_gap_partly_attenuated_or_unresolved"
    )
  )
write_csv_safely(
  discordance_imv_heterogeneity_summary,
  results_path("discordance_imv_heterogeneity_summary.csv"),
  row_names = FALSE
)

## Timing sensitivity
timing_names <- names(subset_data_raw)
gas_time_candidates <- candidate_cols(
  timing_names,
  "(abg|vbg|blood_gas|gas).*(date|time|timestamp|datetime)",
  max_n = 20
)
proc_time_candidates <- candidate_cols(
  timing_names,
  "(imv|niv).*(date|time|timestamp|datetime)",
  max_n = 20




                                                         551
)

timing_field_map_rows <- list()
for (field in unique(c(gas_time_candidates, proc_time_candidates))) {
  x <- subset_data_raw[[field]]
  parsed_detail <- parse_discordance_time_detail(x, field = field, reference_date = encounter_date_reference)
  parsed <- parsed_detail$parsed
  timing_field_map_rows[[length(timing_field_map_rows) + 1L]] <- tibble::tibble(
    field = field,
    field_role = dplyr::case_when(
       field %in% gas_time_candidates ~ "gas_time",
       field %in% proc_time_candidates ~ "procedure_time",
       TRUE ~ "unknown"
    ),
    modality = dplyr::case_when(
       grepl("abg|arterial", field, ignore.case = TRUE) ~ "ABG",
       grepl("vbg|venous", field, ignore.case = TRUE) ~ "VBG",
       TRUE ~ ""
    ),
    outcome = dplyr::case_when(
       grepl("imv", field, ignore.case = TRUE) ~ "IMV",
       grepl("niv", field, ignore.case = TRUE) ~ "NIV",
       TRUE ~ ""
    ),
    class = paste(class(x), collapse = "/"),
    n_nonmissing = sum(!is.na(x)),
    n_parsed = sum(!is.na(parsed)),
    parse_fraction_among_nonmissing = ifelse(sum(!is.na(x)) > 0, sum(!is.na(parsed)) / sum(!is.na(x)), NA_real_),
    parse_method = parsed_detail$parse_method,
    parse_status = parsed_detail$parse_status
  )
}
discordance_timing_field_map <- if (length(timing_field_map_rows)) {
  dplyr::bind_rows(timing_field_map_rows)
} else {
  tibble::tibble(




                                                         552
    field = NA_character_,
    field_role = NA_character_,
    modality = NA_character_,
    outcome = NA_character_,
    class = NA_character_,
    n_nonmissing = 0L,
    n_parsed = 0L,
    parse_fraction_among_nonmissing = NA_real_,
    parse_method = "no_candidate_fields",
    parse_status = "skipped"
  )
}
write_csv_safely(
  discordance_timing_field_map,
  results_path("discordance_timing_field_map.csv"),
  row_names = FALSE
)

timing_pair_specs <- tidyr::crossing(
  group = discordance_groups,
  outcome_var = discordance_outcome_vars
) |>
  dplyr::mutate(
    outcome = unname(discordance_outcome_labels[outcome_var]),
    gas_time_field = dplyr::case_when(
       group == "ABG" ~ first_existing_col(
         c("abg_ph_date", "abg_hco3_date", "abg_co2_date", gas_time_candidates[grepl("abg|arterial",
          ↪  gas_time_candidates, ignore.case = TRUE)]),
         timing_names
       ),
       TRUE ~ first_existing_col(
         c("vbg_ph_date", "vbg_hco3_date", "vbg_co2_date", gas_time_candidates[grepl("vbg|venous", gas_time_candidates,
          ↪  ignore.case = TRUE)]),
         timing_names
       )
    ),




                                                          553
      procedure_time_field = dplyr::case_when(
         outcome_var == "imv_proc" ~ first_existing_col(
           c("imv_proc_first_date", "imv_first_date", proc_time_candidates[grepl("imv", proc_time_candidates, ignore.case
            ↪  = TRUE)]),
           timing_names
         ),
         TRUE ~ first_existing_col(
           c("niv_proc_first_date", "niv_first_date", proc_time_candidates[grepl("niv", proc_time_candidates, ignore.case
            ↪  = TRUE)]),
           timing_names
         )
      ),
      feasible_pair = !is.na(.data$gas_time_field) & !is.na(.data$procedure_time_field)
  )

timing_restricted_rows <- list()
if (any(timing_pair_specs$feasible_pair)) {
   for (imp_index in seq_len(imp_n)) {
     d_imp <- get_imp(imp_index)
     for (pair_idx in seq_len(nrow(timing_pair_specs))) {
       pair_i <- timing_pair_specs[pair_idx, ]
       if (!pair_i$feasible_pair) next
       gas_time <- parse_discordance_time(
         subset_data_raw[[pair_i$gas_time_field]],
         field = pair_i$gas_time_field,
         reference_date = encounter_date_reference
       )
       proc_time <- parse_discordance_time(
         subset_data_raw[[pair_i$procedure_time_field]],
         field = pair_i$procedure_time_field,
         reference_date = encounter_date_reference
       )
       date_only_pair <- !grepl("time|timestamp|datetime", paste(pair_i$gas_time_field, pair_i$procedure_time_field),
 ↪   ignore.case = TRUE)
       gas_precedes_proc <- if (date_only_pair) {
         !is.na(gas_time) & !is.na(proc_time) & as.Date(gas_time) <= as.Date(proc_time)




                                                            554
} else {
  !is.na(gas_time) & !is.na(proc_time) &
     as.numeric(difftime(proc_time, gas_time, units = "mins")) >= 30
}
treat_var <- if (identical(pair_i$group, "ABG")) "has_abg" else "has_vbg"
co2_var <- if (identical(pair_i$group, "ABG")) "paco2" else "vbg_co2"
low_cut <- if (identical(pair_i$group, "ABG")) ABG_CO2_LOW else VBG_CO2_LOW
high_cut <- if (identical(pair_i$group, "ABG")) ABG_CO2_HIGH else VBG_CO2_HIGH
weights_i <- get_mi_weight(pair_i$group, imp_index)
y <- to01(d_imp[[pair_i$outcome_var]])
tested_with_gas_time <- d_imp[[treat_var]] == 1 & !is.na(gas_time)
event_after_gas <- tested_with_gas_time & y == 1 & gas_precedes_proc
co2_category <- factor(
  make_co2_cat3(suppressWarnings(as.numeric(d_imp[[co2_var]])), low_cut, high_cut),
  levels = c("Low", "Normal", "High"),
  ordered = TRUE
)
timing_restricted_rows[[length(timing_restricted_rows) + 1L]] <- tibble::tibble(
  co2_level = as.character(co2_category),
  denominator = tested_with_gas_time,
  event_after_gas = event_after_gas,
  event_original = tested_with_gas_time & y == 1,
  w = weights_i
) |>
  dplyr::filter(.data$denominator, !is.na(.data$co2_level)) |>
  dplyr::group_by(.data$co2_level) |>
  dplyr::summarise(
     n_restricted = dplyr::n(),
     original_events = sum(.data$event_original, na.rm = TRUE),
     gas_precedes_events = sum(.data$event_after_gas, na.rm = TRUE),
     weighted_event_rate_original = weighted_mean_safe(.data$event_original, .data$w),
     weighted_event_rate_gas_precedes = weighted_mean_safe(.data$event_after_gas, .data$w),
     weighted_n = sum(.data$w, na.rm = TRUE),
     ess = weighted_ess(.data$w),
     .groups = "drop"
  ) |>




                                                    555
           dplyr::mutate(
             imp = imp_index,
             group = pair_i$group,
             outcome = pair_i$outcome,
             outcome_var = pair_i$outcome_var,
             gas_time_field = pair_i$gas_time_field,
             procedure_time_field = pair_i$procedure_time_field,
             timing_rule = ifelse(date_only_pair, "gas_date_on_or_before_procedure_date",
              ↪  "gas_time_at_least_30_minutes_before_procedure_time"),
             component_status = "completed",
             reason = "restricted_event_definition_uses_gas_precedes_procedure"
           )
        }
        rm(d_imp)
        invisible(gc(FALSE))
    }
}

if (length(timing_restricted_rows)) {
   discordance_timing_restricted_summary <- dplyr::bind_rows(timing_restricted_rows) |>
     dplyr::group_by(group, outcome, outcome_var, co2_level, gas_time_field, procedure_time_field, timing_rule,
 ↪   component_status, reason) |>
     dplyr::summarise(
       n_restricted = safe_median_numeric(.data$n_restricted),
       original_events = safe_median_numeric(.data$original_events),
       gas_precedes_events = safe_median_numeric(.data$gas_precedes_events),
       weighted_event_rate_original = safe_median_numeric(.data$weighted_event_rate_original),
       weighted_event_rate_gas_precedes = safe_median_numeric(.data$weighted_event_rate_gas_precedes),
       weighted_n = safe_median_numeric(.data$weighted_n),
       ess = safe_median_numeric(.data$ess),
       m_used = dplyr::n_distinct(.data$imp),
       .groups = "drop"
     )
   timing_status_value <- "completed"
   timing_status_reason <- "Timing-restricted event summaries were generated from feasible gas/procedure timestamp
 ↪   pairs."




                                                            556
} else {
  discordance_timing_restricted_summary <- tibble::tibble(
    group = timing_pair_specs$group,
    outcome = timing_pair_specs$outcome,
    outcome_var = timing_pair_specs$outcome_var,
    co2_level = NA_character_,
    gas_time_field = ifelse(is.na(timing_pair_specs$gas_time_field), "", timing_pair_specs$gas_time_field),
    procedure_time_field = ifelse(is.na(timing_pair_specs$procedure_time_field), "",
     ↪  timing_pair_specs$procedure_time_field),
    timing_rule = NA_character_,
    n_restricted = NA_real_,
    original_events = NA_real_,
    gas_precedes_events = NA_real_,
    weighted_event_rate_original = NA_real_,
    weighted_event_rate_gas_precedes = NA_real_,
    weighted_n = NA_real_,
    ess = NA_real_,
    m_used = NA_integer_,
    component_status = "skipped",
    reason = "No feasible parsed gas/procedure timestamp pair produced restricted rows."
  )
  timing_status_value <- "skipped"
  timing_status_reason <- "No feasible parsed gas/procedure timestamp pair produced restricted rows."
}

discordance_timing_status <- tibble::tibble(
  component = "timing_sensitivity",
  status = timing_status_value,
  gas_time_fields = paste(gas_time_candidates, collapse = "; "),
  procedure_time_fields = paste(proc_time_candidates, collapse = "; "),
  feasible_pairs = sum(timing_pair_specs$feasible_pair, na.rm = TRUE),
  reason = timing_status_reason
)
