## Summary of hypotheses and interpretation
standardization_supported <- any(
  is.finite(discordance_standardization_summary$gap_current_ref) &
    (
       abs(discordance_standardization_summary$gap_common_ref) <=
         0.75 * abs(discordance_standardization_summary$gap_current_ref) |
         abs(discordance_standardization_summary$gap_marginal_standardized) <=
           0.75 * abs(discordance_standardization_summary$gap_current_ref)
    ),
  na.rm = TRUE
)

scale_supported <- any(
  grepl("Relative odds are closer", discordance_scale_summary$comment, fixed = TRUE),




                                                          558
    na.rm = TRUE
)

capture_threshold_rows <- discordance_capture_summary_enhanced |>
  dplyr::filter(.data$threshold_flag %in% TRUE)
capture_evidence_families <- dplyr::n_distinct(capture_threshold_rows$proxy_family)
capture_event_conditional_signal <- any(
  capture_threshold_rows$proxy_family == "event_conditional_timestamp_completeness",
  na.rm = TRUE
)
legacy_capture_signal <- any(
  missingness_capture_summary$max_abs_abg_vbg_difference > 0.05,
  na.rm = TRUE
)
capture_supported <- capture_evidence_families >= 2L && capture_event_conditional_signal
capture_partially_supported <- !capture_supported &&
  (capture_evidence_families >= 1L || legacy_capture_signal)
capture_evidence_status <- dplyr::case_when(
  capture_supported ~ "supported",
  capture_partially_supported ~ "partially_supported",
  legacy_capture_signal ~ "partially_supported",
  TRUE ~ "not_supported"
)

setting_supported <- any(discordance_setting_rate_ranges$rate_range > 0.10, na.rm = TRUE) ||
  any(discordance_imv_heterogeneity_summary$evidence_status %in% c(
    "within_setting_persists",
    "setting_heterogeneity_present",
    "site_signal_present"
  ), na.rm = TRUE)

sentinel_selected_n <- sum(discordance_sentinel_procedure_selection_v2$selected %in% TRUE, na.rm = TRUE)
sentinel_inconclusive <- sentinel_selected_n < 2L
sentinel_v2_evidence <- discordance_sentinel_procedure_selection_v2 |>
  dplyr::filter(.data$selected) |>
  dplyr::left_join(




                                                         559
     discordance_sentinel_procedure_summary_v2 |>
        dplyr::select(
          sentinel_concept, binary_field, date_field, weighted_abs_diff,
          date_missing_abs_diff, m_used, interpretation
        ),
     by = c("sentinel_concept", "binary_field", "date_field")
   ) |>
   dplyr::mutate(
     large_weighted_diff = is.finite(.data$weighted_abs_diff) & abs(.data$weighted_abs_diff) > 0.05,
     large_date_diff = is.finite(.data$date_missing_abs_diff) & .data$date_missing_abs_diff > 0.05,
     large_difference = .data$large_weighted_diff | .data$large_date_diff,
     lower_specificity = .data$physiologic_specificity %in% c("low", "medium"),
     direction = dplyr::case_when(
        is.finite(.data$weighted_abs_diff) & .data$weighted_abs_diff > 0 ~ "ABG_higher",
        is.finite(.data$weighted_abs_diff) & .data$weighted_abs_diff < 0 ~ "VBG_higher",
        TRUE ~ "no_clear_direction"
     )
   )
sentinel_large_lower_specificity <- sentinel_v2_evidence |>
   dplyr::filter(.data$large_difference, .data$lower_specificity)
sentinel_supported <- !sentinel_inconclusive &&
   nrow(sentinel_large_lower_specificity) >= 2L &&
   dplyr::n_distinct(sentinel_large_lower_specificity$direction[sentinel_large_lower_specificity$direction !=
 ↪   "no_clear_direction"]) <= 1L
sentinel_partially_supported <- !sentinel_supported &&
   !sentinel_inconclusive &&
   any(sentinel_v2_evidence$large_difference, na.rm = TRUE)
sentinel_evidence_status <- dplyr::case_when(
   sentinel_supported ~ "supported",
   sentinel_partially_supported ~ "partially_supported",
   sentinel_inconclusive ~ "inconclusive",
   TRUE ~ "not_supported"
)

tail_supported <- any(discordance_tail_support_summary$support_flag %in% TRUE, na.rm = TRUE)




                                                          560
dual_inconclusive <- any(
  dplyr::bind_rows(discordance_status_rows) |>
    dplyr::filter(.data$component == "dual_tested_sensitivity") |>
    dplyr::pull(status) == "skipped",
  na.rm = TRUE
)

timing_inconclusive <- any(
  dplyr::bind_rows(discordance_status_rows) |>
    dplyr::filter(.data$component == "timing_sensitivity") |>
    dplyr::pull(status) == "skipped",
  na.rm = TRUE
)

timing_supported <- any(
  is.finite(discordance_timing_restricted_summary$weighted_event_rate_original) &
    is.finite(discordance_timing_restricted_summary$weighted_event_rate_gas_precedes) &
    abs(discordance_timing_restricted_summary$weighted_event_rate_original -
          discordance_timing_restricted_summary$weighted_event_rate_gas_precedes) > 0.05,
  na.rm = TRUE
)
timing_evidence_status <- dplyr::case_when(
  timing_inconclusive ~ "inconclusive",
  timing_supported ~ "partially_supported",
  TRUE ~ "not_supported"
)

discordance_write_md(
  c(
    "# Discordance Interpretation Rules",
    "",
    "These rules intentionally separate broad workflow/completeness signals from stronger evidence for
     ↪  modality-specific procedure-capture bias.",
    "",
    "- Reference-profile / standardization is supported when common-reference or common-source marginal
     ↪  standardization shrinks at least one current probability gap by at least 25%.",




                                                         561
      "- Setting/workflow heterogeneity is supported when within-modality setting ranges exceed 10 percentage points or
       ↪  IMV-focused within-setting/site diagnostics show persistent heterogeneity.",
      "- Differential missingness or procedure capture is supported only when at least two enhanced proxy families cross
       ↪  the 5-point threshold and event-conditional timestamp completeness also points to a difference; otherwise any
       ↪  weaker signal is partial.",
      "- Sentinel procedure capture/completeness is supported only when at least two selected low/medium-specificity
       ↪  sentinels show large differences in the same direction; workflow-dependent sentinels are partial evidence.",
      "- Timing is inconclusive unless feasible gas/procedure pairs can be parsed; timing-restricted differences above 5
       ↪  points are treated as partial evidence, not proof.",
      "- Tail support is supported when the existing ESS/event-count support flag is triggered.",
      "- Intrinsic modality-specific measurement is not supported by default when dual-tested summaries are available
       ↪  for review."
    ),
    "discordance_interpretation_rules.md"
)

discordance_interpretation_summary <- tibble::tibble(
  hypothesis = c(
    "Reference-profile / standardization effect",
    "Setting or workflow heterogeneity",
    "Differential missingness or procedure capture",
    "Sentinel procedure capture/completeness",
    "Scale / noncollapsibility effect",
    "Same-encounter timing structure",
    "Tail support / positivity",
    "Intrinsic modality-specific measurement effect"
  ),
  evidence_status = c(
    ifelse(standardization_supported, "supported", "not_supported"),
    ifelse(setting_supported, "supported", "not_supported"),
    capture_evidence_status,
    sentinel_evidence_status,
    ifelse(scale_supported, "supported", "not_supported"),
    timing_evidence_status,
    ifelse(tail_supported, "supported", "not_supported"),
    ifelse(dual_inconclusive, "inconclusive", "not_supported")




                                                           562
  ),
  key_evidence = c(
    ifelse(standardization_supported, "Common or marginal standardization shrank at least one current probability gap
     ↪   by >=25%.", "Standardization did not shrink probability gaps by >=25%."),
    ifelse(setting_supported, "Setting-rate ranges or IMV-focused setting/site diagnostics show material
     ↪   heterogeneity.", "Within-modality setting-specific weighted event-rate ranges were <=10 percentage points and
     ↪   IMV follow-up did not show a large setting/site signal."),
    dplyr::case_when(
       capture_supported ~ "Multiple enhanced proxy families plus event-conditional timestamp completeness point to
↪   capture/completeness differences.",
       capture_partially_supported ~ "At least one broad capture/completeness proxy differs, but evidence is not
↪   specific enough to prove procedure-capture bias.",
       TRUE ~ "Enhanced capture/completeness proxies did not show large usable ABG-VBG differences."
    ),
    dplyr::case_when(
       sentinel_inconclusive ~ "Fewer than two suitable v2 sentinel procedure concepts were selected.",
       sentinel_supported ~ "At least two selected low/medium-specificity sentinels showed large same-direction
↪   capture/completeness differences.",
       sentinel_partially_supported ~ "Selected sentinels show some capture/completeness differences, but specificity
↪   or directional consistency is insufficient.",
       TRUE ~ "Selected v2 sentinels did not show large capture/completeness differences."
    ),
    ifelse(scale_supported, "At least one contrast had closer ABG-VBG agreement on OR scale than risk-difference
     ↪   scale.", "OR-scale agreement was not consistently closer than probability-scale agreement."),
    dplyr::case_when(
       timing_inconclusive ~ "Timestamp fields were unavailable, ambiguous, or could not support a restricted subset.",
       timing_supported ~ "Gas-precedes-procedure restricted event rates differed from original event rates by >5
↪   points.",
       TRUE ~ "Timing-restricted summaries were feasible but did not show a large difference."
    ),
    ifelse(tail_supported, "At least one clinical/quantile bin had ESS <100 or weighted events <10.", "Tail bins did
     ↪   not trigger the ESS/event-count support flag."),
    ifelse(dual_inconclusive, "Dual-tested subset was unavailable in this render subset.", "Dual-tested subset event
     ↪   rates were generated for direct review.")
  ),
  recommended_next_step = c(




                                                         563
   "If supported, consider whether manuscript probability curves should use common or marginal standardization in a
    ↪  future methodological ticket.",
   "If supported, consider setting-stratified or setting-interaction sensitivity models.",
   "If supported, audit NIV/IMV source-field construction and coding-density definitions before changing models.",
   "If supported, inspect selected sentinel source fields and date-field definitions before attributing NIV/IMV gaps
    ↪  to physiology.",
   "Use risk differences/RRs beside ORs when communicating procedure outcomes.",
   "If timestamps become available, restrict to blood gases clearly preceding NIV/IMV.",
   "If supported, avoid overinterpreting tail probability gaps and consider trimming/support annotations.",
   "Compare dual-tested event-rate patterns against primary ABG/VBG gaps before attributing discordance to modality."
  )
) |>
  dplyr::mutate(
    supported = .data$evidence_status == "supported",
    not_supported = .data$evidence_status == "not_supported",
    inconclusive = .data$evidence_status == "inconclusive"
  ) |>
  dplyr::select(
    hypothesis, evidence_status, supported, not_supported, inconclusive,
    key_evidence, recommended_next_step
  )
write_csv_safely(
  discordance_interpretation_summary,
  results_path("discordance_interpretation_summary.csv"),
  row_names = FALSE
)

metadata_audit_rows <- list()
metadata_audit_row <- function(component, artifact, check, observed, expected, status, detail) {
  metadata_audit_rows[[length(metadata_audit_rows) + 1L]] <<- tibble::tibble(
    component = component,
    artifact = artifact,
    check = check,
    observed = as.character(observed),
    expected = as.character(expected),
    status = status,
    detail = detail
  )
  invisible(TRUE)
}

discordance_cap_values <- unique(discordance_standardization_summary$standardization_sample_cap)

  "standardization_metadata",
  "discordance_standardization_summary.csv",
  "sample_cap_matches_common_source_policy",
  paste(discordance_cap_values, collapse = "; "),
  standardization_sample_cap,
  ifelse(length(discordance_cap_values) == 1L && identical(as.integer(discordance_cap_values[[1L]]),
   ↪  as.integer(standardization_sample_cap)), "passed", "failed"),
  "Discordance marginal-standardization cap should match the manuscript common-source cap for this run mode."
)

    TRUE ~ "csv"
  ),
  exists = vapply(
    artifact_path,
    function(path) {
       if (identical(path, "discordance_artifact_manifest.csv")) return(TRUE)
       file.exists(results_path(path))

    logical(1L)
  ),

missing_files <- expected_diag[!file.exists(results_path(expected_diag))]
stopifnot(length(missing_files) == 0)

# Only a subset of diagnostics tables are guaranteed to be rewritten with the
# current run metadata on every render. Many analysis CSVs are checked here for
# existence, but their contents may be intentionally preserved across reruns or
# written by helpers that do not stamp the current run_id into the first row.
# Restrict freshness checks to the end-of-run diagnostics that are explicitly
# regenerated in this session.
run_id_check_files <- c(
  "runtime_log.csv", "runtime_summary.csv", "runtime_summary_top15.csv",
  "warnings_log.csv", "mi_warnings_log.csv", "mi_info_log.csv",
  "diagnostics_summary.csv", "diagnostics_missingness.csv",
  "diagnostics_missingness-by-strata.csv", "plot_drop_log.csv"
)

run_id_mismatch <- character()




                                                         577
for (f in run_id_check_files) {
  path <- results_path(f)
  if (grepl("\\.csv$", f)) {
    df <- tryCatch(read.csv(path, nrows = 1), error = function(e) NULL)
    stopifnot(!is.null(df))
    stopifnot("run_id" %in% names(df))
    if (nrow(df) > 0 && !identical(as.character(df$run_id[1]), diag_run_id)) {
      run_id_mismatch <- c(run_id_mismatch, f)
    }
  }
}

if (length(missing_files) || length(run_id_mismatch)) {
  msg <- paste0(
    "Diagnostics completeness check failed: missing files [",
    paste(missing_files, collapse = ", "),
    "]; run_id mismatch [",
    paste(run_id_mismatch, collapse = ", "),
    "]."
  )
  stop(msg)
}

# Purpose: diagnostics audit run.
audit_script <- here::here("R", "diagnostics_audit.R")
audit_md <- results_path("diagnostics_audit.md")
audit_summary <- results_path("diagnostics_audit_summary.csv")
audit_issues <- results_path("diagnostics_audit_issues.csv")
stopifnot(file.exists(audit_script))
old_diag_results_dir <- Sys.getenv("DIAG_RESULTS_DIR", unset = "")
on.exit(Sys.setenv(DIAG_RESULTS_DIR = old_diag_results_dir), add = TRUE)
Sys.setenv(DIAG_RESULTS_DIR = results_dir)
audit_env <- new.env(parent = globalenv())
audit_result <- tryCatch(



                                                         578
  {
    sys.source(audit_script, envir = audit_env)
    TRUE
  },
  error = function(e) e
)
if (inherits(audit_result, "error")) {
  stop("diagnostics_audit.R failed: ", conditionMessage(audit_result), call. = FALSE)
}

read_required_audit_csv <- function(path, required_cols, label) {
  if (!file.exists(path)) {
    stop(label, " missing after diagnostics audit: ", path, call. = FALSE)
  }
  df <- tryCatch(
    utils::read.csv(path, stringsAsFactors = FALSE),
    error = function(e) stop(label, " could not be read: ", conditionMessage(e), call. = FALSE)
  )
  missing_cols <- setdiff(required_cols, names(df))
  if (length(missing_cols)) {
    stop(
      label, " missing required columns [",
      paste(missing_cols, collapse = ", "),
      "]: ", path,
      call. = FALSE
    )
  }
  df
}

diagnostics_audit_summary_df <- read_required_audit_csv(
  audit_summary,
  required_cols = c("component", "metric", "value", "status", "severity", "evidence_file", "note", "run_id",
   ↪  "run_ts"),
  label = "diagnostics_audit_summary.csv"
)

   ↪  "run_id", "run_ts"),

)

# Purpose: mi save exports.
stopifnot(
  exists("abg_curves"), exists("vbg_curves"),
  exists("abg_prob_curves"), exists("vbg_prob_curves"),
  exists("abg_coefs"), exists("vbg_coefs")
)
saveRDS(
  list(
    abg_curves = abg_curves,
    vbg_curves = vbg_curves,
    abg_prob_curves = abg_prob_curves,
    vbg_prob_curves = vbg_prob_curves,
    abg_coefs = abg_coefs,
    vbg_coefs = vbg_coefs
  ),
  mi_pooled_file
)

# Purpose: mi session.
session_lines <- capture.output(sessionInfo())
writeLines(session_lines, results_path("sessionInfo.txt"))
writeLines(session_lines, results_path("session_info.txt"))
renv_status_lines <- if ("renv" %in% rownames(installed.packages())) {
  tryCatch(capture.output(renv::status()), error = function(e) c("renv::status() failed:", conditionMessage(e)))
} else {
  "renv package is not installed in this environment."
}
writeLines(renv_status_lines, results_path("renv_status.txt"))

# Purpose: software statement.
cat("Software: R ", as.character(getRversion()),
    "; key packages: mice, WeightIt, cobalt, survey, rms.\n")

Software: R 4.5.3 ; key packages: mice, WeightIt, cobalt, survey, rms.

# Purpose: record that render-path validation is deferred to wrapper postflight,
# which is the first point where the current render's TeX actually exists.
scan_out <- results_path("render_path_hygiene_scan.csv")

scan_df <- data.frame(
  scan_status = "deferred_to_wrapper",
  line = "",
  run_id = diag_run_id,
  run_ts = diag_run_ts,
  stringsAsFactors = FALSE
)
write_csv_safely(scan_df, scan_out, row_names = FALSE)

# Purpose: record that PDF hygiene validation is deferred to wrapper postflight,
# which is the first point where the current render's PDF actually exists.
scan_out <- results_path("pdf_hygiene_scan.csv")
scan_df <- data.frame(
  scan_status = "deferred_to_wrapper",
  scanner = "wrapper_postflight",
  line = "",
  run_id = diag_run_id,
  run_ts = diag_run_ts,
  stringsAsFactors = FALSE
)
write_csv_safely(scan_df, scan_out, row_names = FALSE)

# Purpose: numbering hygiene scan.
qmd_file <- resolve_current_qmd()
src_lines <- readLines(qmd_file, warn = FALSE)
pattern_manual <- "(^#+\\s+[0-9]+(\\.[0-9]+)*\\s+[0-9]+\\))|(Table\\s+[0-9]+:\\s+Table\\s+[0-9]+)"
hits <- which(grepl(pattern_manual, src_lines))
scan_df <- data.frame(
  line_no = hits,
  line = src_lines[hits],
  stringsAsFactors = FALSE
)
write_csv_safely(scan_df, results_path("numbering_hygiene_scan.csv"), row_names = FALSE)

# Purpose: remove transient MI scratch artifacts after a successful render.
cleanup_mi_transient_outputs()
